// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  STORAGE KEYS & HELPERS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const STORE_KEY    = "rentkeeper-v1";
const BASELINE_KEY = "rentkeeper-baseline-v1";

async function loadData() {
  try { const r = await storage.get(STORE_KEY); return JSON.parse(r.value); } catch { return null; }
}
async function saveData(d) {
  try { await storage.set(STORE_KEY, JSON.stringify(d)); } catch {}
}
async function loadBaseline() {
  try { const r = await storage.get(BASELINE_KEY); return JSON.parse(r.value); } catch { return null; }
}
async function saveBaseline(d) {
  try { await storage.set(BASELINE_KEY, JSON.stringify(d)); } catch {}
}

const fmt       = (n) => `NT$ ${Number(n || 0).toLocaleString()}`;
const uid       = () => Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 9);
const nowISO    = () => new Date().toISOString();
const todayStr  = () => new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
const addOneYear = (s) => { if (!s) return ""; const d = new Date(s); d.setFullYear(d.getFullYear()+1); return d.toISOString().slice(0,10); };
const daysUntil = (d) => Math.ceil((new Date(d) - new Date()) / 86400000);
const toROC = (s, t=false) => {
  if (!s) return "—";
  const d = new Date(s); if (isNaN(d)) return s;
  const y = d.getFullYear()-1911, mo = String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,"0"), dy = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,"0");
  if (t) { const h=String(d.getHours()).padStart(2,"0"), m=String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2,"0"); return `民國${y}年${mo}月${dy}日 ${h}:${m}`; }
  return `民國${y}年${mo}月${dy}日`;
};
const toROCMonth = (s) => { if (!s) return "—"; const p=s.split("-"); return p.length>=2?`民國${parseInt(p[0])-1911}年${p[1]}月`:s; };
const SL = { rented:"已出租", vacant:"空房", pending:"待處理", in_progress:"處理中", done:"已完成", paid:"已繳", unpaid:"未繳", rent:"租金", electric:"電費" };
const csvEsc = (s) => { const str=String(s??""); return /[,"\n\r]/.test(str)?`"${str.replace(/"/g,'""')}"`:str; };
const downloadCSV = (filename, content) => {
  const url=URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([content],{type:"text/csv;charset=utf-8;"}));
  const a=document.createElement("a"); a.href=url; a.download=filename;
  document.body.appendChild(a); a.click(); document.body.removeChild(a); URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
};

// 開啟 LINE 分享對象選單（一律以「新分頁」開啟，不覆蓋原頁面）
// 必須在同步的 click handler 中第一個呼叫，否則行動瀏覽器會擋 popup
// 同時把文字複製到剪貼簿作為保險，即使開啟失敗也能手動貼上
const openLineShare = (text) => {
  try {
    if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).catch(() => {});
    } else {
      const ta = document.createElement("textarea");
      ta.value = text; ta.style.position = "fixed"; ta.style.opacity = "0";
      document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select();
      try { document.execCommand("copy"); } catch {}
      document.body.removeChild(ta);
    }
  } catch {}

  const encoded = encodeURIComponent(text);
  const url = `https://line.me/R/msg/text/?${encoded}`;
  let opened = false;

  // 優先：window.open 新分頁
  try {
    const w = window.open(url, "_blank", "noopener,noreferrer");
    opened = !!(w && !w.closed);
  } catch {}

  // 備援：模擬超連結點擊（target=_blank），不會覆蓋當前頁面
  if (!opened) {
    try {
      const a = document.createElement("a");
      a.href = url; a.target = "_blank"; a.rel = "noopener noreferrer";
      a.style.display = "none";
      document.body.appendChild(a);
      a.click();
      document.body.removeChild(a);
      opened = true;
    } catch {}
  }

  if (!opened) {
    alert("無法自動開啟 LINE（可能為預覽環境或瀏覽器限制）。\n催繳文字已複製到剪貼簿，請手動開啟 LINE 後貼上傳送。");
  } else {
    try {
      const toast = document.createElement("div");
      toast.textContent = "✓ 已於新分頁開啟 LINE，文字已複製到剪貼簿";
      toast.style.cssText = "position:fixed;bottom:24px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);background:#059669;color:#fff;padding:10px 18px;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;z-index:99999;box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,.2)";
      document.body.appendChild(toast);
      setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 2500);
    } catch {}
  }
  return opened;
};

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  SECURITY — SHA-256, PASSWORD MIGRATION, LOCKOUT
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function sha256(str) {
  const buf = await crypto.subtle.digest("SHA-256", new TextEncoder().encode(str));
  return Array.from(new Uint8Array(buf)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, "0")).join("");
}
const isHashed = (s) => typeof s === "string" && /^[0-9a-f]{64}$/.test(s);
async function migratePasswords(data) {
  if (!data?.users) return data;
  const needsMigration = data.users.some(u => u.password && !isHashed(u.password));
  if (!needsMigration) return data;
  const users = await Promise.all(data.users.map(async u => ({
    ...u, password: isHashed(u.password) ? u.password : await sha256(u.password || "")
  })));
  return { ...data, users };
}

const LOCKOUT_KEY      = "rentkeeper-lockout-v1";
const MAX_ATTEMPTS     = 5;
const LOCKOUT_DURATION = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 分鐘
function getLockout(id) {
  try { const d = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LOCKOUT_KEY) || "{}"); return d[id] || { attempts:0, lockedUntil:null }; }
  catch { return { attempts:0, lockedUntil:null }; }
}
function setLockoutData(id, info) {
  try { const d = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LOCKOUT_KEY) || "{}"); d[id]=info; localStorage.setItem(LOCKOUT_KEY, JSON.stringify(d)); }
  catch {}
}
function clearLockout(id) {
  try { const d = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LOCKOUT_KEY) || "{}"); delete d[id]; localStorage.setItem(LOCKOUT_KEY, JSON.stringify(d)); }
  catch {}
}
function checkLocked(id) {
  const lock = getLockout(id);
  if (lock.lockedUntil && Date.now() < lock.lockedUntil) {
    const remaining = Math.ceil((lock.lockedUntil - Date.now()) / 60000);
    return `登入失敗次數過多，請 ${remaining} 分鐘後再試`;
  }
  return null;
}
function recordFailure(id) {
  const lock = getLockout(id);
  const attempts = (lock.attempts || 0) + 1;
  const lockedUntil = attempts >= MAX_ATTEMPTS ? Date.now() + LOCKOUT_DURATION : null;
  setLockoutData(id, { attempts, lockedUntil });
  return attempts;
}

  return icons[n] || null;
};

// J.R.M 公司 Logo（家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司）
const JRMLogo = ({ s=56 }) => (
  <img src="./jrm-logo.jpg" alt="J.R.M 家樂美房產管理顧問" width={s} height={s} style={{ display:"block", objectFit:"contain", borderRadius:6 }}/>
);

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  UI PRIMITIVES
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function Modal({ title, onClose, children, width=480 }) {
  return (
    <div style={{ position:"fixed", inset:0, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.35)", zIndex:1000, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:16, backdropFilter:"blur(4px)" }}>
      <div style={{ background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:16, width:"100%", maxWidth:width, maxHeight:"90vh", overflow:"auto", boxShadow:"0 24px 48px rgba(0,0,0,0.14)" }}>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", padding:"16px 20px 14px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, position:"sticky", top:0, background:T.bg, zIndex:1 }}>
          <span style={{ fontWeight:700, fontSize:15, color:T.text }}>{title}</span>
          <button onClick={onClose} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", color:T.textSub, padding:4, borderRadius:6, display:"flex" }}><Icon n="x"/></button>
        </div>
        <div style={{ padding:20 }}>{children}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function Toast({ msg, type }) {
  const bg = type==="error"?T.red : type==="chat"?T.text : T.green;
  return <div style={{ position:"fixed", bottom:90, left:"50%", transform:"translateX(-50%)", background:bg, color:"#fff", padding:"10px 20px", borderRadius:10, fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, zIndex:9999, boxShadow:"0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.22)", whiteSpace:"nowrap", maxWidth:"90vw", overflow:"hidden", textOverflow:"ellipsis" }}>{msg}</div>;
}

function AvatarBadge({ user, size=34 }) {
  const r = safeRole(user.role);
  return (
    <div style={{ position:"relative", display:"inline-flex" }}>
      <div style={{ width:size, height:size, borderRadius:"50%", background:r.color+"22", border:`1.5px solid ${r.color}55`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:size*0.38, fontWeight:700, color:r.color }}>{user.avatar||(user.name||"?")[0]}</div>
      <div style={{ position:"absolute", bottom:-1, right:-1, width:10, height:10, borderRadius:"50%", background:user.online?T.green:T.borderMd, border:`2px solid ${T.bg}` }}/>
    </div>
  );
}

function ROCDateInput({ value, onChange }) {
  const parts = value ? value.split("-") : ["","",""];
  const rocYear = parts[0] ? String(parseInt(parts[0])-1911) : "";
  const month   = parts[1]||"";
  const day     = parts[2]||"";
  const sel = (filled) => ({ flex:1, background:filled?"#fff":"#f3f4f6", border:`1px solid ${T.borderMd}`, borderRadius:8, color:T.text, padding:"10px 4px", fontSize:14, outline:"none", cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" });
  const emit = (y,m,d) => { if(y&&m&&d) onChange({ target:{ value:`${parseInt(y)+1911}-${m}-${d}` } }); };
  return (
    <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:4, marginBottom:12 }}>
      <select value={rocYear} onChange={e=>emit(e.target.value,month,day)} style={sel(!!rocYear)}>
        <option value="">民國年</option>
        {Array.from({length:36},(_,i)=>95+i).map(y=><option key={y} value={y}>民國 {y} 年</option>)}
      </select>
      <select value={month} onChange={e=>emit(rocYear,e.target.value,day)} style={sel(!!month)}>
        <option value="">月</option>
        {Array.from({length:12},(_,i)=>String(i+1).padStart(2,"0")).map(m=><option key={m} value={m}>{parseInt(m)} 月</option>)}
      </select>
      <select value={day} onChange={e=>emit(rocYear,month,e.target.value)} style={sel(!!day)}>
        <option value="">日</option>
        {Array.from({length:31},(_,i)=>String(i+1).padStart(2,"0")).map(d=><option key={d} value={d}>{parseInt(d)} 日</option>)}
      </select>
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  CREDENTIAL STORE — 每個身份類型各存一份「記住我」憑證
//  格式：{ tenant: { phone, rememberMe }, admin: { email, pw, rememberMe }, superadmin: { email, pw, rememberMe } }
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const CRED_KEY     = "rentkeeper-credentials-v1";
const ACCOUNTS_KEY = "rentkeeper-quick-accounts-v1";

function loadCreds() {
  try { const v = localStorage.getItem(CRED_KEY); return v ? JSON.parse(v) : {}; } catch { return {}; }
}
function saveCreds(obj) {
  try { localStorage.setItem(CRED_KEY, JSON.stringify(obj)); } catch {}
}
function loadAccounts() {
  try { const v = localStorage.getItem(ACCOUNTS_KEY); return v ? JSON.parse(v) : []; } catch { return []; }
}
function persistAccount(entry) {
  const prev = loadAccounts();
  const uk = entry.email || entry.phone;
  const next = [entry, ...prev.filter(a => (a.email || a.phone) !== uk)].slice(0, 6);
  try { localStorage.setItem(ACCOUNTS_KEY, JSON.stringify(next)); } catch {}
}
function dropAccount(uk) {
  try { localStorage.setItem(ACCOUNTS_KEY, JSON.stringify(loadAccounts().filter(a => (a.email || a.phone) !== uk))); } catch {}
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  LOGIN
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function LoginScreen({ users, tenants, onLogin }) {
  const rolesMeta = [
    { key:"tenant",     label:"租客",     icon:"person", color:"#6b7280", bg:"#f3f4f6" },
    { key:"admin",      label:"管理員",   icon:"shield", color:"#2563eb", bg:"#eff6ff" },
    { key:"superadmin", label:"後台管理員", icon:"build",  color:"#dc2626", bg:"#fef2f2" },
    { key:"finance",    label:"財務/行政",icon:"dollar", color:"#7c3aed", bg:"#faf5ff" },
  ];
  const roleLabel = { tenant:"租客", admin:"管理員", superadmin:"後台管理員", finance:"財務/行政" };
  const roleColor = { tenant:"#6b7280", admin:"#2563eb", superadmin:"#dc2626", finance:"#7c3aed" };

  // ── 初始化：從 localStorage 載入上次的記住我憑證 ────────
  const initCreds = loadCreds();
  const [sel, setSel]         = useState(null);
  const [phone, setPhone]     = useState("");
  const [email, setEmail]     = useState("");
  const [pw, setPw]           = useState("");
  // 每個 tab 各自的記住我勾選狀態
  const [rememberMe, setRememberMe] = useState({
    tenant:     initCreds.tenant?.rememberMe     || false,
    admin:      initCreds.admin?.rememberMe      || false,
    superadmin: initCreds.superadmin?.rememberMe || false,
    finance:    initCreds.finance?.rememberMe    || false,
  });
  const [err, setErr]         = useState("");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [accounts, setAccounts]     = useState(() => loadAccounts());
  const [showAccounts, setShowAccounts] = useState(true);
  const [confirmRemove, setConfirmRemove] = useState(null);
  // 記住我已帶入標記（顯示小綠勾）
  const [autoFilled, setAutoFilled] = useState(false);

  // ── 切換身份時自動帶入「記住我」的已儲存憑證 ────────
  const switchRole = (roleKey) => {
    setSel(roleKey);
    setErr(""); setAutoFilled(false);
    const cred = loadCreds()[roleKey];
    if (cred?.rememberMe) {
      if (roleKey === "tenant") {
        setPhone(cred.phone || ""); setEmail(""); setPw("");
        setAutoFilled(true);
      } else {
        // 不在輸入框顯示密碼 hash，僅帶入帳號
        setEmail(cred.email || ""); setPw(""); setPhone("");
        setAutoFilled(false);
      }
    } else {
      setPhone(""); setEmail(""); setPw("");
    }
    setShowAccounts(false);
  };

  // ── 更新「記住我」勾選 ──────────────────────────────
  const toggleRemember = () => {
    if (!sel) return;
    const next = !rememberMe[sel];
    setRememberMe(r => ({ ...r, [sel]: next }));
    // 若取消勾選，立即清除該身份的已儲存憑證
    if (!next) {
      const creds = loadCreds();
      delete creds[sel];
      saveCreds(creds);
    }
  };

  const canSubmit = sel === "tenant"
    ? phone.trim().length >= 8
    : (email.trim().length > 0 && pw.trim().length > 0);

  // ── 執行登入 ─────────────────────────────────────────
  const doLogin = async (overrides = {}) => {
    const fSel   = overrides.sel   ?? sel;
    const fEmail = overrides.email ?? email;
    const fPw    = overrides.pw    ?? pw;
    const fPhone = overrides.phone ?? phone;
    setLoading(true);

    // 鎖定檢查
    const identifier = fSel === "tenant" ? fPhone.replace(/[-\s]/g,"") : fEmail;
    const lockMsg = checkLocked(identifier);
    if (lockMsg) { setErr(lockMsg); setLoading(false); return; }

    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 480));
    if (fSel === "tenant") {
      const ni = fPhone.replace(/[-\s]/g, "");
      const t  = (tenants||[]).find(t => (t.phone||"").replace(/[-\s]/g,"") === ni);
      if (!t) { recordFailure(ni); setErr("找不到此手機號碼的租客"); setLoading(false); return; }
      // 儲存記住我憑證
      const creds = loadCreds();
      const curRemember = overrides.remember ?? rememberMe.tenant;
      if (curRemember) { creds.tenant = { phone: t.phone, rememberMe: true }; saveCreds(creds); }
      else { delete creds.tenant; saveCreds(creds); }
      clearLockout(ni);
      // 儲存快速帳號
      persistAccount({ type:"tenant", name:t.name, phone:t.phone, role:"viewer", avatar:(t.name||"租")[0], color:"#6b7280", lastLogin:new Date().toISOString() });
      setAccounts(loadAccounts());
      onLogin({ id:t.id, name:t.name, email:t.email||"", role:"viewer", avatar:(t.name||"租")[0], online:true, _tenantId:t.id, _roomId:t.roomId });
    } else {
      // 密碼雜湊：prehashed → 直接用 pwHash；有 pw → 計算 sha256；否則計算輸入的 fPw
      const pwHash = overrides.prehashed
        ? overrides.pwHash
        : await sha256(overrides.pw ?? fPw);
      const u = (users||[]).find(u => u.email===fEmail && u.password===pwHash && u.role===fSel);
      if (u) {
        clearLockout(fEmail);
        const creds = loadCreds();
        const curRemember = overrides.remember ?? rememberMe[fSel];
        // 儲存 hash 而非明文
        if (curRemember) { creds[fSel] = { email:u.email, pwHash, rememberMe:true }; saveCreds(creds); }
        else { delete creds[fSel]; saveCreds(creds); }
        persistAccount({ type:fSel, name:u.name, email:u.email, role:u.role, avatar:u.avatar||u.name[0], color:safeRole(u.role).color, lastLogin:new Date().toISOString() });
        setAccounts(loadAccounts());
        onLogin(u);
      } else {
        const attempts = recordFailure(fEmail);
        const remaining = MAX_ATTEMPTS - attempts;
        if (remaining <= 0) {
          setErr(`帳號或密碼錯誤，帳號已鎖定 15 分鐘`);
        } else {
          setErr(`帳號或密碼錯誤（還可嘗試 ${remaining} 次）`);
        }
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }
  };

  // ── 點擊快速帳號卡片 ─────────────────────────────────
  const handleQuickSelect = (acct) => {
    setErr("");
    const cred = loadCreds()[acct.type];
    if (acct.type === "tenant") {
      // tenant：若有記住我直接登入，否則帶入 phone 進表單
      if (cred?.rememberMe && cred.phone) {
        setSel("tenant"); setPhone(cred.phone); setEmail(""); setPw("");
        setRememberMe(r => ({ ...r, tenant: true }));
        setShowAccounts(false); setAutoFilled(true);
        doLogin({ sel:"tenant", phone:cred.phone, remember:true });
      } else {
        setSel("tenant"); setPhone(acct.phone||""); setEmail(""); setPw("");
        setAutoFilled(false); setShowAccounts(false);
        setTimeout(() => { document.getElementById("rk-phone-input")?.focus(); }, 80);
      }
    } else {
      // admin / superadmin：若有記住我直接登入，否則帶入 email 進表單
      if (cred?.rememberMe && cred.email && (cred.pwHash || cred.pw)) {
        setSel(acct.type); setEmail(cred.email); setPw(""); setPhone("");
        setRememberMe(r => ({ ...r, [acct.type]: true }));
        setShowAccounts(false); setAutoFilled(true);
        if (cred.pwHash) {
          doLogin({ sel:acct.type, email:cred.email, pwHash:cred.pwHash, prehashed:true, remember:true });
        } else {
          doLogin({ sel:acct.type, email:cred.email, pw:cred.pw, remember:true });
        }
      } else {
        setSel(acct.type); setEmail(acct.email||""); setPw(""); setPhone("");
        setAutoFilled(false); setShowAccounts(false);
        setTimeout(() => { document.getElementById("rk-pw-input")?.focus(); }, 80);
      }
    }
  };

  // 格式化時間
  const fmtTime = (iso) => {
    if (!iso) return "";
    const diff = Date.now() - new Date(iso);
    const m = Math.floor(diff/60000), h = Math.floor(diff/3600000), d = Math.floor(diff/86400000);
    if (m < 1) return "剛剛";
    if (m < 60) return `${m}分鐘前`;
    if (h < 24) return `${h}小時前`;
    if (d < 7)  return `${d}天前`;
    const dt = new Date(iso); return `${dt.getMonth()+1}/${dt.getDate()}`;
  };

  // 當前身份是否已有記住我憑證
  const hasSavedCred = sel && loadCreds()[sel]?.rememberMe;

  return (
    <div style={{ minHeight:"100vh", background:`linear-gradient(135deg,#f0f4ff 0%,#fafafa 60%,#fff7ed 100%)`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:24, fontFamily:"'Noto Sans TC',sans-serif" }}>
      <div style={{ width:"100%", maxWidth:400 }}>

        {/* Logo */}
        <div style={{ textAlign:"center", marginBottom:24 }}>
          <div style={{ margin:"0 auto 14px", display:"flex", justifyContent:"center" }}>
            <JRMLogo s={72}/>
          </div>
          <h1 style={{ fontSize:18, fontWeight:800, color:T.text, margin:0, letterSpacing:"-0.02em" }}>家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司</h1>
          <p style={{ color:T.textSub, marginTop:6, fontSize:14 }}>多人協作租屋管理平台</p>
        </div>

        {/* ── 快速帳號列表 ── */}
        {accounts.length > 0 && showAccounts && (
          <div style={{ marginBottom:14 }}>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:10 }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, letterSpacing:"0.05em" }}>⚡ 快速登入</span>
              <button onClick={()=>setShowAccounts(false)} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>＋ 新帳號</button>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:8 }}>
              {accounts.map((acct, i) => {
                const uk = acct.email || acct.phone;
                const isRemoving = confirmRemove === uk;
                const credSaved = loadCreds()[acct.type]?.rememberMe && (loadCreds()[acct.type]?.email === acct.email || loadCreds()[acct.type]?.phone === acct.phone);
                return (
                  <div key={i} style={{ background:T.bg, border:`1.5px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:14, overflow:"hidden", boxShadow:"0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)" }}
                    onMouseEnter={e=>{ if(!isRemoving) e.currentTarget.style.borderColor=roleColor[acct.type]+"66"; }}
                    onMouseLeave={e=>{ e.currentTarget.style.borderColor=T.border; }}>
                    {isRemoving ? (
                      <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, padding:"12px 14px" }}>
                        <span style={{ flex:1, fontSize:13, color:T.text }}>移除「{acct.name}」的快速登入？</span>
                        <button onClick={()=>{ dropAccount(uk); setAccounts(loadAccounts()); setConfirmRemove(null); }} style={{ background:T.redBg, color:T.red, border:"none", borderRadius:7, padding:"5px 12px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>移除</button>
                        <button onClick={()=>setConfirmRemove(null)} style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:"none", borderRadius:7, padding:"5px 10px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button>
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:12, padding:"12px 14px", cursor:"pointer" }}
                        onClick={()=>{ if(!loading) handleQuickSelect(acct); }}>
                        {/* Avatar */}
                        <div style={{ position:"relative", width:42, height:42, flexShrink:0 }}>
                          <div style={{ width:42, height:42, borderRadius:"50%", background:roleColor[acct.type]+"18", border:`2px solid ${roleColor[acct.type]}44`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:17, fontWeight:700, color:roleColor[acct.type] }}>
                            {acct.avatar || acct.name[0]}
                          </div>
                          {/* 記住我標記 */}
                          {credSaved && (
                            <div style={{ position:"absolute", bottom:-1, right:-1, width:14, height:14, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.green, border:`2px solid ${T.bg}`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center" }}>
                              <span style={{ color:"#fff", fontSize:8, lineHeight:1 }}>✓</span>
                            </div>
                          )}
                        </div>
                        {/* Info */}
                        <div style={{ flex:1, minWidth:0 }}>
                          <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                            <span style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{acct.name}</span>
                            <span style={{ fontSize:11, fontWeight:600, background:roleColor[acct.type]+"18", color:roleColor[acct.type], padding:"1px 7px", borderRadius:99 }}>{roleLabel[acct.type]}</span>
                            {credSaved && <span style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.green, fontWeight:600 }}>記住我 ✓</span>}
                          </div>
                          <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2, overflow:"hidden", textOverflow:"ellipsis", whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>
                            {acct.email || acct.phone}
                            {acct.lastLogin && <span style={{ marginLeft:6 }}>· {fmtTime(acct.lastLogin)}</span>}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        {/* Right: arrow + remove */}
                        {loading
                          ? <div style={{ width:18, height:18, borderRadius:"50%", border:`2px solid ${T.border}`, borderTopColor:T.accent, animation:"spin 0.8s linear infinite", flexShrink:0 }}/>
                          : <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:4, flexShrink:0 }}>
                              <span style={{ color:T.textMuted, fontSize:20, lineHeight:1 }}>›</span>
                              <button onClick={e=>{ e.stopPropagation(); setConfirmRemove(uk); }}
                                style={{ background:"none", border:"none", color:T.textMuted, cursor:"pointer", padding:4, borderRadius:6, fontSize:13, lineHeight:1, fontFamily:"inherit" }} title="移除">✕</button>
                            </div>}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* ── 登入表單卡片 ── */}
        <div style={{ background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:20, padding:24, boxShadow:"0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.07)" }}>

          {accounts.length > 0 && !showAccounts && (
            <button onClick={()=>{ setShowAccounts(true); setSel(null); setErr(""); }} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:5, background:"none", border:"none", color:T.accent, fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", marginBottom:14, padding:0, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
              ‹ 回到快速登入
            </button>
          )}

          {!sel && <div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textSub, fontSize:14, padding:"12px 0 8px" }}>請選擇您的身份</div>}

          {/* 自動帶入提示 */}
          {sel && autoFilled && (
            <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:7, background:T.greenBg, border:`1px solid ${T.green}33`, borderRadius:8, padding:"7px 12px", marginBottom:12 }}>
              <span style={{ color:T.green, fontSize:14 }}>✓</span>
              <span style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.green, fontWeight:600 }}>已自動帶入上次儲存的登入資訊</span>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* 租客：手機號碼 */}
          {sel === "tenant" && (
            <>
              <label style={S.label}>手機號碼</label>
              <input id="rk-phone-input" style={S.input} type="tel" value={phone}
                onChange={e=>{ setPhone(e.target.value); setErr(""); setAutoFilled(false); }}
                placeholder="例：0912-345-678"
                onKeyDown={e=>e.key==="Enter"&&canSubmit&&doLogin()} autoFocus/>
            </>
          )}

          {/* 管理員 / 後台維修 / 財務行政：Email + 密碼 */}
          {(sel === "admin" || sel === "superadmin" || sel === "finance") && (
            <>
              <label style={S.label}>帳號</label>
              <input style={S.input} type="text" value={email}
                onChange={e=>{ setEmail(e.target.value); setErr(""); setAutoFilled(false); }}
                placeholder="Email / 手機號碼"
                onKeyDown={e=>e.key==="Enter"&&canSubmit&&doLogin()} autoFocus/>
              <label style={S.label}>密碼</label>
              <input id="rk-pw-input" style={S.input} type="password" value={pw}
                onChange={e=>{ setPw(e.target.value); setErr(""); setAutoFilled(false); }}
                placeholder="••••••••"
                onKeyDown={e=>e.key==="Enter"&&canSubmit&&doLogin()}/>
            </>
          )}

          {/* 記住我 checkbox — 選完身份後才顯示 */}
          {sel && (
            <div onClick={toggleRemember}
              style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, padding:"9px 12px", marginBottom:12, background:rememberMe[sel]?T.greenBg:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${rememberMe[sel]?T.green+"55":T.border}`, borderRadius:9, cursor:"pointer", userSelect:"none", transition:"all 0.15s" }}>
              {/* 勾選框 */}
              <div style={{ width:20, height:20, borderRadius:5, border:`2px solid ${rememberMe[sel]?T.green:T.borderMd}`, background:rememberMe[sel]?T.green:T.bg, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", flexShrink:0, transition:"all 0.15s" }}>
                {rememberMe[sel] && <span style={{ color:"#fff", fontSize:13, lineHeight:1, fontWeight:700 }}>✓</span>}
              </div>
              <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, color:rememberMe[sel]?T.green:T.text }}>記住我的登入資訊</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, marginTop:1 }}>
                  {rememberMe[sel]
                    ? `下次選擇此身份時將自動帶入${sel==="tenant"?"手機號碼":"帳號及密碼"}並直接登入`
                    : `勾選後自動儲存${sel==="tenant"?"手機號碼":"帳號及密碼"}，下次一鍵登入`}
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* 若已儲存過 → 顯示「已儲存」標籤 */}
              {hasSavedCred && (
                <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.green, fontWeight:700, background:T.greenBg, border:`1px solid ${T.green}44`, borderRadius:99, padding:"2px 8px", flexShrink:0 }}>已儲存</span>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* 錯誤提示 */}
          {err && (
            <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6, background:T.redBg, border:`1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px 12px", marginBottom:12 }}>
              <span style={{ color:T.red, fontSize:15 }}>⚠</span>
              <span style={{ color:T.red, fontSize:13, fontWeight:600 }}>{err}</span>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* 登入按鈕 */}
          {sel && (
            <button onClick={()=>doLogin()} disabled={loading||!canSubmit}
              style={{ ...S.btn(), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", padding:"12px", fontSize:15, opacity:(loading||!canSubmit)?0.55:1, marginBottom:0, borderRadius:10, background:loading?T.bgMuted:T.accent }}>
              {loading
                ? <><div style={{ width:16, height:16, borderRadius:"50%", border:"2px solid #fff4", borderTopColor:"#fff", animation:"spin 0.7s linear infinite" }}/>&nbsp;登入中...</>
                : "登入"}
            </button>
          )}

          {/* Divider */}
          <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, margin: sel ? "18px 0 14px" : "8px 0 14px" }}>
            <div style={{ flex:1, height:1, background:T.border }}/>
            <span style={{ color:T.textMuted, fontSize:11, whiteSpace:"nowrap", letterSpacing:"0.06em" }}>選擇登入身份</span>
            <div style={{ flex:1, height:1, background:T.border }}/>
          </div>

          {/* 身份選擇按鈕 */}
          <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8 }}>
            {rolesMeta.map(rb => {
              const active  = sel === rb.key;
              const hasCred = loadCreds()[rb.key]?.rememberMe;
              return (
                <button key={rb.key} onClick={()=>switchRole(rb.key)}
                  style={{ flex:1, display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"center", gap:5, padding:"12px 4px", borderRadius:12, cursor:"pointer", border:`2px solid ${active?rb.color:T.border}`, background:active?rb.bg:T.bgSub, color:active?rb.color:T.textSub, fontWeight:active?700:500, fontSize:12, fontFamily:"inherit", transition:"all 0.15s", position:"relative" }}>
                  <Icon n={rb.icon} s={18}/>
                  {rb.label}
                  {/* 記住我小綠點 */}
                  {hasCred && (
                    <div style={{ position:"absolute", top:6, right:8, width:7, height:7, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.green, border:`1.5px solid ${active?rb.bg:T.bgSub}` }} title="已儲存記住我"/>
                  )}
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>

        <p style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:12, marginTop:14 }}>勾選「記住我」後，下次點擊帳號即可直接登入</p>
      </div>
      <style>{`@keyframes spin{to{transform:rotate(360deg)}}`}</style>
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  DASHBOARD
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function Dashboard({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const { rooms, tenants, bills, repairs, activityLog, users } = data;
  const role = safeRole(currentUser.role);

  const totalRooms = rooms.length;
  const rented = rooms.filter(r=>r.status==="rented").length;
  const occ = totalRooms>0 ? Math.round((rented/totalRooms)*100) : 0;
  const paidRent   = bills.filter(b=>b.status==="paid"&&b.type==="rent").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0);
  const unpaidRent = bills.filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0);
  const pendingCnt = repairs.filter(r=>r.status==="pending").length;
  const expiring   = tenants.filter(t=>t.contractEnd&&!t.isCohabitant&&daysUntil(t.contractEnd)<=60&&daysUntil(t.contractEnd)>0);
  const renewalAlert = rooms.filter(r=>r.status==="rented").map(r=>{
    const t = tenants.find(x=>x.id===r.tenantId||x.roomId===r.id);
    const end = r.contractEnd||t?.contractEnd||"";
    const days = end ? daysUntil(end) : null;
    return { ...r, _end:end, _days:days, _name:r.tenantContactName||t?.name||"" };
  }).filter(r=>r._end&&r._days!==null&&r._days<=45&&r._days>0);
  const onlineUsers = users.filter(u=>u.online&&u.id!==currentUser.id);
  const isFinanceDash = currentUser.role === "finance";

  // ── 催收警示：超過 3 天未繳租 ────────────────────────
  const getOverdueDays = (room) => {
    if (room.status !== "rented") return 0;
    const rentDay = parseInt(room.rentDay || "5");
    // 找最早一筆未繳帳單
    const unpaid = (bills||[]).filter(b => b.roomId===room.id && b.status==="unpaid")
                              .sort((a,b) => a.month.localeCompare(b.month));
    if (!unpaid.length) return 0;
    const [yr, mo] = unpaid[0].month.split("-").map(Number);
    const dueDate  = new Date(yr, mo-1, rentDay);
    return Math.max(0, Math.floor((Date.now() - dueDate.getTime()) / 86400000));
  };
  const overdueRooms = rooms
    .filter(r => r.status==="rented")
    .map(r => ({ ...r, _overdueDays: getOverdueDays(r), _unpaidAmt: (bills||[]).filter(b=>b.roomId===r.id&&b.status==="unpaid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0) }))
    .filter(r => r._overdueDays >= 3)
    .sort((a,b) => b._overdueDays - a._overdueDays);
  // 押金退還待處理（finance 專屬提醒）
  const depositPending = rooms.filter(r => r.depositRefundStatus === "pending");
  // 押金已退還、等待兩日解散的房源
  const depositEvicting = rooms.filter(r => r.depositRefundStatus === "refunded" && !r.depositEvictionDone);

  const doRefundDeposit = (room) => {
    const evictAt = new Date(Date.now() + 2*24*60*60*1000).toISOString();
    onUpdate(d=>({ ...d,
      rooms: d.rooms.map(r => r.id===room.id
        ? { ...r, depositRefundStatus:"refunded", depositRefundedBy:currentUser.id, depositRefundedAt:nowISO(), depositEvictionAt:evictAt }
        : r),
      activityLog: [...d.activityLog, { id:uid(), userId:currentUser.id, action:`【押金退還】「${room.communityName}」已確認退還押金，兩日後自動退租`, timestamp:nowISO() }]
    }));
  };

  const doRenew = (room) => {
    const newEnd = addOneYear(room._end);
    onUpdate(d=>({ ...d, rooms:d.rooms.map(r=>r.id===room.id?{...r,contractEnd:newEnd,leaseStart:room._end}:r), activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`確認「${room.communityName}」續約至 ${newEnd}`,timestamp:nowISO()}] }));
  };

  const stats = [
    { l:"入住率", v:`${occ}%`, sub:`${rented}/${totalRooms} 間`, c:T.blue },
    role.canViewFinance && { l:"待繳款", v:fmt(unpaidRent), sub:`${bills.filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").length} 筆`, c:T.red },
    role.canViewFinance && { l:"已收租金", v:fmt(paidRent), sub:"本月", c:T.green },
    { l:"待處理報修", v:pendingCnt, sub:"件", c:T.amber },
  ].filter(Boolean);

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ marginBottom:20 }}>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, marginBottom:4 }}>
          <h2 style={{ ...S.title, marginBottom:0 }}>總覽</h2>
          {onlineUsers.length>0 && <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:5, background:T.greenBg, border:`1px solid ${T.green}33`, borderRadius:99, padding:"3px 10px" }}>
            <div style={{ width:6, height:6, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.green, animation:"pulse 2s infinite" }}/><span style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.green, fontWeight:600 }}>{onlineUsers.length} 人在線</span>
          </div>}
        </div>
        <p style={{ color:T.textSub, fontSize:14, margin:0 }}>歡迎回來，{currentUser.name} · <span style={{ color:role.color, fontWeight:600 }}>{role.label}</span></p>
      </div>

      {renewalAlert.length>0 && (
        <div style={{ background:T.redBg, border:`2px solid ${T.red}`, borderRadius:12, padding:"14px 16px", marginBottom:16 }}>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, marginBottom:10 }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize:18 }}>🔔</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize:15, fontWeight:800, color:T.red }}>是否確認續約</span>
            <span style={{ marginLeft:"auto", background:T.red, color:"#fff", borderRadius:99, fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, padding:"2px 9px" }}>{renewalAlert.length} 間</span>
          </div>
          {renewalAlert.map(r=>(
            <div key={r.id} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, padding:"10px 0", borderTop:`1px solid ${T.red}33` }}>
              <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, color:T.red }}>{r.communityName}</div>
                {r._name && <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.red, opacity:0.8, marginTop:2 }}>租客：{r._name}</div>}
                <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.red, opacity:0.7, marginTop:2 }}>到期：{toROC(r._end)}　剩 <strong>{r._days}</strong> 天</div>
              </div>
              <button onClick={()=>doRenew(r)} style={{ flexShrink:0, background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"7px 13px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer" }}>✅ 續約完畢</button>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── 催收警示：超過 3 天未繳租 ── */}
      {role.canViewFinance && overdueRooms.length>0 && (
        <div style={{ background:"#fff7ed", border:"2.5px solid #ea580c", borderRadius:12, padding:"14px 16px", marginBottom:16 }}>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, marginBottom:10 }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize:22, animation:"pulse 1s infinite" }}>🚨</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize:15, fontWeight:800, color:"#c2410c" }}>催收警示 — 逾期未繳租</span>
            <span style={{ marginLeft:"auto", background:"#ea580c", color:"#fff", borderRadius:99, fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, padding:"2px 9px", animation:"pulse 1.5s infinite" }}>{overdueRooms.length} 間</span>
          </div>
          {overdueRooms.map(r=>{
            const t = (tenants||[]).find(x => (x.linkedRoom===r.id||x.roomId===r.id) && !x.isCohabitant);
            const daysOver = r._overdueDays;
            const urgency  = daysOver >= 14 ? "#991b1b" : daysOver >= 7 ? "#c2410c" : "#ea580c";
            return (
              <div key={r.id} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, padding:"10px 0", borderTop:"1px solid #ea580c44" }}>
                {/* 房號閃爍標籤 */}
                <div style={{ flexShrink:0, minWidth:72, textAlign:"center", borderRadius:8, padding:"5px 10px", color:"#fff", fontWeight:800, fontSize:13, animation:"warn-blink 1.4s ease-in-out infinite", background:urgency }}>
                  {r.communityName}
                </div>
                <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:"#92400e" }}>
                    {t?.name || r.tenantContactName || "未知租客"}
                    {t?.phone && <span style={{ fontWeight:400, color:"#b45309", marginLeft:6, fontSize:12 }}>{t.phone}</span>}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10, marginTop:3, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:12, color:urgency, fontWeight:700 }}>⏰ 已逾 {daysOver} 天</span>
                    {r._unpaidAmt>0 && <span style={{ fontSize:12, color:"#92400e" }}>未繳：{fmt(r._unpaidAmt)}</span>}
                    {r.rentDay && <span style={{ fontSize:12, color:"#b45309" }}>每月 {r.rentDay} 號應繳</span>}
                  </div>
                </div>
                {role.canEdit && (
                  <button onClick={()=>{
                    const month=new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);
                    const ten=(tenants||[]).find(x=>(x.linkedRoom===r.id||x.roomId===r.id)&&!x.isCohabitant);
                    onUpdate(d=>{
                      // 一次清空該房源所有未繳帳單（聯動房源管理頁的警示狀態）
                      const unpaidMonths=(d.bills||[]).filter(b=>b.roomId===r.id&&b.status==="unpaid").map(b=>b.month);
                      let nb=(d.bills||[]).map(b=>
                        b.roomId===r.id && b.status==="unpaid"
                          ? { ...b, status:"paid", paidDate:todayStr(), recordedBy:currentUser.id }
                          : b
                      );
                      // 若本月尚未產生帳單且也在逾期列表中，補上本月已繳帳單
                      if (!nb.some(b=>b.roomId===r.id&&b.month===month)) {
                        nb=[...nb,{id:uid(),tenantId:ten?.id||r.tenantId||"",roomId:r.id,type:"rent",amount:r.rent,month,status:"paid",paidDate:todayStr(),recordedBy:currentUser.id}];
                        unpaidMonths.push(month);
                      }
                      const monthsLabel=unpaidMonths.length?unpaidMonths.sort().join("、"):month;
                      return{...d,bills:nb,activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`標記「${r.communityName}」${monthsLabel} 租金已繳（催收處理，警示解除）`,timestamp:nowISO()}]};
                    });
                  }} style={{ flexShrink:0, background:"#ea580c", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"7px 12px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit", whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>
                    ✓ 已收款
                  </button>
                )}
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── 財務/行政 專屬：押金退還待處理通知 ── */}
      {isFinanceDash && depositPending.length>0 && (
        <div style={{ background:"#faf5ff", border:"2.5px solid #7c3aed", borderRadius:12, padding:"14px 16px", marginBottom:16 }}>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, marginBottom:10 }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize:22 }}>💰</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize:15, fontWeight:800, color:"#7c3aed" }}>押金退還申請待處理</span>
            <span style={{ marginLeft:"auto", background:"#7c3aed", color:"#fff", borderRadius:99, fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, padding:"2px 9px" }}>{depositPending.length} 間</span>
          </div>
          {depositPending.map(r=>{
            const requestUser = (users||[]).find(u=>u.id===r.depositRefundRequestedBy);
            return (
              <div key={r.id} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, padding:"10px 0", borderTop:"1px solid #7c3aed33" }}>
                <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, color:"#7c3aed" }}>{r.communityName}</div>
                  {r.address&&<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:"#7c3aed", opacity:0.8, marginTop:2 }}>📍 {r.address}</div>}
                  {requestUser&&<div style={{ fontSize:11, color:"#9ca3af", marginTop:2 }}>申請人：{requestUser.name} · {toROC(r.depositRefundRequestedAt,true)}</div>}
                </div>
                <button onClick={()=>doRefundDeposit(r)} style={{ flexShrink:0, background:"#7c3aed", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"8px 14px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>✅ 已退還押金</button>
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── 押金已退還、即將解散的房源提示 ── */}
      {depositEvicting.length>0 && (
        <div style={{ background:"#fffbeb", border:"1.5px solid #f59e0b", borderRadius:10, padding:"12px 14px", marginBottom:14 }}>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:7, marginBottom:8 }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize:16 }}>⏳</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:"#d97706" }}>押金已退回 · 即將自動解除</span>
          </div>
          {depositEvicting.map(r=>{
            const evictDate = r.depositEvictionAt ? new Date(r.depositEvictionAt) : null;
            const daysLeft = evictDate ? Math.max(0, Math.ceil((evictDate - Date.now()) / 86400000)) : null;
            return (
              <div key={r.id} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, padding:"6px 0", borderTop:"1px solid #f59e0b44" }}>
                <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                  <span style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, color:"#92400e" }}>{r.communityName}</span>
                  {daysLeft!==null&&<span style={{ fontSize:12, color:"#d97706", marginLeft:8 }}>約 {daysLeft} 天後自動退租</span>}
                </div>
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}

      <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:10, marginBottom:14 }}>
        {stats.map((s,i)=>(
          <div key={i} style={S.card}>
            <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, letterSpacing:"0.07em", marginBottom:8 }}>{s.l.toUpperCase()}</div>
            <div style={{ fontSize:22, fontWeight:800, color:s.c }}>{s.v}</div>
            <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2 }}>{s.sub}</div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <div style={{ ...S.card, marginBottom:12 }}>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:8 }}>
          <span style={{ color:T.textSub, fontSize:13, fontWeight:600 }}>房間入住狀況</span>
          <span style={{ color:T.blue, fontWeight:700, fontSize:13 }}>{occ}%</span>
        </div>
        <div style={{ background:T.bgMuted, borderRadius:99, height:6, overflow:"hidden", marginBottom:10 }}>
          <div style={{ width:`${occ}%`, height:"100%", background:`linear-gradient(90deg,${T.blue},${T.accent})`, borderRadius:99, transition:"width 0.8s ease" }}/>
        </div>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:4, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
          {rooms.map(r=><div key={r.id} title={r.communityName} style={{ height:6, width:24, borderRadius:3, background:r.status==="rented"?T.blue:T.bgMuted, border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}/>)}
        </div>
      </div>

      {(expiring.length>0||pendingCnt>0) && (
        <div style={{ ...S.card, marginBottom:12 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.amber, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:12 }}>⚠ 待辦事項</div>
          {expiring.map(t=>(
            <div key={t.id} style={{ display:"flex", gap:10, alignItems:"center", padding:"8px 0", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
              <div style={{ width:6, height:6, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.amber, flexShrink:0 }}/>
              <div><div style={{ color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{t.name} 合約即將到期</div><div style={{ color:T.textSub, fontSize:12 }}>剩 {daysUntil(t.contractEnd)} 天</div></div>
            </div>
          ))}
          {pendingCnt>0 && <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10, alignItems:"center", paddingTop:8 }}><div style={{ width:6, height:6, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.red }}/><div style={{ color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{pendingCnt} 件報修待處理</div></div>}
        </div>
      )}

      <div style={S.card}>
        <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:12 }}>最近動態</div>
        {[...activityLog].reverse().slice(0,5).map(log=>{
          const u = users.find(u=>u.id===log.userId);
          const lr = u?safeRole(u.role):null;
          return (
            <div key={log.id} style={{ display:"flex", gap:10, alignItems:"flex-start", padding:"8px 0", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
              {u?<AvatarBadge user={u} size={28}/>:<div style={{ width:28, height:28, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.bgMuted }}/>}
              <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.text }}><span style={{ color:lr?lr.color:T.textSub, fontWeight:600 }}>{u?.name||"系統"}</span> {log.action}</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2 }}>{toROC(log.timestamp,true)}</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  PAYMENT RECORDS — 匯款截圖記錄元件
//  結構：room.paymentRecords = [{ id, month, uploadedBy, uploadedAt, note, image }]
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function PaymentRecords({ room, currentUser, isViewer, onUpdate, onViewPhoto }) {
  const records     = (room.paymentRecords || []).sort((a, b) => b.month.localeCompare(a.month));
  const thisMonth   = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 7);
  const uploadRef   = useRef(null);
  const [uploading, setUploading]   = useState(false);
  const [noteInput, setNoteInput]   = useState("");
  const [showUpload, setShowUpload] = useState(false);
  const [selectedMonth, setSelectedMonth] = useState(thisMonth);
  const [viewConfirmDel, setViewConfirmDel] = useState(null); // record id to delete

  // 產生近 12 個月選單
  const monthOptions = Array.from({ length: 18 }, (_, i) => {
    const d = new Date();
    d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - i);
    return d.toISOString().slice(0, 7);
  });

  const handleFileChange = (e) => {
    const files = Array.from(e.target.files || []);
    if (!files.length) return;
    setUploading(true);
    let done = 0;
    const newRecords = [];
    files.forEach(file => {
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = (ev) => {
        newRecords.push({
          id:          uid(),
          month:       selectedMonth,
          image:       ev.target.result,
          fileName:    file.name,
          fileType:    file.type,
          note:        noteInput.trim(),
          uploadedBy:  currentUser.id,
          uploaderName:currentUser.name,
          uploadedAt:  nowISO(),
        });
        done++;
        if (done === files.length) {
          onUpdate(d => ({
            ...d,
            rooms: d.rooms.map(r => r.id === room.id
              ? { ...r, paymentRecords: [...(r.paymentRecords || []), ...newRecords] }
              : r),
            activityLog: [...d.activityLog, {
              id: uid(), userId: currentUser.id,
              action: `上傳「${room.communityName}」${toROCMonth(selectedMonth)} 匯款截圖 ${files.length} 張`,
              timestamp: nowISO(),
            }],
          }));
          setUploading(false);
          setShowUpload(false);
          setNoteInput("");
        }
      };
      reader.onerror = () => { done++; if (done === files.length) setUploading(false); };
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
    e.target.value = "";
  };

  const deleteRecord = (recId) => {
    const rec = records.find(r => r.id === recId);
    onUpdate(d => ({
      ...d,
      rooms: d.rooms.map(r => r.id === room.id
        ? { ...r, paymentRecords: (r.paymentRecords || []).filter(p => p.id !== recId) }
        : r),
      activityLog: [...d.activityLog, {
        id: uid(), userId: currentUser.id,
        action: `刪除「${room.communityName}」${toROCMonth(rec?.month)} 匯款截圖`,
        timestamp: nowISO(),
      }],
    }));
    setViewConfirmDel(null);
  };

  // 可刪除：superadmin 可刪全部；租客只能刪自己上傳的
  const canDelete = (rec) =>
    isSARole(currentUser.role) ||
    (isViewer && rec.uploadedBy === currentUser.id);

  return (
    <div style={{ marginBottom: 12, border: `1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius: 10, overflow: "hidden" }}>
      {/* Header */}
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "space-between", padding: "10px 14px", background: T.bgSub, borderBottom: records.length > 0 ? `1px solid ${T.border}` : "none" }}>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 7 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 14 }}>💳</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>匯款截圖記錄</span>
          {records.length > 0 && (
            <span style={{ background: T.accent, color: "#fff", fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, borderRadius: 99, padding: "1px 7px" }}>{records.length} 筆</span>
          )}
        </div>
        {/* 租客可上傳；管理員/後台也可以代為上傳 */}
        {(isViewer || currentUser.role === "admin" || isSARole(currentUser.role)) && (
          <button
            onClick={() => setShowUpload(v => !v)}
            style={{ background: showUpload ? T.bgMuted : T.accentBg, color: T.accent, border: `1px solid ${T.accent}44`, borderRadius: 7, padding: "4px 12px", fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>
            {showUpload ? "取消" : "＋ 上傳"}
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 上傳表單 */}
      {showUpload && (
        <div style={{ padding: "12px 14px", background: T.accentBg, borderBottom: `1px solid ${T.accent}22` }}>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginBottom: 8, alignItems: "center" }}>
            <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
              <label style={{ ...S.label, marginBottom: 3 }}>匯款月份</label>
              <select
                value={selectedMonth}
                onChange={e => setSelectedMonth(e.target.value)}
                style={{ ...S.input, marginBottom: 0, fontSize: 13, padding: "7px 10px" }}>
                {monthOptions.map(m => (
                  <option key={m} value={m}>{toROCMonth(m)}</option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>
          <label style={{ ...S.label, marginBottom: 3 }}>備註（選填）</label>
          <input
            style={{ ...S.input, marginBottom: 8, fontSize: 13, padding: "7px 10px" }}
            value={noteInput}
            onChange={e => setNoteInput(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="例：4月租金 NT$16,000"
          />
          <input id={`pay-cam-${room.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" multiple style={{ display: "none" }} onChange={handleFileChange}/>
          <input id={`pay-pic-${room.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*" multiple style={{ display: "none" }} onChange={handleFileChange}/>
          <input id={`pay-file-${room.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf,*/*" multiple style={{ display: "none" }} onChange={handleFileChange}/>
          {uploading ? (
            <div style={{ width: "100%", background: T.accent, color: "#fff", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px", fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, textAlign: "center", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", gap: 7 }}>
              <div style={{ width: 14, height: 14, borderRadius: "50%", border: "2px solid #fff4", borderTopColor: "#fff", animation: "spin 0.7s linear infinite" }}/> 上傳中...
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6 }}>
              <label htmlFor={`pay-cam-${room.id}`} style={{ flex: 1, background: T.accent, color: "#fff", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "center" }}>📷 拍照</label>
              <label htmlFor={`pay-pic-${room.id}`} style={{ flex: 1, background: "#10b981", color: "#fff", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "center" }}>🖼 相簿</label>
              <label htmlFor={`pay-file-${room.id}`} style={{ flex: 1, background: "#6366f1", color: "#fff", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "center" }}>📎 檔案</label>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 記錄列表 */}
      {records.length === 0 ? (
        <div style={{ padding: "20px 14px", textAlign: "center", color: T.textMuted, fontSize: 13 }}>
          尚無匯款截圖記錄
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column" }}>
          {records.map((rec, idx) => (
            <div key={rec.id} style={{ padding: "11px 14px", borderBottom: idx < records.length - 1 ? `1px solid ${T.border}` : "none", background: T.bg }}>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
                {/* 縮圖 */}
                <div
                  onClick={() => onViewPhoto(rec.image)}
                  style={{ width: 52, height: 52, borderRadius: 8, overflow: "hidden", border: `1px solid ${T.border}`, cursor: "pointer", flexShrink: 0, background: T.bgMuted }}>
                  <img src={rec.image} alt="匯款截圖" style={{ width: "100%", height: "100%", objectFit: "cover" }} />
                </div>
                {/* 資訊 */}
                <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>{toROCMonth(rec.month)}</span>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.green, fontWeight: 600, background: T.greenBg, border: `1px solid ${T.green}33`, borderRadius: 99, padding: "1px 7px" }}>✓ 已上傳</span>
                  </div>
                  {rec.note && <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.textSub, marginTop: 2 }}>{rec.note}</div>}
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.textMuted, marginTop: 2 }}>
                    {rec.uploaderName} · {toROC(rec.uploadedAt, true)}
                  </div>
                </div>
                {/* 操作 */}
                <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, flexShrink: 0 }}>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => onViewPhoto(rec.image)}
                    style={{ background: T.bgMuted, color: T.textSub, border: `1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius: 6, padding: "5px 9px", fontSize: 12, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>
                    放大
                  </button>
                  {canDelete(rec) && (
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setViewConfirmDel(rec.id)}
                      style={{ background: T.redBg, color: T.red, border: `1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius: 6, padding: "5px 9px", fontSize: 12, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>
                      刪除
                    </button>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* 確認刪除 inline */}
              {viewConfirmDel === rec.id && (
                <div style={{ marginTop: 8, background: T.redBg, border: `1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius: 8, padding: "9px 12px", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
                  <span style={{ flex: 1, fontSize: 13, color: T.red, fontWeight: 600 }}>確定刪除此截圖？</span>
                  <button onClick={() => deleteRecord(rec.id)} style={{ background: T.red, color: "#fff", border: "none", borderRadius: 6, padding: "5px 12px", fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>刪除</button>
                  <button onClick={() => setViewConfirmDel(null)} style={{ background: T.bgMuted, color: T.textSub, border: "none", borderRadius: 6, padding: "5px 10px", fontSize: 12, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>取消</button>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  DEFECT PANEL
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function DefectPanel({ room, currentUser, onUpdate, onViewPhoto }) {
  const [showForm, setShowForm]     = useState(false);
  const [editItem, setEditItem]     = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm]             = useState({ description:"", photo:"" });
  const [confirmDel, setConfirmDel] = useState(null);
  const [showLog, setShowLog]       = useState(false);
  const defPhotoRef = useRef(null);

  const openAdd  = () => { setForm({ description:"", photo:"" }); setEditItem(null); setShowForm(true); };
  const openEdit = (d) => { setForm({ description:d.description||"", photo:d.photo||"" }); setEditItem(d); setShowForm(true); };
  const cancel   = () => { setShowForm(false); setEditItem(null); };

  const save = () => {
    if (!form.description && !form.photo) return;
    const now = nowISO();
    if (editItem) {
      const entry = { id:uid(), action:"modify", defectId:editItem.id, userId:currentUser.id, userName:currentUser.name, timestamp:now, detail:`修改：${form.description||"（更新照片）"}` };
      onUpdate(d => ({ ...d, rooms:d.rooms.map(r => r.id===room.id ? { ...r,
        defects:(r.defects||[]).map(x => x.id===editItem.id ? {...x,description:form.description,photo:form.photo,updatedBy:currentUser.id,updatedAt:now} : x),
        defectLog:[...(r.defectLog||[]),entry] } : r) }));
    } else {
      const newId = uid();
      const entry = { id:uid(), action:"add", defectId:newId, userId:currentUser.id, userName:currentUser.name, timestamp:now, detail:`新增：${form.description||"（上傳照片）"}` };
      onUpdate(d => ({ ...d, rooms:d.rooms.map(r => r.id===room.id ? { ...r,
        defects:[...(r.defects||[]), { id:newId, description:form.description, photo:form.photo, createdBy:currentUser.id, createdAt:now, updatedBy:null, updatedAt:null }],
        defectLog:[...(r.defectLog||[]),entry] } : r) }));
    }
    cancel();
  };

  const doDelete = (d) => {
    const entry = { id:uid(), action:"delete", defectId:d.id, userId:currentUser.id, userName:currentUser.name, timestamp:nowISO(), detail:`刪除：${d.description||"（已刪除照片）"}` };
    onUpdate(data => ({ ...data, rooms:data.rooms.map(r => r.id===room.id ? { ...r,
      defects:(r.defects||[]).filter(x => x.id!==d.id),
      defectLog:[...(r.defectLog||[]),entry] } : r) }));
    setConfirmDel(null);
  };

  const logColor = { add:T.green, modify:T.amber, delete:T.red };
  const logLabel = { add:"新增", modify:"修改", delete:"刪除" };
  const defects   = room.defects  || [];
  const defectLog = room.defectLog|| [];

  return (
    <div style={{ marginBottom:12 }}>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:8 }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6 }}>
          🔍 屋況瑕疵
          {defects.length>0&&<span style={{ background:T.amberBg, color:T.amber, fontSize:10, fontWeight:700, borderRadius:99, padding:"1px 7px" }}>{defects.length}</span>}
        </div>
        <button onClick={openAdd} style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:12 }}><Icon n="plus" s={12}/> 新增</button>
      </div>

      {defects.length===0&&!showForm&&<div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:12, padding:"8px 0 4px" }}>尚無瑕疵記錄</div>}

      {defects.map(d=>(
        <div key={d.id} style={{ background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 12px", marginBottom:6 }}>
          {confirmDel===d.id?(
            <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8 }}>
              <span style={{ flex:1, fontSize:12, color:T.text }}>確認刪除此瑕疵？</span>
              <button onClick={()=>doDelete(d)} style={{ background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>確認</button>
              <button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(null)} style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button>
            </div>
          ):(
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10, alignItems:"flex-start" }}>
              {d.photo&&<img src={d.photo} style={{ width:54, height:54, borderRadius:6, objectFit:"cover", cursor:"pointer", flexShrink:0, border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }} onClick={()=>onViewPhoto(d.photo)}/>}
              <div style={{ flex:1, minWidth:0 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.text, lineHeight:1.6, wordBreak:"break-all" }}>{d.description||"（無文字描述）"}</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:3 }}>
                  {d.updatedAt?`修改：${toROC(d.updatedAt,true)}`:`新增：${toROC(d.createdAt,true)}`}
                  　by {(d.updatedAt?d.updatedBy:d.createdBy)===currentUser.id?"我":currentUser.name}
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:4, flexShrink:0 }}>
                <button onClick={()=>openEdit(d)} style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 8px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}><Icon n="edit" s={12}/></button>
                <button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(d.id)} style={{ background:T.redBg, color:T.red, border:`1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 8px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}><Icon n="trash" s={12}/></button>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      ))}

      {showForm&&(
        <div style={{ background:T.accentBg, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}33`, borderRadius:8, padding:"12px", marginBottom:8 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, marginBottom:8 }}>{editItem?"✏️ 編輯瑕疵":"➕ 新增瑕疵"}</div>
          <input ref={defPhotoRef} type="file" accept="image/*,*/*" onChange={e=>{ const f=e.target.files[0]; if(!f)return; const r=new FileReader(); r.onload=ev=>setForm(fm=>({...fm,photo:ev.target.result})); r.readAsDataURL(f); }} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
          <button onClick={()=>defPhotoRef.current?.click()} style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", marginBottom:8, fontSize:12 }}>
            {form.photo?"✅ 已上傳照片（點擊更換）":"📷 上傳照片（選填）"}
          </button>
          <textarea value={form.description} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,description:e.target.value}))} placeholder="描述瑕疵狀況，例如：客廳牆壁有裂縫..." style={{ ...S.input, height:68, resize:"vertical", fontSize:13, marginBottom:8 }}/>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8 }}>
            <button onClick={save} style={{ flex:1, ...S.btn(), justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13 }}>儲存</button>
            <button onClick={cancel} style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), fontSize:13 }}>取消</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {defectLog.length>0&&(
        <div style={{ marginTop:6 }}>
          <button onClick={()=>setShowLog(v=>!v)} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:11, fontFamily:"inherit", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:4, padding:"4px 0", userSelect:"none" }}>
            <span style={{ transform:showLog?"rotate(90deg)":"rotate(0deg)", display:"inline-block", transition:"transform .15s" }}>▶</span>
            瑕疵變更記錄（{defectLog.length} 筆）
          </button>
          {showLog&&(
            <div style={{ background:T.bgMuted, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 12px", marginTop:4 }}>
              {[...defectLog].reverse().map(log=>(
                <div key={log.id} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"flex-start", gap:8, marginBottom:5 }}>
                  <span style={{ padding:"2px 7px", borderRadius:99, fontSize:10, fontWeight:700, background:(logColor[log.action]||T.textMuted)+"22", color:logColor[log.action]||T.textMuted, flexShrink:0 }}>{logLabel[log.action]||log.action}</span>
                  <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.text }}>{log.detail}</span>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, marginLeft:6 }}>by {log.userName||"未知"}</span>
                  </div>
                  <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, flexShrink:0, whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>{toROC(log.timestamp,true)}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ── 動態載入外部腳本（jsPDF / html2canvas / SignaturePad）──
const loadScript = (src) => new Promise((res) => {
  if (document.querySelector(`script[src="${src}"]`)) { res(); return; }
  const s = document.createElement("script");
  s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = res; // 失敗也繼續
  document.head.appendChild(s);
});

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  CONTRACT MODAL
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function ContractModal({ room, tenant, onClose }) {
  const landlordRef = useRef(null);
  const tenantRef   = useRef(null);
  const padsRef     = useRef({ landlord:null, tenant:null });
  const contractRef = useRef(null);
  const bigCanvasRef = useRef(null);
  const bigPadRef = useRef(null);
  const [ready,       setReady]       = useState(false);
  const [downloading, setDownloading] = useState(false);
  const [lHint, setLHint] = useState(true);
  const [tHint, setTHint] = useState(true);
  const [sigData, setSigData] = useState({ landlord:null, tenant:null });
  const [bigSig, setBigSig] = useState(null); // { key, label }

  const fmtM = (n) => parseInt(n||0).toLocaleString();
  const todayROC = toROC(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10));
  const dep = tenant?.deposit ? fmtM(tenant.deposit) : "___";

  // ── 載入 CDN 腳本 ────────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    Promise.all([
      loadScript("https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jspdf/2.5.1/jspdf.umd.min.js"),
      loadScript("https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2canvas/1.4.1/html2canvas.min.js"),
      loadScript("https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/signature_pad@4.1.7/dist/signature_pad.umd.min.js"),
    ]).then(() => setReady(true));
  }, []);

  // ── 初始化簽名板（小預覽 canvas 只用來展示，不收手寫輸入）──
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!ready || !window.SignaturePad) return;
    [["landlord", landlordRef, setLHint], ["tenant", tenantRef, setTHint]].forEach(([k, ref, setHint]) => {
      if (!ref.current) return;
      ref.current.width  = ref.current.parentElement.offsetWidth || 300;
      ref.current.height = 90;
      const pad = new window.SignaturePad(ref.current, { penColor:"#111827", backgroundColor:"rgba(0,0,0,0)" });
      pad.addEventListener("beginStroke", () => setHint(false));
      padsRef.current[k] = pad;
    });
  }, [ready]);

  // ── 放大簽名 Pad 初始化 ───────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!bigSig || !window.SignaturePad || !bigCanvasRef.current) return;
    const cv = bigCanvasRef.current;
    const ratio = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const rect = cv.getBoundingClientRect();
    cv.width  = rect.width * ratio;
    cv.height = rect.height * ratio;
    cv.getContext("2d").scale(ratio, ratio);
    const pad = new window.SignaturePad(cv, { penColor:"#111827", backgroundColor:"#ffffff", minWidth:1.2, maxWidth:3 });
    // 若已有之前的簽名，載入
    const prev = sigData[bigSig.key];
    if (prev) pad.fromDataURL(prev, { width:rect.width, height:rect.height });
    bigPadRef.current = pad;
    return () => { pad.off(); bigPadRef.current = null; };
  }, [bigSig]);

  const clearSig = (k) => {
    padsRef.current[k]?.clear();
    setSigData(s => ({ ...s, [k]:null }));
    if (k==="landlord") setLHint(true); else setTHint(true);
  };

  const confirmBigSig = () => {
    if (!bigPadRef.current || bigPadRef.current.isEmpty()) { alert("請先簽名"); return; }
    const dataUrl = bigPadRef.current.toDataURL("image/png");
    const k = bigSig.key;
    setSigData(s => ({ ...s, [k]:dataUrl }));
    // 將簽名畫進小 canvas，讓 html2canvas 能捕捉
    const smallRef = k==="landlord" ? landlordRef : tenantRef;
    const cv = smallRef.current;
    if (cv) {
      const ctx = cv.getContext("2d");
      ctx.clearRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      const img = new Image();
      img.onload = () => { ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, cv.width, cv.height); };
      img.src = dataUrl;
    }
    if (k==="landlord") setLHint(false); else setTHint(false);
    setBigSig(null);
  };

  // ── 下載 PDF ──────────────────────────────────────────
  const downloadPDF = async () => {
    if (!window.html2canvas || !window.jspdf) { alert("PDF 工具載入中，請稍候再試"); return; }
    setDownloading(true);
    try {
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 150));
      const el = contractRef.current;
      const canvas = await window.html2canvas(el, { scale:2, useCORS:true, backgroundColor:"#ffffff", logging:false });
      const { jsPDF } = window.jspdf;
      const doc   = new jsPDF({ orientation:"portrait", unit:"mm", format:"a4" });
      const pageW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
      const pageH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
      const imgW  = pageW - 20;
      const sliceH = Math.floor(canvas.width * (pageH - 20) / imgW);
      let srcY = 0, remaining = canvas.height, firstPage = true;
      while (remaining > 0) {
        const curr = Math.min(remaining, sliceH);
        const c2 = document.createElement("canvas");
        c2.width = canvas.width; c2.height = curr;
        c2.getContext("2d").drawImage(canvas, 0, srcY, canvas.width, curr, 0, 0, canvas.width, curr);
        const h = (curr / canvas.width) * imgW;
        if (!firstPage) doc.addPage();
        doc.addImage(c2.toDataURL("image/jpeg", 0.95), "JPEG", 10, 10, imgW, h);
        remaining -= curr; srcY += curr; firstPage = false;
      }
      const name = room.tenantContactName || tenant?.name || "房客";
      doc.save(`租賃契約書_${name}_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.pdf`);
    } catch(e) { alert("PDF 產生失敗：" + e.message); }
    setDownloading(false);
  };

  // ── 合約區塊輔助元件 ──────────────────────────────────
  const Sec = ({ title, children }) => (
    <div style={{ marginBottom:14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, borderLeft:`3px solid ${T.accent}`, paddingLeft:8, marginBottom:8 }}>{title}</div>
      {children}
    </div>
  );
  const Tbl = ({ rows }) => (
    <table style={{ width:"100%", borderCollapse:"collapse", fontSize:13, marginBottom:4 }}>
      <tbody>
        {rows.map(([k,v],i) => (
          <tr key={i}>
            <td style={{ padding:"6px 10px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, background:T.bgSub, fontWeight:600, width:"35%", color:T.textSub, fontSize:12 }}>{k}</td>
            <td style={{ padding:"6px 10px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, color:T.text }}>{v||"—"}</td>
          </tr>
        ))}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  );
  const Para = ({ children }) => (
    <div style={{ fontSize:13, lineHeight:2, color:"#374151" }}>{children}</div>
  );

  return (
    <Modal title={`📄 合約預覽 — ${room.communityName}`} onClose={onClose} width={680}>
      {/* ── 工具列 ── */}
      <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, marginBottom:14, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
        <button onClick={downloadPDF} disabled={!ready||downloading}
          style={{ ...S.btn(T.green), flex:1, justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13, opacity:(!ready||downloading)?0.6:1 }}>
          {downloading ? "⏳ 產生中…" : "⬇️ 下載 PDF"}
        </button>
        <button onClick={()=>window.print()}
          style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), flex:1, justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13 }}>
          🖨️ 列印
        </button>
      </div>
      {!ready && (
        <div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:13, padding:"8px 0 14px" }}>
          ⏳ 載入 PDF 工具中…
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── 合約本體（html2canvas 捕捉範圍）── */}
      <div ref={contractRef} style={{ background:"#fff", padding:"24px 20px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:10, fontFamily:"'Noto Sans TC',sans-serif" }}>
        {/* 標題 */}
        <div style={{ textAlign:"center", fontSize:20, fontWeight:800, marginBottom:4, letterSpacing:"0.04em", color:"#111827" }}>房屋租賃契約書</div>
        <div style={{ textAlign:"center", fontSize:12, color:"#6b7280", marginBottom:22 }}>立約日期：{todayROC}　　管理公司：家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司</div>

        <Sec title="第一條　租賃標的">
          <Tbl rows={[
            ["房屋名稱／門牌", (room.address && room.address !== room.communityName) ? `${room.communityName}（${room.address}）` : room.communityName || "___"],
            ["月租金",         `新臺幣 ${fmtM(room.rent)} 元整`],
            ["押金",           `新臺幣 ${dep} 元整`],
            ["每月繳租日",     `每月 ${room.rentDay||"5"} 日前繳清`],
            ["屋主姓名",       room.ownerName || "___"],
          ]}/>
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第二條　租賃期間">
          <Tbl rows={[
            ["起租日期", toROC(room.leaseStart)],
            ["到期日期", toROC(room.contractEnd)],
          ]}/>
          {(room.renewals||[]).length>0&&(
            <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, marginTop:4 }}>
              （已續約 {room.renewals.length} 次，最新到期：{toROC(room.renewals[room.renewals.length-1].renewEnd)}）
            </div>
          )}
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第三條　承租人資料">
          <Tbl rows={[
            ["姓名",       room.tenantContactName || tenant?.name || "___"],
            ["聯絡電話",   room.tenantContactPhone || tenant?.phone || "___"],
            ["緊急聯絡人", tenant?.emergencyName ? `${tenant.emergencyName}${tenant.emergencyPhone?" / "+tenant.emergencyPhone:""}` : "___"],
            ...(room.cohabitants||[]).map((c,i)=>[`同住人 ${i+1}`, `${c.name||"___"}${c.phone?" ／ "+c.phone:""}`]),
          ]}/>
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第四條　使用規定">
          <Para>
            一、承租人應依約定用途使用房屋，不得擅自改裝或破壞結構。<br/>
            二、未經出租人同意，不得將房屋轉租、分租或借他人使用。<br/>
            三、承租人應負責保持房屋及公共區域之整潔。
          </Para>
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第五條　修繕義務">
          <Para>
            一、房屋因自然損耗或設備故障，由出租人負責修繕。<br/>
            二、因承租人使用不當造成之損毀，由承租人自行負責。<br/>
            三、報修請通知管理公司，並於合理期限內完成修繕。
          </Para>
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第六條　違約處理">
          <Para>
            一、承租人無故提前終止契約，應賠償一個月租金作為違約金。<br/>
            二、出租人無故提前終止契約，應退還雙倍押金予承租人。<br/>
            三、租金逾期繳納超過 7 日，出租人得催告；逾期仍未繳清者，得終止契約。
          </Para>
        </Sec>

        {/* ── 簽名區（點擊放大簽名，html2canvas 會捕捉 canvas 內容）── */}
        <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:16, marginTop:20 }}>
          {[
            { label:"出租人（房東）簽名", key:"landlord", ref:landlordRef, hint:lHint },
            { label:"承租人（房客）簽名", key:"tenant",   ref:tenantRef,   hint:tHint },
          ].map(({ label, key, ref, hint }) => (
            <div key={key}>
              <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, marginBottom:6 }}>{label}</div>
              <div onClick={()=>setBigSig({ key, label })}
                style={{ position:"relative", border:`1.5px dashed ${T.accent}88`, borderRadius:8, background:"#fafafa", height:90, overflow:"hidden", cursor:"pointer" }}
                title="點擊放大簽名">
                <canvas ref={ref} style={{ width:"100%", height:"100%", display:"block", pointerEvents:"none" }}/>
                {hint && (
                  <div style={{ position:"absolute", inset:0, display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:12, color:T.accent, pointerEvents:"none", gap:3, fontWeight:600 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:18 }}>✍️</span>
                    <span>點擊此處放大簽名</span>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
              <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginTop:4 }}>
                <button onClick={(e)=>{e.stopPropagation(); clearSig(key);}} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, cursor:"pointer", padding:0, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>✕ 清除</button>
                <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted }}>日期：{todayROC}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, textAlign:"center", marginTop:10, lineHeight:1.6 }}>
        ※ 此為系統自動產出之合約草稿，點擊簽名欄位可放大簽名，簽名後下載 PDF 留存正本。
      </div>

      {/* ── 放大簽名 Modal ── */}
      {bigSig && (
        <div onClick={(e)=>{ if(e.target===e.currentTarget) setBigSig(null); }}
          style={{ position:"fixed", inset:0, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.75)", zIndex:3000, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:12 }}>
          <div style={{ background:"#fff", borderRadius:14, padding:"16px 16px 14px", width:"min(700px,96vw)", display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10 }}>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center" }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize:15, fontWeight:800, color:T.text }}>✍️ {bigSig.label}</div>
