                      </div>}
                    </div>
                    <button onClick={()=>delSpot(spot.id)} style={{ ...S.btn(T.red,true), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:12 }}>🗑 刪除此車位</button>
                  </div>}
                </div>
              );
            };
            return (
              <div style={{ border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:9, marginBottom:14, overflow:"hidden" }}>
                <div onClick={()=>setShowParking(v=>!v)} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", padding:"10px 13px", cursor:"pointer", background:showParking?T.accentBg:T.bgMuted, userSelect:"none" }}>
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:7 }}><span style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:showParking?T.accent:T.text }}>🅿 是否加租其他車位</span>{totalCount>0&&<span style={{ background:T.accent, color:"#fff", fontSize:11, fontWeight:700, borderRadius:99, padding:"1px 7px" }}>{totalCount} 個</span>}</div>
                  <span style={{ color:T.textMuted, fontSize:11, transform:showParking?"rotate(180deg)":"rotate(0deg)", display:"inline-block", transition:"transform 0.2s" }}>▼</span>
                </div>
                {showParking&&<div style={{ padding:"12px 13px", background:T.bg, borderTop:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
                  {/* 汽車車位 */}
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:8 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.text }}>🚗 汽車車位</span>
                    <button onClick={()=>addSpot("car")} style={{ ...S.btn(T.blue,true), fontSize:11, padding:"3px 10px" }}><Icon n="plus" s={11}/> 新增</button>
                  </div>
                  {carSpots.length===0&&<div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:12, padding:"6px 0 10px" }}>尚無汽車車位</div>}
                  {carSpots.map(s=><React.Fragment key={s.id}>{renderParkingSpotBlock(s)}</React.Fragment>)}
                  {/* 機車車位 */}
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginTop:4, marginBottom:8 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.text }}>🛵 機車車位</span>
                    <button onClick={()=>addSpot("moto")} style={{ ...S.btn(T.blue,true), fontSize:11, padding:"3px 10px" }}><Icon n="plus" s={11}/> 新增</button>
                  </div>
                  {motoSpots.length===0&&<div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:12, padding:"6px 0 4px" }}>尚無機車車位</div>}
                  {motoSpots.map(s=><React.Fragment key={s.id}>{renderParkingSpotBlock(s)}</React.Fragment>)}
                </div>}
              </div>
            );
          })()}

          <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.blue, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:10, letterSpacing:"0.06em" }}>租客聯絡</div>
          {[["tenantContactName","主租客姓名"],["tenantContactPhone","主租客電話"]].map(([k,l])=><div key={k}><label style={S.label}>{l}</label><input style={{...S.input,...fs(form[k])}} value={form[k]} onChange={sf(k)}/></div>)}
          {(form.cohabitants||[]).map((c,i)=><div key={i} style={{ background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 12px", marginBottom:8 }}>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:8 }}><span style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700 }}>同住人 {i+1}</span><button onClick={()=>setForm(f=>({...f,cohabitants:f.cohabitants.filter((_,j)=>j!==i)}))} style={{ background:T.redBg, color:T.red, border:"none", borderRadius:5, padding:"3px 9px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>刪除</button></div>
            <label style={S.label}>姓名</label><input style={{...S.input,...fs(c.name)}} value={c.name} placeholder="同住人姓名" onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,cohabitants:f.cohabitants.map((x,j)=>j===i?{...x,name:e.target.value}:x)}))}/>
            <label style={S.label}>電話</label><input style={{ ...S.input, marginBottom:0, ...fs(c.phone) }} value={c.phone} placeholder="同住人電話" onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,cohabitants:f.cohabitants.map((x,j)=>j===i?{...x,phone:e.target.value}:x)}))}/>
          </div>)}
          <button onClick={()=>setForm(f=>({...f,cohabitants:[...(f.cohabitants||[]),{name:"",phone:""}]}))} style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", marginBottom:12 }}><Icon n="plus" s={13}/> 新增同住人</button>
          {/* LINE 分享 */}
          <div style={{ background:"#f0fdf4", border:"1px solid #bbf7d0", borderRadius:9, padding:"10px 12px", marginBottom:12 }}>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, marginBottom:6 }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:"#15803d" }}>💚 LINE 催繳通知</span>
              <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:"#16a34a", background:"#dcfce7", borderRadius:99, padding:"1px 7px", fontWeight:600 }}>點按鈕直接開啟 LINE</span>
            </div>
            <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:"#15803d", lineHeight:1.7, marginBottom:8 }}>
              待繳租時，點「📲 LINE 催繳」按鈕後會自動開啟 LINE，<br/>自行選擇要傳送給哪位租客即可。
            </div>
            <label style={{ ...S.label, color:"#15803d", marginBottom:4 }}>LINE 聯絡備注（選填）</label>
            <input style={{ ...S.input, marginBottom:0, ...fs(form.lineNotifyToken) }} value={form.lineNotifyToken||""} onChange={sf("lineNotifyToken")} placeholder="例如：租客 LINE 暱稱、群組名稱（僅供備注）"/>
          </div>

          {/* 照片區 */}
          <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.blue, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:10, marginTop:4, letterSpacing:"0.06em" }}>照片</div>
          <div style={{ marginBottom:10 }}>
            <label style={S.label}>租約電子檔 <span style={{ fontWeight:400, color:T.textMuted }}>（所有人可讀取下載，可多張）</span></label>
            <input id="ctr-cam" type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" multiple onChange={handleContractUpload} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
            <input id="ctr-pic" type="file" accept="image/*" multiple onChange={handleContractUpload} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
            <input id="ctr-file" type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf,*/*" multiple onChange={handleContractUpload} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:6, marginBottom:8 }}>
              <label htmlFor="ctr-cam" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📷 拍照</label>
              <label htmlFor="ctr-pic" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>🖼 相簿</label>
              <label htmlFor="ctr-file" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📎 檔案</label>
            </div>
            {(form.contractPhotos||[]).length>0&&(
              <div style={{ display:"flex", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:8, marginBottom:4 }}>
                {(form.contractPhotos||[]).map((p,i)=>(
                  <div key={p.id||i} style={{ position:"relative" }}>
                    <img src={p.dataUrl} style={{ width:72, height:72, borderRadius:7, objectFit:"cover", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, cursor:"pointer" }} onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(p.dataUrl)}/>
                    <button onClick={()=>setForm(f=>({...f,contractPhotos:f.contractPhotos.filter((_,j)=>j!==i)}))}
                      style={{ position:"absolute", top:-5, right:-5, width:18, height:18, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:10, fontFamily:"inherit", padding:0 }}>✕</button>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          {/* 屋主匯款帳號：所有人可讀取下載，管理員以上可上傳修改 */}
          <div style={{ marginBottom:10 }}>
            <label style={S.label}>屋主匯款帳號 <span style={{ fontWeight:400, color:T.textMuted }}>（所有人可讀取下載）</span></label>
            {(() => {
              const onBank = e => { const f=e.target.files[0]; if(!f)return; const r=new FileReader(); r.onload=ev=>setForm(fm=>({...fm,ownerBankPhoto:ev.target.result})); r.readAsDataURL(f); e.target.value=""; };
              return <>
                <input id="bnk-cam" type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" onChange={onBank} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
                <input id="bnk-pic" type="file" accept="image/*" onChange={onBank} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
                <input id="bnk-file" type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf,*/*" onChange={onBank} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
              </>;
            })()}
            {form.ownerBankPhoto && <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.green, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:6 }}>✅ 已上傳，點下方按鈕可更換</div>}
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:6 }}>
              <label htmlFor="bnk-cam" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📷 拍照</label>
              <label htmlFor="bnk-pic" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>🖼 相簿</label>
              <label htmlFor="bnk-file" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📎 檔案</label>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* 出租點交室內照片：所有人可讀取下載，管理員以上可上傳修改 */}
          <div style={{ marginBottom:10 }}>
            <label style={S.label}>出租點交室內照片 <span style={{ fontWeight:400, color:T.textMuted }}>（所有人可讀取下載，可多張）</span></label>
            <input id="ins-cam" type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" multiple onChange={handleInspectionUpload} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
            <input id="ins-pic" type="file" accept="image/*" multiple onChange={handleInspectionUpload} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
            <input id="ins-file" type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf,*/*" multiple onChange={handleInspectionUpload} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:6, marginBottom:8 }}>
              <label htmlFor="ins-cam" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📷 拍照</label>
              <label htmlFor="ins-pic" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>🖼 相簿</label>
              <label htmlFor="ins-file" style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"8px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📎 檔案</label>
            </div>
            {(form.inspectionPhotos||[]).length>0&&(
              <div style={{ display:"flex", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:8 }}>
                {(form.inspectionPhotos||[]).map((p,i)=>(
                  <div key={p.id||i} style={{ position:"relative" }}>
                    <img src={p.dataUrl} style={{ width:72, height:72, borderRadius:7, objectFit:"cover", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, cursor:"pointer" }} onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(p.dataUrl)}/>
                    <button onClick={()=>setForm(f=>({...f,inspectionPhotos:f.inspectionPhotos.filter((_,j)=>j!==i)}))}
                      style={{ position:"absolute", top:-5, right:-5, width:18, height:18, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:10, fontFamily:"inherit", padding:0 }}>✕</button>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* ── 負責管理員：多選 ── */}
          {isSA && (
            <div style={{ marginBottom:12 }}>
              <label style={{ ...S.label, marginBottom:8, display:"block" }}>負責管理員 <span style={{ fontWeight:400, color:T.textMuted }}>（可複選，未指定則所有人皆可見）</span></label>
              <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:6 }}>
                {(data.users||[]).filter(u=>u.role!=="system").map(u=>{
                  const checked=(form.assignedAdmins||[]).includes(u.id);
                  const isSelf=u.id===currentUser.id;
                  const roleInfo=safeRole(u.role);
                  return (
                    <label key={u.id} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, cursor:"pointer", background:checked?T.accentBg:T.bgSub, border:`1.5px solid ${checked?T.accent+"66":T.border}`, borderRadius:9, padding:"8px 12px", transition:"all .15s" }}>
                      <input type="checkbox" checked={checked} onChange={()=>setForm(f=>({ ...f, assignedAdmins: checked ? (f.assignedAdmins||[]).filter(id=>id!==u.id) : [...(f.assignedAdmins||[]), u.id] }))} style={{ width:16, height:16, accentColor:T.blue, cursor:"pointer", flexShrink:0 }}/>
                      <div style={{ width:28, height:28, borderRadius:"50%", background:roleInfo.color, color:"#fff", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", flexShrink:0 }}>{u.avatar||u.name[0]}</div>
                      <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                        <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6 }}>
                          <span style={{ fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, color:T.text }}>{u.name}</span>
                          {isSelf&&<span style={{ fontSize:10, fontWeight:700, background:T.blue, color:"#fff", borderRadius:99, padding:"1px 6px" }}>我</span>}
                          <span style={{ fontSize:10, fontWeight:600, color:roleInfo.color, background:roleInfo.color+"18", borderRadius:99, padding:"1px 6px" }}>{roleInfo.label}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted }}>{u.email||u.account||""}</div>
                      </div>
                    </label>
                  );
                })}
                {(data.users||[]).filter(u=>u.role!=="system").length===0&&<div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textMuted, padding:"8px 0" }}>目前尚無帳號</div>}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          <button onClick={saveRoom} style={{ ...S.btn(), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", padding:11, marginTop:4 }}>{editRoom?"儲存修改":"確認新增"}</button>
        </Modal>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  TENANTS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function Tenants({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const { tenants, rooms } = data;
  const isSA = isSARole(currentUser.role);
  const [sel, setSel] = useState(null);
  const [showForm, setShowForm] = useState(false);
  const [editT, setEditT] = useState(null);
  const [confirmDel, setConfirmDel] = useState(null);
  const EMPTY = { name:"",phone:"",email:"",idNo:"",roomId:"",moveIn:"",contractEnd:"",deposit:"",emergencyName:"",emergencyPhone:"",note:"" };
  const [form, setForm] = useState(EMPTY);
  const sf = k => e => setForm(f=>({...f,[k]:e.target.value}));

  const saveTenant = () => {
    if (!form.name) return;
    if (editT) {
      onUpdate(d=>({...d,tenants:d.tenants.map(t=>t.id===editT.id?{...t,...form,deposit:parseInt(form.deposit)||0}:t),rooms:d.rooms.map(r=>{ if(r.id===editT.roomId&&r.id!==form.roomId)return{...r,status:"vacant",tenantId:null}; if(r.id===form.roomId)return{...r,status:"rented",tenantId:editT.id}; return r; }),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`修改房客「${form.name}」資料`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}));
    } else {
      const nid=uid();
      onUpdate(d=>({...d,tenants:[...d.tenants,{id:nid,...form,deposit:parseInt(form.deposit)||0}],rooms:d.rooms.map(r=>r.id===form.roomId?{...r,status:"rented",tenantId:nid}:r),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`新增房客「${form.name}」`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}));
    }
    setShowForm(false); setEditT(null);
  };

  const delTenant = (t) => {
    onUpdate(d=>({...d,tenants:d.tenants.filter(x=>x.id!==t.id),rooms:d.rooms.map(r=>r.id===t.roomId?{...r,status:"vacant",tenantId:null}:r),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`刪除房客「${t.name}」`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}));
    setConfirmDel(null); setSel(null);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:16 }}>
        <h2 style={S.title}>房客管理</h2>
        {isSA&&<button onClick={()=>{setForm(EMPTY);setEditT(null);setShowForm(true);}} style={S.btn()}><Icon n="plus" s={13}/> 新增房客</button>}
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10 }}>
        {(tenants||[]).map(t=>{
          const r=rooms.find(x=>x.id===t.roomId);
          const days=t.contractEnd?daysUntil(t.contractEnd):null;
          const near=days!==null&&days<=60&&days>0;
          const open=sel===t.id;
          return (
            <div key={t.id} style={{ ...S.card, borderColor:near?T.amber+"66":T.border }}>
              <div onClick={()=>setSel(open?null:t.id)} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:12, cursor:"pointer" }}>
                <div style={{ width:38, height:38, borderRadius:"50%", background:t.isCohabitant?T.bgMuted:T.accentBg, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontWeight:700, fontSize:15, color:t.isCohabitant?T.textSub:T.accent, flexShrink:0 }}>{(t.name||"?")[0]}</div>
                <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6 }}><span style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{t.name}</span>{t.isCohabitant&&<span style={S.tag(T.textMuted)}>同住人</span>}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, marginTop:1 }}>{r?.communityName||"未分配"} · {t.phone}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"flex-end", gap:4 }}>
                  {near&&<span style={S.tag(T.amber)}>即將到期</span>}
                  <span style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted }}>{open?"▲":"▼"}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              {open&&<div style={{ marginTop:14, paddingTop:14, borderTop:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
                <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:8, marginBottom:10 }}>
                  {[["入住日",toROC(t.moveIn)],["合約到期",toROC(t.contractEnd)],["押金",t.deposit?fmt(t.deposit):"—"],["剩餘天數",days!==null?`${days} 天`:"—"]].map(([k,v])=><div key={k} style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderRadius:7, padding:"8px 10px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}><div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600, marginBottom:2 }}>{k}</div><div style={{ fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, color:T.text }}>{v}</div></div>)}
                </div>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, marginBottom:isSA?10:0 }}>
                  {t.phone&&<a href={`tel:${t.phone}`} style={{ flex:1, background:T.greenBg, color:T.green, border:`1px solid ${T.green}44`, borderRadius:8, padding:"9px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, textDecoration:"none", textAlign:"center" }}>📞 撥打電話</a>}
                  {t.email&&<a href={`mailto:${t.email}`} style={{ flex:1, background:T.accentBg, color:T.accent, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}44`, borderRadius:8, padding:"9px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, textDecoration:"none", textAlign:"center" }}>✉️ 寄信</a>}
                </div>
                {isSA&&<div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, paddingTop:10, borderTop:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
                  <button onClick={()=>{setForm({...EMPTY,...t,deposit:String(t.deposit||"")});setEditT(t);setShowForm(true);}} style={{ flex:1, ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13 }}><Icon n="edit" s={13}/> 編輯</button>
                  <button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(t)} style={{ flex:1, ...S.btn(T.red,true), justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13 }}><Icon n="trash" s={13}/> 刪除</button>
                </div>}
              </div>}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
      {showForm&&<Modal title={editT?`編輯「${editT.name}」`:"新增房客"} onClose={()=>{setShowForm(false);setEditT(null);}}>
        <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.blue, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:10, letterSpacing:"0.06em" }}>基本資料</div>
        {[["name","姓名 *","text"],["phone","電話","text"],["email","Email","email"],["idNo","身份證號","text"]].map(([k,l,tp])=><div key={k}><label style={S.label}>{l}</label><input style={S.input} type={tp} value={form[k]} onChange={sf(k)}/></div>)}
        <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.blue, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:10, marginTop:4, letterSpacing:"0.06em" }}>租約資訊</div>
        <label style={S.label}>分配房間</label>
        <select style={S.input} value={form.roomId} onChange={sf("roomId")}><option value="">— 選擇房間 —</option>{rooms.filter(r=>r.status==="vacant"||r.id===editT?.roomId).map(r=><option key={r.id} value={r.id}>{r.communityName} {r.id===editT?.roomId?"（目前）":`(${fmt(r.rent)}/月)`}</option>)}</select>
        {[["moveIn","入住日","date"],["contractEnd","合約到期","date"],["deposit","押金金額","number"]].map(([k,l,tp])=><div key={k}><label style={S.label}>{l}</label><input style={S.input} type={tp} value={form[k]} onChange={sf(k)}/></div>)}
        <label style={S.label}>備註</label>
        <textarea style={{ ...S.input, height:68, resize:"vertical" }} value={form.note} onChange={sf("note")} placeholder="特殊注意事項..."/>
        <button onClick={saveTenant} style={{ ...S.btn(), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", padding:11, marginTop:4 }}>{editT?"儲存修改":"確認新增"}</button>
      </Modal>}
      {confirmDel&&<Modal title="確認刪除房客" onClose={()=>setConfirmDel(null)} width={360}><div style={{ textAlign:"center", padding:"8px 0 16px" }}><div style={{ color:T.text, fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:8 }}>刪除「{confirmDel.name}」？</div><div style={{ color:T.textSub, fontSize:14, lineHeight:1.6, marginBottom:20 }}>對應房間將自動設為空房。</div><div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}><button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(null)} style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button><button onClick={()=>delTenant(confirmDel)} style={{ flex:1, background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>確認刪除</button></div></div></Modal>}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  BILLS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function Bills({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const { bills, tenants, rooms } = data;
  const role = safeRole(currentUser.role);
  const isTenant = currentUser.role==="viewer";
  const tenantRoomId = isTenant?(currentUser._roomId||""):"";
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState("all");
  const [monthFilter, setMonthFilter] = useState(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7));
  const [viewProof, setViewProof] = useState(null);
  const proofRefs = useRef({});
  const thisMonth = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);

  const shown = (bills||[]).filter(b=>isTenant?b.roomId===tenantRoomId:true).filter(b=>!monthFilter||b.month===monthFilter).filter(b=>filter==="all"?true:b.status===filter);
  const shownPaid = shown.filter(b=>b.status==="paid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0);
  const shownUnpaid = shown.filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0);
  const missingCnt = rooms.filter(r=>r.status==="rented"&&!(bills||[]).find(b=>b.roomId===r.id&&b.month===thisMonth)).length;
  const allMonths = [...new Set((bills||[]).map(b=>b.month))].sort().reverse();
  if (!allMonths.includes(thisMonth)) allMonths.unshift(thisMonth);

  if (!role.canViewFinance&&!isTenant) return <div style={{ textAlign:"center", padding:60, color:T.textSub }}><Icon n="lock" s={40}/><div style={{ marginTop:12, fontSize:14 }}>您的權限不足以查看財務資料</div></div>;

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:14 }}>
        <h2 style={{ ...S.title, marginBottom:0 }}>{isTenant?"我的帳單":"帳務管理"}</h2>
        {role.canEdit&&missingCnt>0&&<button onClick={()=>onUpdate(d=>{ let nb=[...d.bills]; d.rooms.filter(r=>r.status==="rented").forEach(r=>{ if(!nb.find(b=>b.roomId===r.id&&b.month===thisMonth)){const t=d.tenants.find(t=>(t.linkedRoom===r.id||t.roomId===r.id)&&!t.isCohabitant); nb=[...nb,{id:uid(),tenantId:t?.id||r.tenantId||"",roomId:r.id,type:"rent",amount:r.rent,month:thisMonth,status:"unpaid",paidDate:null,recordedBy:null}];} }); return{...d,bills:nb,activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`產生 ${thisMonth} 月所有房源帳單`,timestamp:nowISO()}]};})} style={{ ...S.btn(T.accent), fontSize:13 }}><Icon n="plus" s={13}/> 產生本月帳單（{missingCnt}間）</button>}
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, marginBottom:12, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
        <select value={monthFilter} onChange={e=>setMonthFilter(e.target.value)} style={{ background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.borderMd}`, borderRadius:7, color:T.text, padding:"6px 10px", fontSize:13, outline:"none", cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
          <option value="">全部月份</option>{allMonths.map(m=><option key={m} value={m}>{toROCMonth(m)}</option>)}
        </select>
        {[["all","全部"],["unpaid","未繳"],["paid","已繳"]].map(([v,l])=><button key={v} onClick={()=>setFilter(v)} style={{ background:filter===v?T.accent:T.bgMuted, color:filter===v?"#fff":T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${filter===v?T.accent:T.border}`, borderRadius:7, padding:"6px 14px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>{l}</button>)}
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:10, marginBottom:14 }}>
        <div style={{ ...S.card, borderColor:T.green+"44" }}><div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700 }}>已收款</div><div style={{ fontSize:20, fontWeight:800, color:T.green, marginTop:6 }}>{fmt(shownPaid)}</div></div>
        <div style={{ ...S.card, borderColor:T.red+"44" }}><div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700 }}>未收款</div><div style={{ fontSize:20, fontWeight:800, color:T.red, marginTop:6 }}>{fmt(shownUnpaid)}</div></div>
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:8 }}>
        {shown.length===0&&<div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textSub, padding:"32px 0", fontSize:14 }}>此條件下無帳單記錄</div>}
        {shown.sort((a,b)=>(a.status==="unpaid"?-1:1)-(b.status==="unpaid"?-1:1)).map(b=>{
          const t=(tenants||[]).find(x=>x.id===b.tenantId);
          const r=rooms.find(x=>x.id===b.roomId);
          const rec=(data.users||[]).find(u=>u.id===b.recordedBy);
          const over=b.status==="unpaid"&&b.month<thisMonth;
          return (
            <div key={b.id} style={{ ...S.card, border:`1px solid ${over?T.red+"66":(b.status==="unpaid"?T.amber+"66":T.border)}` }}>
              <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"flex-start" }}>
                <div style={{ flex:1, minWidth:0 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{r?.communityName||"—"}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, marginTop:2 }}>{isTenant?"":(t?.name||"—")+" · "}{toROCMonth(b.month)} · {SL[b.type]}</div>
                  {rec&&b.status==="paid"&&<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2 }}>由 {rec.name} 記錄</div>}
                  {over&&<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.red, fontWeight:700, marginTop:2 }}>⚠️ 逾期未繳</div>}
                </div>
                <div style={{ textAlign:"right", flexShrink:0, marginLeft:12 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:b.status==="paid"?T.green:(over?T.red:T.amber), fontSize:15 }}>{fmt(b.amount)}</div>
                  {b.status==="unpaid"&&role.canEdit?<button onClick={()=>onUpdate(d=>({...d,bills:d.bills.map(x=>x.id===b.id?{...x,status:"paid",paidDate:todayStr(),recordedBy:currentUser.id}:x),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`標記「${r?.communityName||b.roomId}」款項已繳`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}))} style={{ background:T.greenBg, color:T.green, border:`1px solid ${T.green}44`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:13, cursor:"pointer", marginTop:4, fontWeight:600, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>標記已收</button>:b.paidDate?<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:4 }}>{toROC(b.paidDate)}</div>:null}
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ marginTop:10, borderTop:`1px solid ${T.border}`, paddingTop:10 }}>
                {b.paymentProof?<div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap" }}><button onClick={()=>setViewProof(b.paymentProof)} style={{ background:T.greenBg, color:T.green, border:`1px solid ${T.green}44`, borderRadius:7, padding:"5px 12px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>📷 查看截圖</button></div>:null}
                {isTenant&&<div style={{ display:"flex", gap:6, marginTop:b.paymentProof?8:0, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                  <label htmlFor={`proof-cam-${b.id}`} style={{ background:T.accentBg, color:T.accent, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}44`, borderRadius:7, padding:"6px 10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer" }}>📷 拍照</label>
                  <label htmlFor={`proof-pic-${b.id}`} style={{ background:"#d1fae5", color:"#065f46", border:"1px solid #6ee7b755", borderRadius:7, padding:"6px 10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer" }}>🖼 相簿</label>
                  <label htmlFor={`proof-file-${b.id}`} style={{ background:"#e0e7ff", color:"#4338ca", border:"1px solid #a5b4fc55", borderRadius:7, padding:"6px 10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer" }}>📎 檔案</label>
                </div>}
                {!isTenant && !b.paymentProof && <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted }}>尚未上傳截圖</div>}
                {isTenant&&<>
                  <input id={`proof-cam-${b.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={e=>{ const fs=Array.from(e.target.files||[]); if(!fs.length)return; fs.forEach(f=>{const rd=new FileReader(); rd.onload=ev=>onUpdate(d=>({...d,bills:d.bills.map(x=>x.id===b.id?{...x,paymentProof:ev.target.result,paymentProofs:[...(x.paymentProofs||[]),{id:uid(),dataUrl:ev.target.result,fileName:f.name,uploadedAt:nowISO()}]}:x)})); rd.readAsDataURL(f);}); e.target.value=""; }}/>
                  <input id={`proof-pic-${b.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={e=>{ const fs=Array.from(e.target.files||[]); if(!fs.length)return; fs.forEach(f=>{const rd=new FileReader(); rd.onload=ev=>onUpdate(d=>({...d,bills:d.bills.map(x=>x.id===b.id?{...x,paymentProof:ev.target.result,paymentProofs:[...(x.paymentProofs||[]),{id:uid(),dataUrl:ev.target.result,fileName:f.name,uploadedAt:nowISO()}]}:x)})); rd.readAsDataURL(f);}); e.target.value=""; }}/>
                  <input id={`proof-file-${b.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf,*/*" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={e=>{ const fs=Array.from(e.target.files||[]); if(!fs.length)return; fs.forEach(f=>{const rd=new FileReader(); rd.onload=ev=>onUpdate(d=>({...d,bills:d.bills.map(x=>x.id===b.id?{...x,paymentProof:ev.target.result,paymentProofs:[...(x.paymentProofs||[]),{id:uid(),dataUrl:ev.target.result,fileName:f.name,uploadedAt:nowISO()}]}:x)})); rd.readAsDataURL(f);}); e.target.value=""; }}/>
                </>}
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
      {viewProof&&<div onClick={()=>setViewProof(null)} style={{ position:"fixed", inset:0, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.8)", zIndex:2000, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:16 }}><img src={viewProof} style={{ maxWidth:"90vw", maxHeight:"85vh", borderRadius:10, objectFit:"contain" }} alt="截圖"/></div>}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  REPAIRS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function Repairs({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const { repairs, rooms, users } = data;
  const role    = safeRole(currentUser.role);
  const isTenant = currentUser.role==="viewer";
  const tenantRoomId = isTenant?(currentUser._roomId||""):"";
  const mkEmpty = () => ({roomId:tenantRoomId,title:"",desc:"",priority:"high",photos:[]});
  const [showAdd, setShowAdd]       = useState(false);
  const [form, setForm]             = useState(mkEmpty);
  const [viewPhoto, setViewPhoto]   = useState(null);
  // 修繕照片面板：repairId → { open, note, photos, lineStatus }
  const [repairPanels, setRepairPanels] = useState({});
  const photoRef    = useRef(null);
  const SC = { done:T.green, in_progress:T.blue, pending:T.amber };
  const PC = { high:T.red, low:T.textMuted };
  const visible = isTenant?(repairs||[]).filter(r=>r.roomId===tenantRoomId):(repairs||[]);

  const getPanel = (id) => repairPanels[id] || { open:false, note:"", photos:[], lineStatus:null };
  const setPanel = (id, patch) => setRepairPanels(p=>({ ...p, [id]:{ ...getPanel(id), ...patch } }));

  const addRepair = () => {
    if(!form.title||!form.roomId) return;
    const r=rooms.find(x=>x.id===form.roomId);
    onUpdate(d=>({...d,repairs:[...d.repairs,{id:uid(),...form,status:"pending",date:todayStr(),tenantName:currentUser.name||"—",assignedTo:null,updatedBy:null,photos:form.photos||[],completionPhotos:[],completionNote:""}],activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`新增報修「${form.title}」(${r?.communityName||""})`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}));
    setShowAdd(false); setForm(mkEmpty());
  };

  // ── 儲存修繕照片 ──────────────────────────────────────
  const saveCompletionPhotos = (repId) => {
    const panel = getPanel(repId);
    onUpdate(d=>({
      ...d,
      repairs: d.repairs.map(x => x.id===repId
        ? { ...x, completionPhotos:[...(x.completionPhotos||[]),...panel.photos], completionNote:panel.note, updatedBy:currentUser.id }
        : x),
      activityLog: [...d.activityLog, { id:uid(), userId:currentUser.id, action:`上傳「${d.repairs.find(x=>x.id===repId)?.title||repId}」修繕照片（${panel.photos.length}張）`, timestamp:nowISO() }]
    }));
    setPanel(repId, { photos:[], note:"" });
  };

  // ── LINE 分享發送（修繕完成通知）──────────────────────────────────
  const sendLINE = (rep) => {
    const rm = rooms.find(x=>x.id===rep.roomId);
    const note = getPanel(rep.id).note || rep.completionNote || "";
    const msg = `🔧 修繕完成通知\n\n房源：${rm?.communityName||""}${rm?.address?" ("+rm.address+")":""}\n報修項目：${rep.title}\n${note?"修繕說明："+note+"\n":""}完成日期：${toROC(todayStr())}\n\n如有問題請聯絡管理員，謝謝。\n— 家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司`;
    openLineShare(msg);
    setPanel(rep.id, { lineStatus:"ok" });
    onUpdate(d=>({ ...d, activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{ id:uid(), userId:currentUser.id, action:`LINE 通知「${rep.title}」修繕完成 → 已開啟分享`, timestamp:nowISO() }] }));
  };

  const lineLabel = (s) => s==="ok" ? { text:"✅ 已開啟LINE", color:T.green } : null;

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:16 }}>
        <h2 style={S.title}>報修管理</h2>
        {(role.canEdit||isTenant)&&<button onClick={()=>{setForm(mkEmpty());setShowAdd(true);}} style={S.btn()}><Icon n="plus" s={13}/> 新增報修</button>}
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10 }}>
        {visible.length===0&&<div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textSub, padding:"32px 0", fontSize:14 }}>目前沒有報修記錄</div>}
        {visible.map(rep=>{
          const rm  = rooms.find(x=>x.id===rep.roomId);
          const up  = (users||[]).find(u=>u.id===rep.updatedBy);
          const panel = getPanel(rep.id);

          const ll = lineLabel(panel.lineStatus, panel.lineErr);
          return (
            <div key={rep.id} style={{ ...S.card, borderColor:rep.status==="done"?T.green+"44":T.border }}>
              {/* ── 標題列 ── */}
              <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:8 }}>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8 }}>
                  <div style={{ width:7, height:7, borderRadius:"50%", background:PC[rep.priority]||T.textMuted, flexShrink:0 }}/>
                  <span style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{rep.title}</span>
                </div>
                <span style={S.tag(SC[rep.status]||T.textSub)}>{SL[rep.status]}</span>
              </div>
              <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, marginBottom:4 }}>{rm?.communityName} · {rep.tenantName} · {toROC(rep.date)}</div>
              {rep.desc&&<div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textMuted, marginBottom:8 }}>{rep.desc}</div>}

              {/* ── 報修原始照片（租客上傳）── */}
              {(rep.photos||[]).length>0&&(
                <div style={{ marginBottom:10 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600, marginBottom:6 }}>📷 報修照片</div>
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                    {rep.photos.map((src,i)=><div key={i} onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(src)} style={{ width:72, height:72, borderRadius:8, overflow:"hidden", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, cursor:"pointer", flexShrink:0 }}><img src={src} alt={`報修圖${i+1}`} style={{ width:"100%", height:"100%", objectFit:"cover" }}/></div>)}
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* ── 修繕完成照片（已儲存）── */}
              {(rep.completionPhotos||[]).length>0&&(
                <div style={{ marginBottom:10, background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:9, padding:"10px 12px" }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.green, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:6 }}>🔧 修繕後照片</div>
                  {rep.completionNote&&<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, marginBottom:8 }}>說明：{rep.completionNote}</div>}
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                    {rep.completionPhotos.map((src,i)=><div key={i} onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(src)} style={{ width:72, height:72, borderRadius:8, overflow:"hidden", border:`1px solid ${T.green}44`, cursor:"pointer", flexShrink:0 }}><img src={src} alt={`修繕圖${i+1}`} style={{ width:"100%", height:"100%", objectFit:"cover" }}/></div>)}
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {up&&<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginBottom:8 }}>由 {up.name} 更新</div>}

              {/* ── 管理員動作按鈕 ── */}
              {role.canEdit&&(
                <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap", marginBottom:10 }}>
                  {rep.status==="pending"&&(
                    <button type="button" onClick={()=>onUpdate(d=>({...d,repairs:d.repairs.map(x=>x.id===rep.id?{...x,status:"in_progress",updatedBy:currentUser.id}:x),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`更新報修「${rep.title}」為處理中`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}))} style={S.btn(T.blue,true)}>開始處理</button>
                  )}
                  {rep.status!=="done"&&(
                    <button type="button" onClick={()=>onUpdate(d=>({...d,repairs:d.repairs.map(x=>x.id===rep.id?{...x,status:"done",updatedBy:currentUser.id}:x),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`更新報修「${rep.title}」為已完成`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}))} style={S.btn(T.green,true)}>完成</button>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}

              {/* ── 修繕紀錄上傳區（常駐，管理員以上可編輯；所有角色可檢視已儲存照片）── */}
              {role.canEdit && (
                <div style={{ background:T.bgSub, border:`1.5px solid ${T.accent}33`, borderRadius:10, padding:"12px 14px", marginTop:4 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, marginBottom:10 }}>🔧 新增修繕紀錄（照片 + 說明）</div>

                  <label style={S.label}>修繕說明</label>
                  <textarea style={{ ...S.input, height:64, resize:"vertical", fontSize:13 }}
                    value={panel.note} placeholder="例：已更換馬桶零件、水管重新固定…"
                    onChange={e=>setPanel(rep.id,{note:e.target.value})}/>

                  <label style={S.label}>修繕後照片（可多張）</label>
                  {(() => {
                    const onRep = e => {
                      const files = Array.from(e.target.files||[]);
                      if (files.length===0) return;
                      Promise.all(files.map(f => new Promise(res => {
                        const r = new FileReader();
                        r.onload = ev => res(ev.target.result);
                        r.readAsDataURL(f);
                      }))).then(urls => {
                        setPanel(rep.id, { photos:[...getPanel(rep.id).photos, ...urls] });
                      });
                      e.target.value="";
                    };
                    return <>
                      <input id={`rep-cam-${rep.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={onRep}/>
                      <input id={`rep-pic-${rep.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={onRep}/>
                      <input id={`rep-file-${rep.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf,*/*" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={onRep}/>
                    </>;
                  })()}
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:6, marginBottom:10 }}>
                    <label htmlFor={`rep-cam-${rep.id}`} style={{ flex:1, background:T.accentBg, color:T.accent, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}66`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📷 拍照</label>
                    <label htmlFor={`rep-pic-${rep.id}`} style={{ flex:1, background:"#d1fae5", color:"#065f46", border:"1px solid #6ee7b755", borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>🖼 相簿</label>
                    <label htmlFor={`rep-file-${rep.id}`} style={{ flex:1, background:"#e0e7ff", color:"#4338ca", border:"1px solid #a5b4fc55", borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📎 檔案</label>
                  </div>
                  {panel.photos.length>0&&(
                    <>
                      <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, marginBottom:6 }}>待儲存：共 {panel.photos.length} 張</div>
                      <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap", marginBottom:10 }}>
                        {panel.photos.map((src,i)=>(
                          <div key={i} style={{ position:"relative", width:68, height:68, borderRadius:8, overflow:"hidden", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, flexShrink:0 }}>
                            <img src={src} alt="" style={{ width:"100%", height:"100%", objectFit:"cover", cursor:"pointer" }} onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(src)}/>
                            <button type="button" onClick={()=>setPanel(rep.id,{photos:panel.photos.filter((_,j)=>j!==i)})}
                              style={{ position:"absolute", top:2, right:2, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.6)", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:"50%", width:18, height:18, fontSize:11, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:0, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>✕</button>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </>
                  )}

                  <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                    <button type="button" onClick={()=>saveCompletionPhotos(rep.id)} disabled={panel.photos.length===0&&!panel.note}
                      style={{ ...S.btn(T.accent), flex:1, justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13, opacity:(panel.photos.length===0&&!panel.note)?0.5:1, cursor:(panel.photos.length===0&&!panel.note)?"not-allowed":"pointer" }}>
                      💾 儲存修繕紀錄
                    </button>
                    <button type="button" onClick={()=>sendLINE(rep)}
                      style={{ ...S.btn("#22c55e"), flex:1, justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13 }}>
                      💚 分享到 LINE 通知租客
                    </button>
                  </div>
                  {ll&&<div style={{ marginTop:8, fontSize:13, color:ll.color, fontWeight:600 }}>{ll.text}</div>}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
      {viewPhoto&&<div onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(null)} style={{ position:"fixed", inset:0, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.82)", zIndex:3000, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:16, cursor:"zoom-out" }}><img src={viewPhoto} alt="放大" style={{ maxWidth:"92vw", maxHeight:"88vh", borderRadius:10, objectFit:"contain" }}/></div>}
      {showAdd&&<Modal title="新增報修" onClose={()=>{setShowAdd(false);setForm(mkEmpty());}}>
        <label style={S.label}>房間</label>
        {isTenant?<div style={{ ...S.input, color:T.textSub, background:T.bgMuted, marginBottom:12 }}>{rooms.find(r=>r.id===tenantRoomId)?.communityName||"我的房間"}</div>:<select style={S.input} value={form.roomId} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,roomId:e.target.value}))}><option value="">— 選擇房間 —</option>{rooms.map(r=><option key={r.id} value={r.id}>{r.communityName}</option>)}</select>}
        <label style={S.label}>問題標題 *</label><input style={S.input} value={form.title} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,title:e.target.value}))} placeholder="例：廁所漏水、冷氣不製冷"/>
        <label style={S.label}>問題描述</label><textarea style={{ ...S.input, height:80, resize:"vertical" }} value={form.desc} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,desc:e.target.value}))} placeholder="請描述問題狀況..."/>
        <label style={S.label}>現場照片（選填，可多張）</label>
        {(() => {
          const onNew = e => { Array.from(e.target.files||[]).forEach(file=>{ const r=new FileReader(); r.onload=ev=>setForm(prev=>({...prev,photos:[...(prev.photos||[]),ev.target.result]})); r.readAsDataURL(file); }); e.target.value=""; };
          return <>
            <input id="rn-cam" type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={onNew}/>
            <input id="rn-pic" type="file" accept="image/*" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={onNew}/>
            <input id="rn-file" type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf,*/*" multiple style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={onNew}/>
          </>;
        })()}
        <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:6, marginBottom:12 }}>
          <label htmlFor="rn-cam" style={{ flex:1, background:T.accentBg, color:T.accent, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}66`, borderRadius:8, padding:"12px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📷 拍照</label>
          <label htmlFor="rn-pic" style={{ flex:1, background:"#d1fae5", color:"#065f46", border:"1px solid #6ee7b755", borderRadius:8, padding:"12px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>🖼 相簿</label>
          <label htmlFor="rn-file" style={{ flex:1, background:"#e0e7ff", color:"#4338ca", border:"1px solid #a5b4fc55", borderRadius:8, padding:"12px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"center" }}>📎 檔案</label>
        </div>
        {(form.photos||[]).length>0&&<div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap", marginBottom:14 }}>{form.photos.map((src,i)=><div key={i} style={{ position:"relative", width:70, height:70, borderRadius:8, overflow:"hidden", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, flexShrink:0 }}><img src={src} alt={`圖${i+1}`} style={{ width:"100%", height:"100%", objectFit:"cover" }}/><button onClick={()=>setForm(f=>({...f,photos:f.photos.filter((_,j)=>j!==i)}))} style={{ position:"absolute", top:2, right:2, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.55)", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:"50%", width:18, height:18, fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:0, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>✕</button></div>)}</div>}
        {!isTenant&&<><label style={S.label}>優先級</label><select style={S.input} value={form.priority} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,priority:e.target.value}))}><option value="high">高（緊急）</option><option value="low">低（一般）</option></select></>}
        <button onClick={addRepair} disabled={!form.title||!form.roomId} style={{ ...S.btn(), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", padding:12, opacity:(!form.title||!form.roomId)?0.5:1 }}>送出報修申請</button>
      </Modal>}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  REPORT
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function Report({ bills, rooms, tenants }) {
  const thisYear = new Date().getFullYear();
  const [yr, setYr] = useState(thisYear);
  const [mode, setMode] = useState("monthly");

  const monthly = Array.from({length:12},(_,i)=>{
    const m=`${yr}-${String(i+1).padStart(2,"0")}`;
    const mb=(bills||[]).filter(b=>b.month===m);
    const coll=mb.filter(b=>b.status==="paid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0);
    const uncoll=mb.filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0);
    return { m, roomCount:[...new Set(mb.map(b=>b.roomId))].length, coll, uncoll, total:coll+uncoll };
  });
  const yColl=(monthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.coll,0)), yUncoll=(monthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.uncoll,0));
  const maxT=Math.max(...monthly.map(m=>m.total),1);
  const rented=(rooms||[]).filter(r=>r.status==="rented");
  const occ=(rooms||[]).length>0?Math.round((rented.length/rooms.length)*100):0;
  const yrStr=String(yr);

  const billYears=[...new Set((bills||[]).map(b=>b.month?.slice(0,4)).filter(Boolean).map(Number))];
  const years=[...new Set([...billYears,thisYear-1,thisYear,thisYear+1])].sort((a,b)=>b-a);

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:16 }}>
        <div><h2 style={{ ...S.title, marginBottom:2 }}>房源報表</h2><p style={{ color:T.textSub, fontSize:13, margin:0 }}>民國 {yr-1911} 年</p></div>
        <select value={yr} onChange={e=>setYr(Number(e.target.value))} style={{ background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.borderMd}`, borderRadius:8, color:T.text, padding:"7px 10px", fontSize:13, outline:"none", cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>{years.map(y=><option key={y} value={y}>民國 {y-1911} 年</option>)}</select>
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:10, marginBottom:14 }}>
        {[{l:"目前出租",v:`${rented.length} 間`,sub:`入住率 ${occ}%`,c:T.green},{l:"空房",v:`${(rooms||[]).filter(r=>r.status==="vacant").length} 間`,sub:`共 ${(rooms||[]).length} 間`,c:T.amber},{l:`${yr-1911}年已收款`,v:fmt(yColl),sub:"全年合計",c:T.blue},{l:`${yr-1911}年未收款`,v:fmt(yUncoll),sub:"全年合計",c:T.red}].map((s,i)=>(
          <div key={i} style={S.card}><div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:4 }}>{s.l}</div><div style={{ fontSize:18, fontWeight:800, color:s.c }}>{s.v}</div><div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2 }}>{s.sub}</div></div>
        ))}
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, marginBottom:12, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
        {[["monthly","月份統計"],["rooms","房源明細"]].map(([k,l])=><button key={k} onClick={()=>setMode(k)} style={{ background:mode===k?T.accent:T.bgMuted, color:mode===k?"#fff":T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${mode===k?T.accent:T.border}`, borderRadius:7, padding:"6px 16px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>{l}</button>)}
      </div>
      {mode==="monthly"&&<div style={{ ...S.card, padding:0, overflow:"hidden" }}>
        <div style={{ padding:"14px 14px 6px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:10 }}>月收租走勢（民國 {yr-1911} 年）</div>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:4, alignItems:"flex-end", height:64 }}>
            {monthly.map((m,i)=>{ const h=maxT>0?Math.max(4,Math.round((m.total/maxT)*60)):4; const hp=maxT>0?Math.round((m.coll/maxT)*60):0; const cur=m.m===new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7); return <div key={i} style={{ flex:1, display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"center", gap:2 }}><div style={{ width:"100%", height:h, borderRadius:"4px 4px 0 0", position:"relative", background:T.bgMuted, overflow:"hidden" }}><div style={{ position:"absolute", bottom:0, width:"100%", height:hp, background:cur?T.blue:T.green+"bb", borderRadius:"4px 4px 0 0" }}/></div><div style={{ fontSize:10, color:cur?T.blue:T.textMuted, fontWeight:cur?700:400 }}>{i+1}月</div></div>; })}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style={{ overflowX:"auto" }}>
          <table style={{ width:"100%", borderCollapse:"collapse", fontSize:13 }}>
            <thead><tr style={{ background:T.bgSub }}>{["月份","出租間數","已收租金","未收租金","合計"].map(h=><th key={h} style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:h==="月份"?"left":"right", color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, fontSize:11, borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>{h}</th>)}</tr></thead>
            <tbody>{monthly.map((m,i)=>{ const cur=m.m===new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7); return <tr key={i} style={{ background:cur?T.accentBg:"transparent", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", color:cur?T.accent:T.text, fontWeight:cur?700:500 }}>{i+1} 月{cur&&<span style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.accent, marginLeft:4 }}>●本月</span>}</td><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.text, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.roomCount} 間</td><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:"right", color:m.coll>0?T.green:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.coll>0?fmt(m.coll):"—"}</td><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:"right", color:m.uncoll>0?T.red:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.uncoll>0?fmt(m.uncoll):"—"}</td><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.text, fontWeight:700 }}>{m.total>0?fmt(m.total):"—"}</td></tr>; })}</tbody>
            <tfoot><tr style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderTop:`2px solid ${T.borderMd}` }}><td style={{ padding:"10px", fontWeight:800, color:T.text }}>全年合計</td><td style={{ padding:"10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.textSub }}>—</td><td style={{ padding:"10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.green, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(yColl)}</td><td style={{ padding:"10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.red, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(yUncoll)}</td><td style={{ padding:"10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.accent, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(yColl+yUncoll)}</td></tr></tfoot>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>}
      {mode==="rooms"&&<div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:8 }}>{(rooms||[]).map(r=>{ const yb=(bills||[]).filter(b=>b.roomId===r.id&&b.month?.startsWith(yrStr)); const rc=yb.filter(b=>b.status==="paid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0); const ru=yb.filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0); return <div key={r.id} style={S.card}><div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"flex-start", marginBottom:8 }}><div><div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{r.communityName}</div>{r.address&&<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, marginTop:1 }}>📍 {r.address}</div>}</div><span style={S.tag(r.status==="rented"?T.green:T.amber)}>{r.status==="rented"?"已出租":"空房"}</span></div><div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr 1fr", gap:6 }}>{[["月租金",fmt(r.rent),T.text],[`${yr-1911}年已收`,fmt(rc),T.green],[`${yr-1911}年未收`,fmt(ru),T.red]].map(([l,v,c])=><div key={l} style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderRadius:7, padding:"7px 8px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}><div style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.textMuted, fontWeight:700 }}>{l}</div><div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:c, marginTop:2 }}>{v}</div></div>)}</div></div>; })}</div>}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  USER MANAGEMENT
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function UserManagement({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const [showAdd, setShowAdd] = useState(false);
  const [confirmDel, setConfirmDel] = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ name:"", email:"", password:"", role:"viewer" });
  const save = async () => {
    if(!form.name||!form.email) return;
    const rawPw = form.password || form.email;
    const hashedPw = await sha256(rawPw);
    const nu={id:uid(),...form,password:hashedPw,avatar:form.name[0],online:false,lastSeen:null};
    onUpdate(d=>({...d,users:[...d.users,nu],activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`新增使用者 ${form.name}`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}));
    setShowAdd(false); setForm({name:"",email:"",password:"",role:"viewer"});
  };
  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:16 }}>
        <h2 style={S.title}>人員管理</h2>
        <button onClick={()=>setShowAdd(true)} style={S.btn()}><Icon n="plus" s={13}/> 新增人員</button>
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10 }}>
        {(data.users||[]).map(u=>(
          <div key={u.id} style={{ ...S.card, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:12 }}>
            <AvatarBadge user={u} size={40}/>
            <div style={{ flex:1 }}><div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6 }}><span style={{ fontWeight:600, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{u.name}</span>{u.id===currentUser.id&&<span style={S.tag(T.blue)}>我</span>}</div><div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, marginTop:2 }}>{u.email}</div></div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"flex-end", gap:6 }}>
              <span style={S.tag(safeRole(u.role).color)}>{safeRole(u.role).label}</span>
              {u.id!==currentUser.id&&<>
                <select value={u.role} onChange={e=>onUpdate(d=>({...d,users:d.users.map(x=>x.id===u.id?{...x,role:e.target.value}:x),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`變更 ${u.name} 權限為 ${safeRole(e.target.value).label}`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}))} style={{ background:T.bg, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:6, padding:"3px 8px", fontSize:13, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>{Object.entries(ROLES).filter(([k])=>k!=="system"&&k!=="staff").map(([k,v])=><option key={k} value={k}>{v.label}</option>)}</select>
                <button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(u)} style={{ background:T.redBg, color:T.red, border:`1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:4, fontFamily:"inherit" }}><Icon n="trash" s={12}/> 刪除</button>
              </>}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
      {confirmDel&&<Modal title="確認刪除使用者" onClose={()=>setConfirmDel(null)} width={360}><div style={{ textAlign:"center", padding:"8px 0 16px" }}><div style={{ width:52, height:52, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.redBg, border:`2px solid ${T.red}44`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", margin:"0 auto 14px", color:T.red }}><Icon n="trash" s={22}/></div><div style={{ color:T.text, fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:8 }}>刪除「{confirmDel.name}」？</div><div style={{ color:T.textSub, fontSize:14, lineHeight:1.6, marginBottom:20 }}>此操作無法復原。</div><div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}><button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(null)} style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button><button onClick={()=>{onUpdate(d=>({...d,users:d.users.filter(x=>x.id!==confirmDel.id),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`刪除使用者 ${confirmDel.name}`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}));setConfirmDel(null);}} style={{ flex:1, background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>確認刪除</button></div></div></Modal>}
      {showAdd&&<Modal title="新增人員" onClose={()=>setShowAdd(false)}>{[["name","姓名"],["email","Email"],["password","密碼"]].map(([k,l])=><div key={k}><label style={S.label}>{l}</label><input style={S.input} type={k==="password"?"password":"text"} value={form[k]} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,[k]:e.target.value}))}/></div>)}<label style={S.label}>權限角色</label><select style={S.input} value={form.role} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,role:e.target.value}))}>{Object.entries(ROLES).filter(([k])=>k!=="system"&&k!=="staff").map(([k,v])=><option key={k} value={k}>{v.label}</option>)}</select><button onClick={save} style={{ ...S.btn(), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", padding:11 }}>確認新增</button></Modal>}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  ACTIVITY LOG
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function ActivityLog({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const { activityLog, users, bills, rooms, repairs } = data;
  const isSA    = isSARole(currentUser?.role);
  const isAdmin = currentUser?.role === "admin";
  const canExportLog = isSA || isAdmin;

  const thisYear = new Date().getFullYear();
  const [confirmClear,     setConfirmClear]     = useState(false);
  const [confirmExportLog, setConfirmExportLog] = useState(false);
  const [showPL,           setShowPL]           = useState(false);
  const [plYear,           setPlYear]           = useState(thisYear);
  const [pendingImport,    setPendingImport]    = useState(null); // { data, meta }
  const importFileRef                           = useRef(null);

  // ── 年度損益計算 ──────────────────────────────────────
  const plBillYears = [...new Set((bills||[]).map(b=>b.month?.slice(0,4)).filter(Boolean).map(Number))];
  const plYears = [...new Set([...plBillYears, thisYear-1, thisYear])].sort((a,b)=>b-a);

  const buildPLData = (yr) => {
    return Array.from({ length: 12 }, (_, i) => {
      const mo = `${yr}-${String(i+1).padStart(2,"0")}`;
      const mb = (bills||[]).filter(b => b.month === mo);
      const collected   = mb.filter(b=>b.status==="paid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0), 0);
      const uncollected = mb.filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0), 0);
      const expected    = collected + uncollected;
      const rate        = expected > 0 ? Math.round((collected/expected)*100) : null;
      const roomIds     = [...new Set(mb.map(b=>b.roomId))];
      const repairCnt   = (repairs||[]).filter(r => {
        const d = r.date||"";
        return d.startsWith(mo) && roomIds.includes(r.roomId);
      }).length;
      return { mo, roomCount: roomIds.length, expected, collected, uncollected, rate, repairCnt };
    });
  };

  const plMonthly = buildPLData(plYear);
  const plTotalExpected    = plMonthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.expected, 0);
  const plTotalCollected   = plMonthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.collected, 0);
  const plTotalUncollected = plMonthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.uncollected, 0);
  const plAvgRate          = plTotalExpected > 0 ? Math.round((plTotalCollected/plTotalExpected)*100) : null;

  // ── 匯出損益表 CSV ────────────────────────────────────
  const exportPLCSV = () => {
    const rocYr = plYear - 1911;
    const header = ["月份","出租間數","應收租金(NT$)","已收租金(NT$)","未收租金(NT$)","收租率(%)","報修筆數"];
    const rows = plMonthly.map((m, i) => [
      csvEsc(`${rocYr}年${i+1}月`), csvEsc(m.roomCount||0), csvEsc(m.expected), csvEsc(m.collected), csvEsc(m.uncollected),
      m.rate!=null?csvEsc(m.rate+"%"):csvEsc("—"), csvEsc(m.repairCnt),
    ]);
    const totalRow = [
      csvEsc("全年合計"), csvEsc("—"), csvEsc(plTotalExpected), csvEsc(plTotalCollected), csvEsc(plTotalUncollected),
      plAvgRate!=null?csvEsc(plAvgRate+"%"):csvEsc("—"), csvEsc(plMonthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.repairCnt,0)),
    ];
    const lines = [
      csvEsc(`家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司　民國 ${rocYr} 年度損益表`),
      csvEsc(`製表日期：${toROC(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10))}　製表人：${currentUser?.name||""}`),
      "",
      header.map(csvEsc).join(","),
      ...rows.map(r=>r.join(",")),
      totalRow.join(","),
    ];
    downloadCSV(`家樂美_${rocYr}年度損益表.csv`, "\uFEFF"+lines.join("\n"));
    onUpdate(d => ({
      ...d,
      activityLog: [...d.activityLog, { id:uid(), userId:currentUser?.id, action:`匯出民國 ${rocYr} 年度損益表 CSV`, timestamp:nowISO() }],
    }));
  };

  const exportLogCSV = () => {
    const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    const header = ["時間","操作人員","角色","操作內容"].map(csvEsc).join(",");
    const rows = [...(activityLog||[])]
      .sort((a,b)=>new Date(a.timestamp)-new Date(b.timestamp))
      .map(log => {
        const u = (users||[]).find(u=>u.id===log.userId);
        return [csvEsc(toROC(log.timestamp,true)), csvEsc(u?.name||"系統"), csvEsc(u?safeRole(u.role).label:"—"), csvEsc(log.action)].join(",");
      });
    downloadCSV(`家樂美_操作記錄_${today}.csv`, "\uFEFF"+[header,...rows].join("\n"));
    onUpdate(d=>({...d, activityLog:[{ id:uid(), userId:currentUser?.id, action:`匯出操作記錄 CSV（共 ${(activityLog||[]).length} 筆），並清空記錄`, timestamp:new Date().toISOString() }]}));
    setConfirmExportLog(false);
  };

  // ── 匯入系統備份（JSON）────────────────────────────────
  const handleImportFile = (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    e.target.value = "";
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (ev) => {
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(ev.target.result);
        if (!parsed._rentkeeper || !Array.isArray(parsed.users) || !Array.isArray(parsed.rooms)) {
          showToast("檔案格式不正確，非 RentKeeper 備份檔", "error");
          return;
        }
        setPendingImport({
          data: parsed,
          meta: {
            backupTime: parsed._backupTime || "未知",
            rooms: (parsed.rooms||[]).length,
            tenants: (parsed.tenants||[]).length,
            users: (parsed.users||[]).length,
            bills: (parsed.bills||[]).length,
            repairs: (parsed.repairs||[]).length,
            fileName: file.name,
          },
        });
      } catch (err) {
        showToast("無法解析備份檔："+err.message, "error");
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file, "utf-8");
  };

  const confirmImportBackup = () => {
    if (!pendingImport) return;
    const { _backupTime, _rentkeeper, ...clean } = pendingImport.data;
    onUpdate(() => ({
      ...clean,
      activityLog: [
        ...(clean.activityLog || []),
        { id: uid(), userId: currentUser?.id || "system",
          action: `匯入系統備份還原資料（${pendingImport.meta.fileName}，備份時間：${pendingImport.meta.backupTime.slice(0,19).replace("T"," ")}）`,
          timestamp: nowISO() },
      ],
    }));
    setPendingImport(null);
    showToast("已還原備份資料！", "success");
  };

  // ── 匯出系統備份（JSON）────────────────────────────────
  const exportBackup = () => {
    const ts   = new Date().toISOString();
    const snap = { ...data, _backupTime: ts, _rentkeeper: true };
    const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(snap, null, 2)], { type: "application/json" });
    const url  = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a    = document.createElement("a");
    a.href     = url;
    a.download = `RentKeeper_備份_${ts.slice(0, 10)}.json`;
    document.body.appendChild(a); a.click();
    document.body.removeChild(a); URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    onUpdate(d => ({
      ...d,
      activityLog: [...d.activityLog, {
        id: uid(), userId: currentUser?.id || "system",
        action: "手動匯出系統備份檔案",
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      }],
    }));
  };

  const logCount = (activityLog || []).length;

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:16 }}>
        <h2 style={{ ...S.title, marginBottom:0 }}>操作記錄</h2>
        <span style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub }}>共 <strong style={{ color:T.text }}>{logCount}</strong> 筆</span>
      </div>

      {/* ── 操作按鈕區 ── */}
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10, marginBottom:20 }}>

        {/* 年度損益表 + 一鍵匯出記錄（管理員 + 後台維修） */}
        {canExportLog && (
          <button onClick={()=>setShowPL(true)}
            style={{ width:"100%", background:"#7c3aed", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:12, padding:"13px 16px", fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:8, fontFamily:"inherit", boxShadow:"0 4px 12px #7c3aed44" }}>
            📊 匯出年度損益表
          </button>
        )}
        {canExportLog && (
          <button onClick={()=>setConfirmExportLog(true)}
            style={{ width:"100%", background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:12, padding:"13px 16px", fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:8, fontFamily:"inherit", boxShadow:`0 4px 12px ${T.green}44` }}>
            📋 一鍵匯出操作記錄（CSV）
          </button>
        )}

        {/* 備份 / 還原 / 清空（僅後台維修） */}
        {isSA && (
          <>
            <div style={{ background:T.accentBg, border:`1.5px solid ${T.accent}44`, borderRadius:10, padding:"10px 12px", marginBottom:2, fontSize:12, color:T.text, lineHeight:1.6 }}>
              <div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, marginBottom:4 }}>💾 資料備份建議</div>
              建議每次新增大量房源後，點「⬇ 匯出系統備份」下載 JSON 檔；若遇到資料消失（清快取、換裝置、空間不足），可點「⬆ 匯入備份」一鍵還原。
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}>
              <button onClick={exportBackup}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.accent, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:10, padding:"11px 8px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:6, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                ⬇ 匯出系統備份
              </button>
              <input ref={importFileRef} type="file" accept=".json,application/json" style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={handleImportFile}/>
              <button onClick={()=>importFileRef.current?.click()}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:10, padding:"11px 8px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:6, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                ⬆ 匯入備份
              </button>
              <button onClick={()=>setConfirmClear(true)}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.bg, color:T.red, border:`1px solid ${T.red}44`, borderRadius:10, padding:"11px 8px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:6, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                🗑 清空記錄
              </button>
            </div>
          </>
        )}

        {/* 權限說明 */}
        {!canExportLog && (
          <div style={{ ...S.card, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, padding:"12px 16px" }}>
            <Icon n="lock" s={16}/>
            <span style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub }}>您的身份無法匯出或清空記錄</span>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* ── 年度損益表 Modal ── */}
      {showPL && (
        <Modal title="年度損益表" onClose={()=>setShowPL(false)} width={600}>
          <div style={{ paddingBottom:8 }}>
            {/* 年份選擇器 */}
            <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:14 }}>
              <div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700 }}>家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2 }}>製表日期：{toROC(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10))}</div>
              </div>
              <select value={plYear} onChange={e=>setPlYear(Number(e.target.value))}
                style={{ background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.borderMd}`, borderRadius:8, color:T.text, padding:"6px 10px", fontSize:13, outline:"none", cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                {plYears.map(y=><option key={y} value={y}>民國 {y-1911} 年</option>)}
              </select>
            </div>

            {/* 統計卡片 */}
            <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:8, marginBottom:14 }}>
              {[
                { l:"全年應收租金",   v:fmt(plTotalExpected),    c:"#7c3aed", sub:"已收＋未收合計" },
                { l:"全年已收租金",   v:fmt(plTotalCollected),   c:T.green,   sub:`佔應收 ${plAvgRate!=null?plAvgRate+"%" : "—"}` },
                { l:"全年未收租金",   v:fmt(plTotalUncollected), c:T.red,     sub:"尚未繳清款項" },
                { l:"全年收租率",     v:plAvgRate!=null?`${plAvgRate}%`:"—", c:plAvgRate>=90?T.green:plAvgRate>=70?T.amber:T.red, sub:"按已收/應收計算" },
              ].map((s,i)=>(
                <div key={i} style={{ background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:10, padding:"11px 12px" }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700 }}>{s.l}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:17, fontWeight:800, color:s.c, margin:"4px 0 2px" }}>{s.v}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted }}>{s.sub}</div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            {/* 月份明細表 */}
            <div style={{ overflowX:"auto", borderRadius:8, border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
              <table style={{ width:"100%", borderCollapse:"collapse", fontSize:12 }}>
                <thead>
                  <tr style={{ background:T.bgSub }}>
                    {["月份","間數","應收","已收","未收","收租率"].map(h=>(
                      <th key={h} style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:h==="月份"?"left":"right", color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, fontSize:11, borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>{h}</th>
                    ))}
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                  {plMonthly.map((m,i)=>{
                    const isCur = m.mo === new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);
                    const hasData = m.expected > 0;
                    return (
                      <tr key={i} style={{ background:isCur?T.accentBg:"transparent", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", color:isCur?T.accent:T.text, fontWeight:isCur?700:500, whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>
                          {i+1} 月{isCur&&<span style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.accent, marginLeft:4 }}>●</span>}
                        </td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:hasData?T.text:T.textMuted }}>{hasData?`${m.roomCount} 間`:"—"}</td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:hasData?T.text:T.textMuted, fontWeight:500 }}>{hasData?fmt(m.expected):"—"}</td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:m.collected>0?T.green:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.collected>0?fmt(m.collected):"—"}</td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:m.uncollected>0?T.red:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.uncollected>0?fmt(m.uncollected):"—"}</td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right" }}>
                          {m.rate!=null
                            ? <span style={{ color:m.rate>=90?T.green:m.rate>=70?T.amber:T.red, fontWeight:700 }}>{m.rate}%</span>
                            : <span style={{ color:T.textMuted }}>—</span>
                          }
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    );
                  })}
                </tbody>
                <tfoot>
                  <tr style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderTop:`2px solid ${T.borderMd}` }}>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", fontWeight:800, color:T.text }}>全年合計</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:T.textMuted }}>—</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:T.text, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(plTotalExpected)}</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:T.green, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(plTotalCollected)}</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:T.red, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(plTotalUncollected)}</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:plAvgRate>=90?T.green:plAvgRate>=70?T.amber:T.red, fontWeight:800 }}>
                      {plAvgRate!=null?`${plAvgRate}%`:"—"}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                </tfoot>
              </table>
            </div>

            {/* 備註 */}
            <div style={{ marginTop:10, padding:"8px 12px", background:T.bgMuted, borderRadius:8, fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, lineHeight:1.6 }}>
              ⚠️ 備註：本損益表以帳單紀錄計算，應收 = 已收 ＋ 未收，收租率 = 已收 ÷ 應收。匯出為 CSV 可直接用 Excel 開啟。
            </div>

            {/* 匯出按鈕 */}
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10, marginTop:14 }}>
              <button onClick={()=>setShowPL(false)}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                關閉
              </button>
              <button onClick={exportPLCSV}
                style={{ flex:2, background:"#7c3aed", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:6 }}>
                ⬇ 下載 CSV（可用 Excel 開啟）
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      )}

      {/* ── 確認匯出記錄對話框 ── */}
      {confirmExportLog && (
        <Modal title="確認匯出並清空記錄" onClose={()=>setConfirmExportLog(false)} width={360}>
          <div style={{ padding:"4px 0 16px" }}>
            <div style={{ background:T.accentBg, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}33`, borderRadius:10, padding:"14px", marginBottom:14 }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, marginBottom:6 }}>📋 匯出操作記錄</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, lineHeight:1.7 }}>
                將匯出 <strong style={{ color:T.text }}>{logCount} 筆</strong> 記錄為 CSV 檔案，<br/>
                可直接用 Excel 開啟。<br/>
                <span style={{ color:T.amber, fontWeight:600 }}>匯出完成後記錄將自動清空。</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}>
              <button onClick={()=>setConfirmExportLog(false)}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                取消
              </button>
              <button onClick={exportLogCSV}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                確認匯出並清空
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      )}

      {/* ── 確認清空對話框 ── */}
      {confirmClear && (
        <Modal title="確認清空記錄" onClose={()=>setConfirmClear(false)} width={360}>
          <div style={{ padding:"4px 0 16px" }}>
