    isSARole(currentUser.role) ||
    (isViewer && rec.uploadedBy === currentUser.id);

  return (
    <div style={{ marginBottom: 12, border: `1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius: 10, overflow: "hidden" }}>
      {/* Header */}
      <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "space-between", padding: "10px 14px", background: T.bgSub, borderBottom: records.length > 0 ? `1px solid ${T.border}` : "none" }}>
        <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 7 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 14 }}>💳</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>匯款截圖記錄</span>
          {records.length > 0 && (
            <span style={{ background: T.accent, color: "#fff", fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, borderRadius: 99, padding: "1px 7px" }}>{records.length} 筆</span>
          )}
        </div>
        {/* 租客可上傳；管理員/後台也可以代為上傳 */}
        {(isViewer || currentUser.role === "admin" || isSARole(currentUser.role)) && (
          <button
            onClick={() => setShowUpload(v => !v)}
            style={{ background: showUpload ? T.bgMuted : T.accentBg, color: T.accent, border: `1px solid ${T.accent}44`, borderRadius: 7, padding: "4px 12px", fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>
            {showUpload ? "取消" : "＋ 上傳"}
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 上傳表單 */}
      {showUpload && (
        <div style={{ padding: "12px 14px", background: T.accentBg, borderBottom: `1px solid ${T.accent}22` }}>
          <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginBottom: 8, alignItems: "center" }}>
            <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
              <label style={{ ...S.label, marginBottom: 3 }}>匯款月份</label>
              <select
                value={selectedMonth}
                onChange={e => setSelectedMonth(e.target.value)}
                style={{ ...S.input, marginBottom: 0, fontSize: 13, padding: "7px 10px" }}>
                {monthOptions.map(m => (
                  <option key={m} value={m}>{toROCMonth(m)}</option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>
          <label style={{ ...S.label, marginBottom: 3 }}>備註（選填）</label>
          <input
            style={{ ...S.input, marginBottom: 8, fontSize: 13, padding: "7px 10px" }}
            value={noteInput}
            onChange={e => setNoteInput(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="例：4月租金 NT$16,000"
          />
          <input id={`pay-cam-${room.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*" capture="environment" multiple style={{ display: "none" }} onChange={handleFileChange}/>
          <input id={`pay-pic-${room.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*" multiple style={{ display: "none" }} onChange={handleFileChange}/>
          <input id={`pay-file-${room.id}`} type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf,*/*" multiple style={{ display: "none" }} onChange={handleFileChange}/>
          {uploading ? (
            <div style={{ width: "100%", background: T.accent, color: "#fff", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px", fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, textAlign: "center", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", justifyContent: "center", gap: 7 }}>
              <div style={{ width: 14, height: 14, borderRadius: "50%", border: "2px solid #fff4", borderTopColor: "#fff", animation: "spin 0.7s linear infinite" }}/> 上傳中...
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6 }}>
              <label htmlFor={`pay-cam-${room.id}`} style={{ flex: 1, background: T.accent, color: "#fff", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "center" }}>📷 拍照</label>
              <label htmlFor={`pay-pic-${room.id}`} style={{ flex: 1, background: "#10b981", color: "#fff", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "center" }}>🖼 相簿</label>
              <label htmlFor={`pay-file-${room.id}`} style={{ flex: 1, background: "#6366f1", color: "#fff", borderRadius: 8, padding: "10px", fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", textAlign: "center" }}>📎 檔案</label>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 記錄列表 */}
      {records.length === 0 ? (
        <div style={{ padding: "20px 14px", textAlign: "center", color: T.textMuted, fontSize: 13 }}>
          尚無匯款截圖記錄
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column" }}>
          {records.map((rec, idx) => (
            <div key={rec.id} style={{ padding: "11px 14px", borderBottom: idx < records.length - 1 ? `1px solid ${T.border}` : "none", background: T.bg }}>
              <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
                {/* 縮圖 */}
                <div
                  onClick={() => onViewPhoto(rec.image)}
                  style={{ width: 52, height: 52, borderRadius: 8, overflow: "hidden", border: `1px solid ${T.border}`, cursor: "pointer", flexShrink: 0, background: T.bgMuted }}>
                  <img src={rec.image} alt="匯款截圖" style={{ width: "100%", height: "100%", objectFit: "cover" }} />
                </div>
                {/* 資訊 */}
                <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                  <div style={{ display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 6, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: T.text }}>{toROCMonth(rec.month)}</span>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.green, fontWeight: 600, background: T.greenBg, border: `1px solid ${T.green}33`, borderRadius: 99, padding: "1px 7px" }}>✓ 已上傳</span>
                  </div>
                  {rec.note && <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: T.textSub, marginTop: 2 }}>{rec.note}</div>}
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: T.textMuted, marginTop: 2 }}>
                    {rec.uploaderName} · {toROC(rec.uploadedAt, true)}
                  </div>
                </div>
                {/* 操作 */}
                <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 6, flexShrink: 0 }}>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => onViewPhoto(rec.image)}
                    style={{ background: T.bgMuted, color: T.textSub, border: `1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius: 6, padding: "5px 9px", fontSize: 12, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>
                    放大
                  </button>
                  {canDelete(rec) && (
                    <button
                      onClick={() => setViewConfirmDel(rec.id)}
                      style={{ background: T.redBg, color: T.red, border: `1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius: 6, padding: "5px 9px", fontSize: 12, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>
                      刪除
                    </button>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* 確認刪除 inline */}
              {viewConfirmDel === rec.id && (
                <div style={{ marginTop: 8, background: T.redBg, border: `1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius: 8, padding: "9px 12px", display: "flex", alignItems: "center", gap: 10 }}>
                  <span style={{ flex: 1, fontSize: 13, color: T.red, fontWeight: 600 }}>確定刪除此截圖？</span>
                  <button onClick={() => deleteRecord(rec.id)} style={{ background: T.red, color: "#fff", border: "none", borderRadius: 6, padding: "5px 12px", fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 700, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>刪除</button>
                  <button onClick={() => setViewConfirmDel(null)} style={{ background: T.bgMuted, color: T.textSub, border: "none", borderRadius: 6, padding: "5px 10px", fontSize: 12, cursor: "pointer", fontFamily: "inherit" }}>取消</button>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  DEFECT PANEL
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function DefectPanel({ room, currentUser, onUpdate, onViewPhoto }) {
  const [showForm, setShowForm]     = useState(false);
  const [editItem, setEditItem]     = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm]             = useState({ description:"", photo:"" });
  const [confirmDel, setConfirmDel] = useState(null);
  const [showLog, setShowLog]       = useState(false);
  const defPhotoRef = useRef(null);

  const openAdd  = () => { setForm({ description:"", photo:"" }); setEditItem(null); setShowForm(true); };
  const openEdit = (d) => { setForm({ description:d.description||"", photo:d.photo||"" }); setEditItem(d); setShowForm(true); };
  const cancel   = () => { setShowForm(false); setEditItem(null); };

  const save = () => {
    if (!form.description && !form.photo) return;
    const now = nowISO();
    if (editItem) {
      const entry = { id:uid(), action:"modify", defectId:editItem.id, userId:currentUser.id, userName:currentUser.name, timestamp:now, detail:`修改：${form.description||"（更新照片）"}` };
      onUpdate(d => ({ ...d, rooms:d.rooms.map(r => r.id===room.id ? { ...r,
        defects:(r.defects||[]).map(x => x.id===editItem.id ? {...x,description:form.description,photo:form.photo,updatedBy:currentUser.id,updatedAt:now} : x),
        defectLog:[...(r.defectLog||[]),entry] } : r) }));
    } else {
      const newId = uid();
      const entry = { id:uid(), action:"add", defectId:newId, userId:currentUser.id, userName:currentUser.name, timestamp:now, detail:`新增：${form.description||"（上傳照片）"}` };
      onUpdate(d => ({ ...d, rooms:d.rooms.map(r => r.id===room.id ? { ...r,
        defects:[...(r.defects||[]), { id:newId, description:form.description, photo:form.photo, createdBy:currentUser.id, createdAt:now, updatedBy:null, updatedAt:null }],
        defectLog:[...(r.defectLog||[]),entry] } : r) }));
    }
    cancel();
  };

  const doDelete = (d) => {
    const entry = { id:uid(), action:"delete", defectId:d.id, userId:currentUser.id, userName:currentUser.name, timestamp:nowISO(), detail:`刪除：${d.description||"（已刪除照片）"}` };
    onUpdate(data => ({ ...data, rooms:data.rooms.map(r => r.id===room.id ? { ...r,
      defects:(r.defects||[]).filter(x => x.id!==d.id),
      defectLog:[...(r.defectLog||[]),entry] } : r) }));
    setConfirmDel(null);
  };

  const logColor = { add:T.green, modify:T.amber, delete:T.red };
  const logLabel = { add:"新增", modify:"修改", delete:"刪除" };
  const defects   = room.defects  || [];
  const defectLog = room.defectLog|| [];

  return (
    <div style={{ marginBottom:12 }}>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:8 }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6 }}>
          🔍 屋況瑕疵
          {defects.length>0&&<span style={{ background:T.amberBg, color:T.amber, fontSize:10, fontWeight:700, borderRadius:99, padding:"1px 7px" }}>{defects.length}</span>}
        </div>
        <button onClick={openAdd} style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:12 }}><Icon n="plus" s={12}/> 新增</button>
      </div>

      {defects.length===0&&!showForm&&<div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:12, padding:"8px 0 4px" }}>尚無瑕疵記錄</div>}

      {defects.map(d=>(
        <div key={d.id} style={{ background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 12px", marginBottom:6 }}>
          {confirmDel===d.id?(
            <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8 }}>
              <span style={{ flex:1, fontSize:12, color:T.text }}>確認刪除此瑕疵？</span>
              <button onClick={()=>doDelete(d)} style={{ background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>確認</button>
              <button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(null)} style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button>
            </div>
          ):(
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10, alignItems:"flex-start" }}>
              {d.photo&&<img src={d.photo} style={{ width:54, height:54, borderRadius:6, objectFit:"cover", cursor:"pointer", flexShrink:0, border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }} onClick={()=>onViewPhoto(d.photo)}/>}
              <div style={{ flex:1, minWidth:0 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.text, lineHeight:1.6, wordBreak:"break-all" }}>{d.description||"（無文字描述）"}</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:3 }}>
                  {d.updatedAt?`修改：${toROC(d.updatedAt,true)}`:`新增：${toROC(d.createdAt,true)}`}
                  　by {(d.updatedAt?d.updatedBy:d.createdBy)===currentUser.id?"我":currentUser.name}
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:4, flexShrink:0 }}>
                <button onClick={()=>openEdit(d)} style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 8px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}><Icon n="edit" s={12}/></button>
                <button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(d.id)} style={{ background:T.redBg, color:T.red, border:`1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 8px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}><Icon n="trash" s={12}/></button>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      ))}

      {showForm&&(
        <div style={{ background:T.accentBg, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}33`, borderRadius:8, padding:"12px", marginBottom:8 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, marginBottom:8 }}>{editItem?"✏️ 編輯瑕疵":"➕ 新增瑕疵"}</div>
          <input ref={defPhotoRef} type="file" accept="image/*,*/*" onChange={e=>{ const f=e.target.files[0]; if(!f)return; const r=new FileReader(); r.onload=ev=>setForm(fm=>({...fm,photo:ev.target.result})); r.readAsDataURL(f); }} style={{ display:"none" }}/>
          <button onClick={()=>defPhotoRef.current?.click()} style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", marginBottom:8, fontSize:12 }}>
            {form.photo?"✅ 已上傳照片（點擊更換）":"📷 上傳照片（選填）"}
          </button>
          <textarea value={form.description} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,description:e.target.value}))} placeholder="描述瑕疵狀況，例如：客廳牆壁有裂縫..." style={{ ...S.input, height:68, resize:"vertical", fontSize:13, marginBottom:8 }}/>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8 }}>
            <button onClick={save} style={{ flex:1, ...S.btn(), justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13 }}>儲存</button>
            <button onClick={cancel} style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), fontSize:13 }}>取消</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {defectLog.length>0&&(
        <div style={{ marginTop:6 }}>
          <button onClick={()=>setShowLog(v=>!v)} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:11, fontFamily:"inherit", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:4, padding:"4px 0", userSelect:"none" }}>
            <span style={{ transform:showLog?"rotate(90deg)":"rotate(0deg)", display:"inline-block", transition:"transform .15s" }}>▶</span>
            瑕疵變更記錄（{defectLog.length} 筆）
          </button>
          {showLog&&(
            <div style={{ background:T.bgMuted, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 12px", marginTop:4 }}>
              {[...defectLog].reverse().map(log=>(
                <div key={log.id} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"flex-start", gap:8, marginBottom:5 }}>
                  <span style={{ padding:"2px 7px", borderRadius:99, fontSize:10, fontWeight:700, background:(logColor[log.action]||T.textMuted)+"22", color:logColor[log.action]||T.textMuted, flexShrink:0 }}>{logLabel[log.action]||log.action}</span>
                  <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.text }}>{log.detail}</span>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, marginLeft:6 }}>by {log.userName||"未知"}</span>
                  </div>
                  <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, flexShrink:0, whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>{toROC(log.timestamp,true)}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ── 動態載入外部腳本（jsPDF / html2canvas / SignaturePad）──
const loadScript = (src) => new Promise((res) => {
  if (document.querySelector(`script[src="${src}"]`)) { res(); return; }
  const s = document.createElement("script");
  s.src = src; s.onload = res; s.onerror = res; // 失敗也繼續
  document.head.appendChild(s);
});

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  CONTRACT MODAL
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function ContractModal({ room, tenant, onClose }) {
  const landlordRef = useRef(null);
  const tenantRef   = useRef(null);
  const padsRef     = useRef({ landlord:null, tenant:null });
  const contractRef = useRef(null);
  const bigCanvasRef = useRef(null);
  const bigPadRef = useRef(null);
  const [ready,       setReady]       = useState(false);
  const [downloading, setDownloading] = useState(false);
  const [lHint, setLHint] = useState(true);
  const [tHint, setTHint] = useState(true);
  const [sigData, setSigData] = useState({ landlord:null, tenant:null });
  const [bigSig, setBigSig] = useState(null);

  const fmtM = (n) => parseInt(n||0).toLocaleString();
  const todayROC = toROC(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10));
  const dep = tenant?.deposit ? fmtM(tenant.deposit) : "___";

  // ── 載入 CDN 腳本 ────────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    Promise.all([
      loadScript("https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jspdf/2.5.1/jspdf.umd.min.js"),
      loadScript("https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2canvas/1.4.1/html2canvas.min.js"),
      loadScript("https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/signature_pad@4.1.7/dist/signature_pad.umd.min.js"),
    ]).then(() => setReady(true));
  }, []);

  // ── 初始化簽名板 ──────────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!ready || !window.SignaturePad) return;
    [["landlord", landlordRef, setLHint], ["tenant", tenantRef, setTHint]].forEach(([k, ref, setHint]) => {
      if (!ref.current) return;
      ref.current.width  = ref.current.parentElement.offsetWidth || 300;
      ref.current.height = 90;
      const pad = new window.SignaturePad(ref.current, { penColor:"#111827", backgroundColor:"rgba(0,0,0,0)" });
      pad.addEventListener("beginStroke", () => setHint(false));
      padsRef.current[k] = pad;
    });
  }, [ready]);

  // ── 放大簽名 Pad 初始化 ───────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!bigSig || !window.SignaturePad || !bigCanvasRef.current) return;
    const cv = bigCanvasRef.current;
    const ratio = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
    const rect = cv.getBoundingClientRect();
    cv.width  = rect.width * ratio;
    cv.height = rect.height * ratio;
    cv.getContext("2d").scale(ratio, ratio);
    const pad = new window.SignaturePad(cv, { penColor:"#111827", backgroundColor:"#ffffff", minWidth:1.2, maxWidth:3 });
    const prev = sigData[bigSig.key];
    if (prev) pad.fromDataURL(prev, { width:rect.width, height:rect.height });
    bigPadRef.current = pad;
    return () => { pad.off(); bigPadRef.current = null; };
  }, [bigSig]);

  const clearSig = (k) => {
    padsRef.current[k]?.clear();
    setSigData(s => ({ ...s, [k]:null }));
    if (k==="landlord") setLHint(true); else setTHint(true);
  };

  const confirmBigSig = () => {
    if (!bigPadRef.current || bigPadRef.current.isEmpty()) { alert("請先簽名"); return; }
    const dataUrl = bigPadRef.current.toDataURL("image/png");
    const k = bigSig.key;
    setSigData(s => ({ ...s, [k]:dataUrl }));
    const smallRef = k==="landlord" ? landlordRef : tenantRef;
    const cv = smallRef.current;
    if (cv) {
      const ctx = cv.getContext("2d");
      ctx.clearRect(0,0,cv.width,cv.height);
      const img = new Image();
      img.onload = () => { ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, cv.width, cv.height); };
      img.src = dataUrl;
    }
    if (k==="landlord") setLHint(false); else setTHint(false);
    setBigSig(null);
  };

  // ── 下載 PDF ──────────────────────────────────────────
  const downloadPDF = async () => {
    if (!window.html2canvas || !window.jspdf) { alert("PDF 工具載入中，請稍候再試"); return; }
    setDownloading(true);
    try {
      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 150));
      const el = contractRef.current;
      const canvas = await window.html2canvas(el, { scale:2, useCORS:true, backgroundColor:"#ffffff", logging:false });
      const { jsPDF } = window.jspdf;
      const doc   = new jsPDF({ orientation:"portrait", unit:"mm", format:"a4" });
      const pageW = doc.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
      const pageH = doc.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
      const imgW  = pageW - 20;
      const sliceH = Math.floor(canvas.width * (pageH - 20) / imgW);
      let srcY = 0, remaining = canvas.height, firstPage = true;
      while (remaining > 0) {
        const curr = Math.min(remaining, sliceH);
        const c2 = document.createElement("canvas");
        c2.width = canvas.width; c2.height = curr;
        c2.getContext("2d").drawImage(canvas, 0, srcY, canvas.width, curr, 0, 0, canvas.width, curr);
        const h = (curr / canvas.width) * imgW;
        if (!firstPage) doc.addPage();
        doc.addImage(c2.toDataURL("image/jpeg", 0.95), "JPEG", 10, 10, imgW, h);
        remaining -= curr; srcY += curr; firstPage = false;
      }
      const name = room.tenantContactName || tenant?.name || "房客";
      doc.save(`租賃契約書_${name}_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.pdf`);
    } catch(e) { alert("PDF 產生失敗：" + e.message); }
    setDownloading(false);
  };

  // ── 合約區塊輔助元件 ──────────────────────────────────
  const Sec = ({ title, children }) => (
    <div style={{ marginBottom:14 }}>
      <div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, borderLeft:`3px solid ${T.accent}`, paddingLeft:8, marginBottom:8 }}>{title}</div>
      {children}
    </div>
  );
  const Tbl = ({ rows }) => (
    <table style={{ width:"100%", borderCollapse:"collapse", fontSize:13, marginBottom:4 }}>
      <tbody>
        {rows.map(([k,v],i) => (
          <tr key={i}>
            <td style={{ padding:"6px 10px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, background:T.bgSub, fontWeight:600, width:"35%", color:T.textSub, fontSize:12 }}>{k}</td>
            <td style={{ padding:"6px 10px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, color:T.text }}>{v||"—"}</td>
          </tr>
        ))}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  );
  const Para = ({ children }) => (
    <div style={{ fontSize:13, lineHeight:2, color:"#374151" }}>{children}</div>
  );

  return (
    <Modal title={`📄 合約預覽 — ${room.communityName}`} onClose={onClose} width={680}>
      {/* ── 工具列 ── */}
      <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, marginBottom:14, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
        <button onClick={downloadPDF} disabled={!ready||downloading}
          style={{ ...S.btn(T.green), flex:1, justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13, opacity:(!ready||downloading)?0.6:1 }}>
          {downloading ? "⏳ 產生中…" : "⬇️ 下載 PDF"}
        </button>
        <button onClick={()=>window.print()}
          style={{ ...S.btn(T.textSub,true), flex:1, justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13 }}>
          🖨️ 列印
        </button>
      </div>
      {!ready && (
        <div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:13, padding:"8px 0 14px" }}>
          ⏳ 載入 PDF 工具中…
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── 合約本體（html2canvas 捕捉範圍）── */}
      <div ref={contractRef} style={{ background:"#fff", padding:"24px 20px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:10, fontFamily:"'Noto Sans TC',sans-serif" }}>
        {/* 標題 */}
        <div style={{ textAlign:"center", fontSize:20, fontWeight:800, marginBottom:4, letterSpacing:"0.04em", color:"#111827" }}>房屋租賃契約書</div>
        <div style={{ textAlign:"center", fontSize:12, color:"#6b7280", marginBottom:22 }}>立約日期：{todayROC}　　管理公司：家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司</div>

        <Sec title="第一條　租賃標的">
          <Tbl rows={[
            ["房屋名稱／門牌", (room.address && room.address !== room.communityName) ? `${room.communityName}（${room.address}）` : room.communityName || "___"],
            ["月租金",         `新臺幣 ${fmtM(room.rent)} 元整`],
            ["押金",           `新臺幣 ${dep} 元整`],
            ["每月繳租日",     `每月 ${room.rentDay||"5"} 日前繳清`],
            ["屋主姓名",       room.ownerName || "___"],
          ]}/>
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第二條　租賃期間">
          <Tbl rows={[
            ["起租日期", toROC(room.leaseStart)],
            ["到期日期", toROC(room.contractEnd)],
          ]}/>
          {(room.renewals||[]).length>0&&(
            <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, marginTop:4 }}>
              （已續約 {room.renewals.length} 次，最新到期：{toROC(room.renewals[room.renewals.length-1].renewEnd)}）
            </div>
          )}
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第三條　承租人資料">
          <Tbl rows={[
            ["姓名",       room.tenantContactName || tenant?.name || "___"],
            ["聯絡電話",   room.tenantContactPhone || tenant?.phone || "___"],
            ["緊急聯絡人", tenant?.emergencyName ? `${tenant.emergencyName}${tenant.emergencyPhone?" / "+tenant.emergencyPhone:""}` : "___"],
            ...(room.cohabitants||[]).map((c,i)=>[`同住人 ${i+1}`, `${c.name||"___"}${c.phone?" ／ "+c.phone:""}`]),
          ]}/>
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第四條　使用規定">
          <Para>
            一、承租人應依約定用途使用房屋，不得擅自改裝或破壞結構。<br/>
            二、未經出租人同意，不得將房屋轉租、分租或借他人使用。<br/>
            三、承租人應負責保持房屋及公共區域之整潔。
          </Para>
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第五條　修繕義務">
          <Para>
            一、房屋因自然損耗或設備故障，由出租人負責修繕。<br/>
            二、因承租人使用不當造成之損毀，由承租人自行負責。<br/>
            三、報修請通知管理公司，並於合理期限內完成修繕。
          </Para>
        </Sec>

        <Sec title="第六條　違約處理">
          <Para>
            一、承租人無故提前終止契約，應賠償一個月租金作為違約金。<br/>
            二、出租人無故提前終止契約，應退還雙倍押金予承租人。<br/>
            三、租金逾期繳納超過 7 日，出租人得催告；逾期仍未繳清者，得終止契約。
          </Para>
        </Sec>

        {/* ── 簽名區（點擊放大簽名，html2canvas 會捕捉 canvas 內容）── */}
        <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:16, marginTop:20 }}>
          {[
            { label:"出租人（房東）簽名", key:"landlord", ref:landlordRef, hint:lHint },
            { label:"承租人（房客）簽名", key:"tenant",   ref:tenantRef,   hint:tHint },
          ].map(({ label, key, ref, hint }) => (
            <div key={key}>
              <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, marginBottom:6 }}>{label}</div>
              <div onClick={()=>setBigSig({ key, label })}
                style={{ position:"relative", border:`1.5px dashed ${T.accent}88`, borderRadius:8, background:"#fafafa", height:90, overflow:"hidden", cursor:"pointer" }}
                title="點擊放大簽名">
                <canvas ref={ref} style={{ width:"100%", height:"100%", display:"block", pointerEvents:"none" }}/>
                {hint && (
                  <div style={{ position:"absolute", inset:0, display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:12, color:T.accent, pointerEvents:"none", gap:3, fontWeight:600 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize:18 }}>✍️</span>
                    <span>點擊此處放大簽名</span>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
              <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginTop:4 }}>
                <button onClick={(e)=>{e.stopPropagation(); clearSig(key);}} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, cursor:"pointer", padding:0, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>✕ 清除</button>
                <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted }}>日期：{todayROC}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, textAlign:"center", marginTop:10, lineHeight:1.6 }}>
        ※ 此為系統自動產出之合約草稿，點擊簽名欄位可放大簽名，簽名後下載 PDF 留存正本。
      </div>

      {/* ── 放大簽名 Modal ── */}
      {bigSig && (
        <div onClick={(e)=>{ if(e.target===e.currentTarget) setBigSig(null); }}
          style={{ position:"fixed", inset:0, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.75)", zIndex:3000, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:12 }}>
          <div style={{ background:"#fff", borderRadius:14, padding:"16px 16px 14px", width:"min(700px,96vw)", display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10 }}>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center" }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize:15, fontWeight:800, color:T.text }}>✍️ {bigSig.label}</div>
              <button onClick={()=>setBigSig(null)} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", color:T.textSub, fontSize:20, padding:4, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>×</button>
            </div>
            <div style={{ border:`2px dashed ${T.accent}`, borderRadius:10, background:"#fff", height:"min(55vh,360px)", touchAction:"none" }}>
              <canvas ref={bigCanvasRef} style={{ width:"100%", height:"100%", display:"block", borderRadius:10 }}/>
            </div>
            <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, textAlign:"center" }}>請在上方空白區域以手指或滑鼠完成簽名</div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8 }}>
              <button onClick={()=>bigPadRef.current?.clear()} style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:10, padding:"12px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>🗑 清除重簽</button>
              <button onClick={()=>setBigSig(null)} style={{ flex:1, background:"#fff", color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:10, padding:"12px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button>
              <button onClick={confirmBigSig} style={{ flex:1.2, background:T.accent, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:10, padding:"12px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>✓ 確認簽名</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </Modal>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  ROOMS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function Rooms({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const { rooms, tenants, bills } = data;
  const role       = safeRole(currentUser.role);
  const isSA       = isSARole(currentUser.role);
  const isFinance  = currentUser.role === "finance";
  const isAdmin    = currentUser.role === "admin";
  // ── 權限規則 ──────────────────────────────────────────
  // canEditRoom : superadmin + admin 都可以新增 / 編輯房源
  // canDeleteRoom: 只有 superadmin 可以刪除房源
  const canEditRoom   = isSA || isAdmin;
  const canDeleteRoom = isSA;
  const isViewer   = currentUser.role === "viewer";
  const viewerRoomId = isViewer ? (currentUser._roomId || "") : "";
  const todayDay   = new Date().getDate();
  const thisMonthStr = () => new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 7);

  const isRentDue = (room) => {
    if (room.status !== "rented") return false;
    if (todayDay < parseInt(room.rentDay || "5")) return false;
    return !(bills || []).some(b => b.roomId === room.id && b.month === thisMonthStr() && b.status === "paid");
  };

  const markPaid = (room) => {
    const month = thisMonthStr();
    const t = (tenants || []).find(t => t.linkedRoom === room.id && !t.isCohabitant)
           || (tenants || []).find(t => t.roomId === room.id && !t.isCohabitant)
           || (tenants || []).find(t => t.roomId === room.id);
    onUpdate(d => {
      const ex = d.bills.find(b => b.roomId === room.id && b.month === month);
      const nb = ex
        ? d.bills.map(b => b.id === ex.id ? { ...b, status:"paid", paidDate:todayStr(), recordedBy:currentUser.id } : b)
        : [...d.bills, { id:uid(), tenantId:t?.id||room.tenantId||"", roomId:room.id, type:"rent", amount:room.rent, month, status:"paid", paidDate:todayStr(), recordedBy:currentUser.id }];
      return { ...d, bills:nb, activityLog:[...d.activityLog, { id:uid(), userId:currentUser.id, action:`標記「${room.communityName}」${month} 月租金已繳`, timestamp:nowISO() }] };
    });
  };

  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(() => { const s = new Set(); if (isViewer && viewerRoomId) s.add(viewerRoomId); return s; });
  const toggle = (id) => setExpanded(p => { const n = new Set(p); n.has(id) ? n.delete(id) : n.add(id); return n; });

  const emptyForm = () => { const t = todayStr(); return { communityName:"", address:"", ownerName:"", salesRep:"", rentDay:"5", rent:"", leaseStart:t, contractEnd:addOneYear(t), tenantContactName:"", tenantContactPhone:"", cohabitants:[], renewals:[], contractPhotos:[], ownerBankPhoto:"", inspectionPhotos:[], autoRentRemind:false, rentalSubsidy:false, taxDeclaration:false, householdRegistration:false, roomType:"general", electricityType:"fixed", electricityFixedRate:"", waterType:"fixed", waterFixedRate:"", assignedAdmins:[], parkingSpots:[], lineNotifyToken:"" }; };
  const newParkingSpot = (type, leaseStart, contractEnd) => ({ id:uid(), type, spotNo:"", linkedRoomId:"", rent:"", leaseStart:leaseStart||"", contractEnd:contractEnd||"", renewals:[] });
  const [showAdd, setShowAdd]     = useState(false);
  const [editRoom, setEditRoom]   = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm]           = useState(emptyForm);
  const [showRenew, setShowRenew] = useState(false);
  const [showParking, setShowParking]       = useState(false);
  const [openParkingIds, setOpenParkingIds] = useState(new Set());
  const [parkingRenewIds, setParkingRenewIds] = useState(new Set());
  const [confirmDel, setConfirmDel]   = useState(null);
  const [viewPhoto, setViewPhoto]       = useState(null);
  const [contractRoom, setContractRoom] = useState(null);
  const [lineRemind, setLineRemind]     = useState({});
  const lineRemindTimer                 = useRef({});
  const [showMeterForm, setShowMeterForm] = useState(null); // room.id
  const [meterDraft, setMeterDraft]       = useState({ date:"", reading:"", rate:"" });

  const generateElecReport = useCallback((room) => {
    const readings = (room.meterReadings||[]).slice().sort((a,b)=>a.date.localeCompare(b.date));
    const rent = Number(room.rent||0);
    const label = `${room.communityName}${room.address?" "+room.address:""}`;
    const lines = [`【${label} 電費月報表】`, ""];
    lines.push("抄表日期\t抄表度數\t電費單價\t本期電費\t租金\t合計匯款");
    lines.push("─".repeat(52));
    readings.forEach((r,i) => {
      const prev = i>0 ? readings[i-1] : null;
      const diff = prev ? r.reading - prev.reading : 0;
      const elecFee = prev ? Math.round(diff * r.ratePerKwh) : null;
      const total = elecFee!==null ? elecFee+rent : null;
      const isLast = i===readings.length-1;
      const elecStr = elecFee!==null ? elecFee.toLocaleString() : "—";
      const totalStr = total!==null ? total.toLocaleString() : (i===0?"（起始）":"—");
      const rateStr = elecFee!==null ? r.ratePerKwh.toFixed(2) : "—";
      lines.push(`${toROC(r.date)}\t${r.reading.toLocaleString()}\t${rateStr}\t${elecStr}\t${rent.toLocaleString()}\t${totalStr}${isLast?" ◀ 本期":""}`);
    });
    lines.push("");
    if (readings.length>1) {
      const last=readings[readings.length-1], prev=readings[readings.length-2];
      const fee=Math.round((last.reading-prev.reading)*last.ratePerKwh);
      const total=fee+rent;
      lines.push(`▶ 本期應匯款：NT$ ${total.toLocaleString()}`);
      lines.push(`   電費 NT$${fee.toLocaleString()} ＋ 租金 NT$${rent.toLocaleString()}`);
    } else if (readings.length===1) {
      lines.push(`▶ 本月租金：NT$ ${rent.toLocaleString()}`);
    }
    lines.push(`▶ 請於每月 ${room.rentDay||5} 號前完成匯款`);
    lines.push(""); lines.push("感謝您的配合！");
    lines.push("— 家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司");
    return lines.join("\n");
  }, []);

  const sendLineReminder = (room) => {
    const unpaidBills = (bills||[]).filter(b=>b.roomId===room.id&&b.status==="unpaid").sort((a,b)=>a.month.localeCompare(b.month));
    const totalUnpaid = unpaidBills.reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0), 0);
    const monthList   = unpaidBills.map(b=>toROCMonth(b.month)).join("、")||toROCMonth(thisMonthStr());
    const amount      = totalUnpaid || room.rent || 0;
    const contactNote = room.lineNotifyToken?.trim() ? `（${room.lineNotifyToken.trim()}）` : "";
    const msg = `⚠️ 租金催繳通知${contactNote}\n\n房源：${room.communityName}${room.address?" ("+room.address+")":""}\n催繳月份：${monthList}\n應繳金額：NT$ ${Number(amount).toLocaleString()}\n繳租日：每月 ${room.rentDay||5} 號\n\n請您盡速完成匯款，謝謝您的配合。\n— 家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司`;
    // 優先：先同步開 LINE（保留 user gesture），再更新狀態
    openLineShare(msg);
    setLineRemind(s=>({...s,[room.id]:"sent"}));
    onUpdate(d=>({...d, activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{ id:uid(), userId:currentUser.id, action:`LINE 催繳通知「${room.communityName}」→ 已開啟分享（${monthList}，NT$ ${Number(amount).toLocaleString()}）`, timestamp:nowISO() }]}));
    clearTimeout(lineRemindTimer.current[room.id]);
    lineRemindTimer.current[room.id] = setTimeout(()=>setLineRemind(s=>({...s,[room.id]:"idle"})), 5000);
  };
  const [openChat, setOpenChat]       = useState(null);
  const [chatInput, setChatInput]     = useState({});
  const [editTpl, setEditTpl]         = useState(false);
  const [tplDraft, setTplDraft]       = useState(null);
  const fileRef        = useRef(null);
  const bankRef        = useRef(null);
  const inspectionRef  = useRef(null);
  const sf = k => e => setForm(f => ({ ...f, [k]: e.target.value }));
  const handleInspectionUpload = (e) => {
    Array.from(e.target.files).forEach(file => {
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = ev => setForm(f => ({ ...f, inspectionPhotos:[...(f.inspectionPhotos||[]), { id:uid(), dataUrl:ev.target.result, uploadedAt:nowISO() }] }));
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
    e.target.value = "";
  };
  const handleContractUpload = (e) => {
    Array.from(e.target.files).forEach(file => {
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = ev => setForm(f => ({ ...f, contractPhotos:[...(f.contractPhotos||[]), { id:uid(), dataUrl:ev.target.result, uploadedAt:nowISO() }] }));
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
    e.target.value = "";
  };

  const openEdit = (room) => {
    setForm({ communityName:room.communityName||"", address:room.address||"", ownerName:room.ownerName||"", salesRep:room.salesRep||"", rentDay:room.rentDay||"5", rent:room.rent||"", leaseStart:room.leaseStart||"", contractEnd:room.contractEnd||"", tenantContactName:room.tenantContactName||"", tenantContactPhone:room.tenantContactPhone||"", cohabitants:(room.cohabitants||[]).map(c=>({name:c.name||"",phone:c.phone||""})), renewals:(room.renewals||[]).map(r=>({renewStart:r.renewStart||"",renewEnd:r.renewEnd||""})), contractPhotos:room.contractPhotos||(room.contractPhoto?[{id:uid(),dataUrl:room.contractPhoto,uploadedAt:""}]:[]), ownerBankPhoto:room.ownerBankPhoto||"", inspectionPhotos:room.inspectionPhotos||[], autoRentRemind:room.autoRentRemind||false, rentalSubsidy:room.rentalSubsidy||false, taxDeclaration:room.taxDeclaration||false, householdRegistration:room.householdRegistration||false, roomType:room.roomType||"general", electricityType:room.electricityType||"fixed", electricityFixedRate:room.electricityFixedRate||"", waterType:room.waterType||"fixed", waterFixedRate:room.waterFixedRate||"", assignedAdmins:room.assignedAdmins||[], parkingSpots:(room.parkingSpots||[]).map(s=>({...s,renewals:(s.renewals||[]).map(r=>({...r}))})), lineNotifyToken:room.lineNotifyToken||"" });
    setShowRenew((room.renewals || []).length > 0);
    setShowParking((room.parkingSpots||[]).length > 0);
    setOpenParkingIds(new Set()); setParkingRenewIds(new Set());
    setEditRoom(room); setShowAdd(true);
  };

  // ── 儲存房源：產生詳細的 diff 記錄 ───────────────────
  const saveRoom = () => {
    if (!form.communityName || !form.rent) return;
    const rid = editRoom ? editRoom.id : uid();
    onUpdate(d => {
      let nr = editRoom
        ? d.rooms.map(r => r.id === editRoom.id ? { ...r, ...form, rent:parseInt(form.rent) } : r)
        : [...d.rooms, { id:rid, status:"vacant", tenantId:null, propId:"p1", ...form, rent:parseInt(form.rent) }];

      let nt = d.tenants.filter(t => t.linkedRoom !== rid);
      let mainId = null;
      if (form.tenantContactName) {
        const ex = d.tenants.find(t => t.linkedRoom === rid && !t.isCohabitant);
        mainId = ex ? ex.id : uid();
        nt = [...nt, { id:mainId, name:form.tenantContactName, phone:form.tenantContactPhone||"", email:ex?.email||"", roomId:rid, moveIn:ex?.moveIn||form.leaseStart||"", contractEnd:form.contractEnd||"", deposit:ex?.deposit||0, linkedRoom:rid, isCohabitant:false }];
        nr = nr.map(r => r.id === rid ? { ...r, status:"rented", tenantId:mainId } : r);
        (form.cohabitants || []).forEach((c, i) => {
          if (c.name) {
            const ec = d.tenants.find(t => t.linkedRoom === rid && t.isCohabitant && t.cohabitantIndex === i);
            nt = [...nt, { id:ec?ec.id:uid(), name:c.name, phone:c.phone||"", email:ec?.email||"", roomId:rid, moveIn:"", contractEnd:form.contractEnd||"", deposit:0, linkedRoom:rid, isCohabitant:true, cohabitantIndex:i }];
          }
        });
      } else {
        nr = nr.map(r => r.id === rid ? { ...r, status:"vacant", tenantId:null } : r);
      }

      let nb = d.bills;
      if (!editRoom && mainId) {
        const mo = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 7);
        if (!nb.find(b => b.roomId === rid && b.month === mo))
          nb = [...nb, { id:uid(), tenantId:mainId, roomId:rid, type:"rent", amount:parseInt(form.rent), month:mo, status:"unpaid", paidDate:null, recordedBy:null }];
      }

      // ── 產生詳細 diff 記錄 ───────────────────────────
      let logAction;
      if (!editRoom) {
        // 新增：記錄所有填寫的主要欄位
        const details = [
          form.communityName && `房源名稱：${form.communityName}`,
          form.rent          && `月租金：${fmt(form.rent)}`,
          form.rentDay       && `繳租日：每月 ${form.rentDay} 號`,
          form.leaseStart    && `起租日：${toROC(form.leaseStart)}`,
          form.contractEnd   && `到期日：${toROC(form.contractEnd)}`,
          form.tenantContactName && `主租客：${form.tenantContactName}`,
          form.ownerName     && `屋主：${form.ownerName}`,
          form.salesRep      && `業務：${form.salesRep}`,
        ].filter(Boolean).join("、");
        logAction = `【新增房源】「${form.communityName}」（${details}）`;
      } else {
        // 編輯：比對與原始資料的差異
        const prev = d.rooms.find(r => r.id === editRoom.id) || editRoom;
        const diffs = [];
        const checkField = (key, label, formatFn) => {
          const oldVal = prev[key] != null ? String(prev[key]) : "";
          const newVal = form[key]  != null ? String(form[key]) : "";
          if (oldVal !== newVal) {
            const fmtOld = formatFn ? formatFn(oldVal) : (oldVal || "（空）");
            const fmtNew = formatFn ? formatFn(newVal) : (newVal || "（空）");
            diffs.push(`${label}：${fmtOld} → ${fmtNew}`);
          }
        };
        checkField("communityName",      "名稱");
        checkField("address",            "地址");
        checkField("ownerName",          "屋主");
        checkField("salesRep",           "業務");
        checkField("rent",               "月租金", v => v ? fmt(v) : "（空）");
        checkField("rentDay",            "繳租日", v => v ? `每月 ${v} 號` : "（空）");
        checkField("leaseStart",         "起租日", v => toROC(v) || "（空）");
        checkField("contractEnd",        "到期日", v => toROC(v) || "（空）");
        checkField("tenantContactName",  "主租客");
        checkField("tenantContactPhone", "主租客電話");
        const oldAutoRemind = prev.autoRentRemind ? "開啟" : "關閉";
        const newAutoRemind = form.autoRentRemind ? "開啟" : "關閉";
        if (oldAutoRemind !== newAutoRemind) diffs.push(`自動提醒：${oldAutoRemind} → ${newAutoRemind}`);
        [["rentalSubsidy","租屋補助"],["taxDeclaration","是否報稅"],["householdRegistration","入戶籍"]].forEach(([k,l])=>{
          const o = prev[k]?"是":"否", n = form[k]?"是":"否";
          if (o !== n) diffs.push(`${l}：${o} → ${n}`);
        });
        const rtLabel = v => v==="shared"?"分租套房":"一般房型";
        if ((prev.roomType||"general")!==(form.roomType||"general")) diffs.push(`房型：${rtLabel(prev.roomType)} → ${rtLabel(form.roomType)}`);
        if (form.roomType==="shared") {
          if ((prev.electricityType||"fixed")!==form.electricityType) diffs.push(`電費類型：${prev.electricityType||"fixed"}→${form.electricityType}`);
          if (form.electricityType==="fixed"&&String(prev.electricityFixedRate||"")!==String(form.electricityFixedRate||"")) diffs.push(`電費單價：${prev.electricityFixedRate||"0"}→${form.electricityFixedRate}元/度`);
          if ((prev.waterType||"fixed")!==form.waterType) diffs.push(`水費類型：${prev.waterType||"fixed"}→${form.waterType}`);
          if (form.waterType==="fixed"&&String(prev.waterFixedRate||"")!==String(form.waterFixedRate||"")) diffs.push(`水費單價：${prev.waterFixedRate||"0"}→${form.waterFixedRate}元/人`);
        }
        const oldRenewals = (prev.renewals || []).length;
        const newRenewals = (form.renewals || []).length;
        if (oldRenewals !== newRenewals) diffs.push(`續約記錄：${oldRenewals} 筆 → ${newRenewals} 筆`);
        const oldAdmins = [...(prev.assignedAdmins||[])].sort().join(",");
        const newAdmins = [...(form.assignedAdmins||[])].sort().join(",");
        if (oldAdmins !== newAdmins) {
          const getName = id => { const u=(d.users||[]).find(x=>x.id===id); return u?u.name:id; };
          const oldNames = (prev.assignedAdmins||[]).map(getName).join("、")||"（未指定）";
          const newNames = (form.assignedAdmins||[]).map(getName).join("、")||"（未指定）";
          diffs.push(`負責管理員：${oldNames} → ${newNames}`);
        }
        const oldCar  = (prev.parkingSpots||[]).filter(s=>s.type==="car").length;
        const newCar  = (form.parkingSpots||[]).filter(s=>s.type==="car").length;
        const oldMoto = (prev.parkingSpots||[]).filter(s=>s.type==="moto").length;
        const newMoto = (form.parkingSpots||[]).filter(s=>s.type==="moto").length;
        if (oldCar!==newCar)   diffs.push(`汽車車位：${oldCar} 個 → ${newCar} 個`);
        if (oldMoto!==newMoto) diffs.push(`機車車位：${oldMoto} 個 → ${newMoto} 個`);

        logAction = diffs.length > 0
          ? `【修改房源】「${form.communityName}」變更：${diffs.join("；")}`
          : `【修改房源】「${form.communityName}」（無欄位異動，僅重新儲存）`;
      }

      return { ...d, rooms:nr, tenants:nt, bills:nb, activityLog:[...d.activityLog, { id:uid(), userId:currentUser.id, action:logAction, timestamp:nowISO() }] };
    });
    setShowAdd(false); setEditRoom(null);
  };

  // ── 刪除：只有 superadmin 才能執行 ───────────────────
  const deleteRoom = (room) => {
    if (!canDeleteRoom) return; // 防呆
    onUpdate(d => ({
      ...d,
      rooms: d.rooms.filter(r => r.id !== room.id),
      tenants: d.tenants.filter(t => t.linkedRoom !== room.id),
      activityLog: [...d.activityLog, { id:uid(), userId:currentUser.id, action:`【刪除房源】「${room.communityName}」（月租金 ${fmt(room.rent)}，狀態：${room.status === "rented" ? "出租中" : "空房"}）`, timestamp:nowISO() }],
    }));
    setConfirmDel(null);
  };

  // ── Chat View ──
  if (openChat) {
    const room = rooms.find(r=>r.id===openChat);
    if (!room) { setOpenChat(null); return null; }
    const msgs = room.messages||[];
    const text = chatInput[openChat]||"";
    const tpls = data.chatTemplates||["","","",""];
    const draft = tplDraft??tpls;
    const doSend = (ov) => {
      const t=(ov??text).trim(); if(!t) return;
      const msg={id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,userName:currentUser.name,userRole:currentUser.role,text:t,timestamp:nowISO()};
      onUpdate(d=>({...d,rooms:d.rooms.map(r=>r.id===openChat?{...r,messages:[...(r.messages||[]),msg]}:r)}));
      if(!ov) setChatInput(c=>({...c,[openChat]:""}));
    };
    const saveTpl = () => { onUpdate(d=>({...d,chatTemplates:draft})); setEditTpl(false); setTplDraft(null); };
    return (
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", height:"calc(100vh - 130px)" }}>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:12, padding:"0 0 12px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, marginBottom:12, flexShrink:0 }}>
          <button onClick={()=>setOpenChat(null)} style={{ background:T.bgMuted, border:"none", borderRadius:7, color:T.textSub, padding:"6px 12px", fontSize:14, cursor:"pointer", fontWeight:600, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>‹ 返回</button>
          <div style={{ flex:1 }}><div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:15 }}>{room.communityName}</div>{room.address&&<div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub }}>📍 {room.address}</div>}</div>
          <span style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub }}>{msgs.length} 則訊息</span>
        </div>
        <div style={{ flex:1, overflowY:"auto", display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10, paddingBottom:8 }}>
          {msgs.length===0 ? <div style={{ flex:1, display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", color:T.textSub, gap:8 }}><div style={{ fontSize:32 }}>💬</div><div style={{ fontSize:14, fontWeight:600 }}>尚無對話</div></div>
            : msgs.map((m,i)=>{
              const isMe=m.userId===currentUser.id, isSys=m.isSystem;
              const mr=safeRole(m.userRole);
              const showD=i===0||new Date(m.timestamp).toDateString()!==new Date(msgs[i-1].timestamp).toDateString();
              return <div key={m.id}>
                {showD&&<div style={{ textAlign:"center", marginBottom:8 }}><span style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, fontSize:12, fontWeight:600, padding:"2px 10px", borderRadius:99 }}>{new Date(m.timestamp).getMonth()+1}月{new Date(m.timestamp).getDate()}日</span></div>}
                {isSys ? <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"center", margin:"4px 0" }}><div style={{ background:T.amberBg, border:`1px solid ${T.amber}44`, borderRadius:10, padding:"10px 14px", maxWidth:"88%", fontSize:13, color:T.text, lineHeight:1.6 }}><div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.amber, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:4 }}>🔔 系統自動提醒</div>{m.text}</div></div>
                  : <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:isMe?"row-reverse":"row", alignItems:"flex-end", gap:8 }}>
                    <div style={{ width:28, height:28, borderRadius:"50%", background:mr.color+"22", border:`1px solid ${mr.color}44`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:mr.color, flexShrink:0 }}>{m.userName?.[0]||"?"}</div>
                    <div style={{ maxWidth:"75%", display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:isMe?"flex-end":"flex-start", gap:3 }}>
                      <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, display:"flex", gap:5 }}>{!isMe&&<span style={{ color:mr.color, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.userName}</span>}<span>{new Date(m.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString("zh-TW",{hour:"2-digit",minute:"2-digit"})}</span></div>
                      <div style={{ background:isMe?T.accent:T.bgMuted, color:isMe?"#fff":T.text, border:isMe?"none":`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:isMe?"14px 14px 4px 14px":"14px 14px 14px 4px", padding:"9px 14px", fontSize:14, lineHeight:1.5, wordBreak:"break-word" }}>{m.text}</div>
                    </div>
                  </div>}
              </div>;
            })}
        </div>
        {/* 快速範本：租客身份不顯示 */}
        {!isViewer && (
          <div style={{ borderTop:`1px solid ${T.border}`, paddingTop:10, flexShrink:0 }}>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:7 }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, fontWeight:700 }}>⚡ 快速範本</span>
              {role.canEdit && (editTpl
                ? <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:6 }}><button onClick={saveTpl} style={{ background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:6, padding:"3px 10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>儲存</button><button onClick={()=>{setTplDraft(null);setEditTpl(false);}} style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:"none", borderRadius:6, padding:"3px 10px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button></div>
                : <button onClick={()=>{setTplDraft([...tpls]);setEditTpl(true);}} style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:6, padding:"3px 10px", fontSize:12, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>✎ 編輯</button>)}
            </div>
            {editTpl ? <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:6, marginBottom:10 }}>{draft.map((t,i)=><div key={i} style={{ display:"flex", gap:6 }}><span style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, width:18, textAlign:"right" }}>{i+1}.</span><input style={{ flex:1, background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.borderMd}`, borderRadius:7, color:T.text, padding:"7px 10px", fontSize:13, outline:"none", fontFamily:"inherit" }} value={t} placeholder={`範本 ${i+1}`} onChange={e=>setTplDraft(p=>(p??tpls).map((v,j)=>j===i?e.target.value:v))}/></div>)}</div>
              : <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:7, overflowX:"auto", paddingBottom:8 }}>{tpls.map((t,i)=>t.trim()?<button key={i} onClick={()=>doSend(t)} style={{ flexShrink:0, maxWidth:200, background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"6px 12px", fontSize:12, color:T.text, cursor:"pointer", whiteSpace:"nowrap", overflow:"hidden", textOverflow:"ellipsis", fontFamily:"inherit" }} title={t}>{t.length>22?t.slice(0,22)+"…":t}</button>:null)}</div>}
          </div>
        )}
        <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, paddingTop:6, flexShrink:0 }}>
          <input style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:10, color:T.text, padding:"10px 14px", fontSize:14, outline:"none", fontFamily:"inherit" }} placeholder="輸入訊息…" value={text} onChange={e=>setChatInput(c=>({...c,[openChat]:e.target.value}))} onKeyDown={e=>e.key==="Enter"&&!e.shiftKey&&doSend()}/>
          <button onClick={()=>doSend()} style={{ background:text.trim()?T.accent:T.bgMuted, color:text.trim()?"#fff":T.textSub, border:"none", borderRadius:10, padding:"10px 18px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>送出</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const roomPriority = (r) => {
    const rd = parseInt(r.rentDay||"5");
    const unpaid = (bills||[]).filter(b=>b.roomId===r.id&&b.status==="unpaid").sort((a,b)=>a.month.localeCompare(b.month));
    let overdueDays = 0;
    if (r.status==="rented" && unpaid.length) {
      const [yr,mo]=unpaid[0].month.split("-").map(Number);
      overdueDays = Math.max(0,Math.floor((Date.now()-new Date(yr,mo-1,rd).getTime())/86400000));
    }
    if (overdueDays >= 3) return 5;
    if (isRentDue(r)) return 4;
    if (r.depositRefundStatus==="refunded" && !r.depositEvictionDone) return 3;
    if (r.depositRefundStatus==="pending") return 2;
    const dl = r.contractEnd?daysUntil(r.contractEnd):null;
    if (dl!==null && dl<=60 && dl>0) return 1;
    return 0;
  };

  const visibleRooms = rooms.filter(r=>{
    if (isViewer) return r.id===viewerRoomId;
    if (isSA)     return true;
    if (isAdmin)  return !(r.assignedAdmins||[]).length || (r.assignedAdmins||[]).includes(currentUser.id);
    return true;
  }).sort((a,b)=> roomPriority(b) - roomPriority(a));

  const fs = (v) => (v !== undefined && v !== null && String(v).trim() !== "") ? { background:"#fff" } : { background:"#f3f4f6" };

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:16 }}>
        <h2 style={S.title}>房源管理</h2>
        {canEditRoom && <button onClick={()=>{setForm(emptyForm());setEditRoom(null);setShowAdd(true);setShowRenew(false);setShowParking(false);setOpenParkingIds(new Set());setParkingRenewIds(new Set());}} style={S.btn()}><Icon n="plus" s={13}/> 新增房源</button>}
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:8 }}>
        {visibleRooms.map(room=>{
          const dl = room.contractEnd?daysUntil(room.contractEnd):null;
          const near = dl!==null&&dl<=60&&dl>0;
          const due  = isRentDue(room);
          const open = expanded.has(room.id);
          const overdueDays = (() => {
            if (room.status!=="rented") return 0;
            const rd = parseInt(room.rentDay||"5");
            const unpaid = (bills||[]).filter(b=>b.roomId===room.id&&b.status==="unpaid").sort((a,b)=>a.month.localeCompare(b.month));
            if (!unpaid.length) return 0;
            const [yr,mo]=unpaid[0].month.split("-").map(Number);
            return Math.max(0,Math.floor((Date.now()-new Date(yr,mo-1,rd).getTime())/86400000));
          })();
          const isOverdue = overdueDays >= 3;
          const isEvicting = room.depositRefundStatus==="refunded" && !room.depositEvictionDone;
          const bc   = isEvicting?"#7c3aed":(isOverdue?"#ea580c":(due?T.red:(near?T.amber+"99":T.border)));
          const cardBg = isEvicting?"#faf5ff":(isOverdue?"#fff7ed":(due?T.redBg:(near?T.amberBg:T.bg)));
          return (
            <div key={room.id} style={{ borderRadius:12, border:`${isEvicting||due||isOverdue?2:1}px solid ${bc}`, overflow:"hidden", background:cardBg, animation: !open && (isOverdue||due||isEvicting||near||room.depositRefundStatus==="pending") ? "flash-alert-border 1.3s ease-in-out infinite" : "none" }}>
              <div onClick={()=>toggle(room.id)} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10, padding:"13px 16px", cursor:"pointer", background:cardBg, userSelect:"none" }}>
                <div style={{ width:9, height:9, borderRadius:"50%", flexShrink:0, background:isOverdue?"#ea580c":(due?T.red:(room.status==="rented"?T.green:T.amber)), animation:isOverdue?"pulse 1s infinite":"none" }}/>
                <div style={{ flex:1, minWidth:0 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:15, whiteSpace:"nowrap", overflow:"hidden", textOverflow:"ellipsis" }}>{room.communityName}</div>
                  {!open && <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, marginTop:1, display:"flex", gap:8, alignItems:"center", flexWrap:"wrap" }}>{room.rent&&<span>{fmt(room.rent)}/月</span>}{room.tenantContactName&&<span>· {room.tenantContactName}</span>}{isOverdue&&<span style={{ color:"#ea580c", fontWeight:800, animation:"pulse 1s infinite" }}>· 🚨 逾期 {overdueDays} 天</span>}{due&&!isOverdue&&<span style={{ color:T.red, fontWeight:700 }}>· ⚠️ 待繳租</span>}{near&&!due&&!isOverdue&&<span style={{ color:T.amber, fontWeight:700 }}>· 即將到期</span>}{isEvicting&&<span style={{ color:"#7c3aed", fontWeight:700 }}>· 💰 押金已退回</span>}{room.depositRefundStatus==="pending"&&<span style={{ color:"#7c3aed", fontWeight:700 }}>· 💰 押金退還申請中</span>}{(room.assignedAdmins||[]).length>0&&<span style={{ display:"inline-flex", gap:3, alignItems:"center" }}>{(room.assignedAdmins||[]).map(uid=>{const u=(data.users||[]).find(x=>x.id===uid);return u?<span key={uid} title={u.name} style={{ width:16,height:16,borderRadius:"50%",background:T.blue,color:"#fff",fontSize:9,fontWeight:700,display:"inline-flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",flexShrink:0 }}>{u.avatar||u.name[0]}</span>:null;})}</span>}</div>}
                </div>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6, flexShrink:0 }}>
                  {due&&role.canEdit&&<button onClick={e=>{e.stopPropagation();markPaid(room);}} style={{ background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:7, padding:"5px 11px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", whiteSpace:"nowrap", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>已繳租完畢</button>}
                  {(due||isOverdue)&&(isSA||isAdmin)&&(()=>{
                    const rs = lineRemind[room.id]||"idle";
                    const sent = rs==="sent";
                    return (
                      <button onClick={e=>{e.stopPropagation();sendLineReminder(room);}}
                        title="開啟 LINE 分享催繳訊息"
                        style={{ background:sent?"#22c55e":"#06b6d4", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:7, padding:"5px 10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", whiteSpace:"nowrap", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                        {sent?"✅ 已開啟":"📲 LINE催繳"}
                      </button>
                    );
                  })()}
                  <span style={S.tag(room.status==="rented"?T.green:T.amber)}>{SL[room.status]}</span>
                  <span style={{ color:T.textMuted, fontSize:11, transition:"transform 0.2s", transform:open?"rotate(180deg)":"rotate(0deg)", display:"inline-block" }}>▼</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              {open && (
                <div style={{ borderTop:`1px solid ${T.border}`, padding:"14px 16px" }}>
                  {(due||isOverdue) && (()=>{
                    const rs = lineRemind[room.id]||"idle";
                    const sent = rs==="sent";
                    return (
                      <div style={{ background:isOverdue?"#fff7ed":T.redBg, border:`1px solid ${isOverdue?"#ea580c55":T.red+"55"}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 12px", marginBottom:12 }}>
                        <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                          <div style={{ color:isOverdue?"#c2410c":T.red, fontWeight:700, fontSize:13 }}>
                            {isOverdue?`🚨 租金逾期 ${overdueDays} 天（每月 ${room.rentDay} 號繳租）`:`⚠️ 本月租金待繳（每月 ${room.rentDay} 號繳租）`}
                          </div>
                          <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, flexShrink:0 }}>
                            {(isSA||isAdmin)&&(
                              <button onClick={e=>{e.stopPropagation();sendLineReminder(room);}}
                                style={{ background:sent?"#22c55e":"#06b6d4", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:7, padding:"6px 13px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", flexShrink:0, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                                {sent?"✅ 已開啟LINE":"📲 LINE 催繳通知"}
                              </button>
                            )}
                            {role.canEdit&&<button onClick={e=>{e.stopPropagation();markPaid(room);}} style={{ background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:7, padding:"6px 14px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", flexShrink:0, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>已繳租完畢</button>}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    );
                  })()}
                  {room.address&&<div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, marginBottom:8 }}>📍 {room.address}</div>}
                  {(isSA||isAdmin) && (room.tenantContactName||(room.cohabitants||[]).length>0) && (
                    <div style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 12px", marginBottom:10, border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
                      <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:8 }}>👥 租客聯絡資訊</div>
                      {room.tenantContactName&&<div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:(room.cohabitants||[]).length>0?8:0 }}>
                        <div><div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6 }}><span style={{ fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, color:T.text }}>{room.tenantContactName}</span><span style={S.tag(T.blue)}>主租客</span></div>{room.tenantContactPhone&&<div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, marginTop:2 }}>📞 {room.tenantContactPhone}</div>}</div>
                        {room.tenantContactPhone&&<a href={`tel:${room.tenantContactPhone}`} style={{ background:T.greenBg, color:T.green, border:`1px solid ${T.green}44`, borderRadius:7, padding:"5px 10px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, textDecoration:"none" }}>📞</a>}
                      </div>}
                      {(room.cohabitants||[]).map((c,i)=><div key={i} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginTop:6 }}><div><div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, color:T.textSub }}>{c.name} <span style={S.tag(T.textMuted)}>同住人</span></div>{c.phone&&<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub }}>📞 {c.phone}</div>}</div>{c.phone&&<a href={`tel:${c.phone}`} style={{ background:T.greenBg, color:T.green, border:`1px solid ${T.green}44`, borderRadius:7, padding:"4px 9px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, textDecoration:"none" }}>📞</a>}</div>)}
                    </div>
                  )}
                  <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:8, marginBottom:10 }}>
                    {[["月租金",fmt(room.rent)],["繳租日",room.rentDay?`每月 ${room.rentDay} 號`:"—"],["起租日",toROC(room.leaseStart)],["合約到期",toROC(room.contractEnd)],["剩餘天數",dl!==null?`${dl} 天`:"—"]].map(([k,v])=>(
                      <div key={k} style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderRadius:7, padding:"8px 10px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}><div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600, marginBottom:2 }}>{k}</div><div style={{ fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, color:T.text }}>{v}</div></div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                  {(room.renewals||[]).length>0 && <div style={{ marginBottom:10, background:T.accentBg, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}33`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 12px" }}><div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.accent, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:8 }}>🔄 續約記錄</div>{(room.renewals||[]).map((rv,i)=><div key={i} style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, marginBottom:i<room.renewals.length-1?8:0 }}><div style={{ background:T.bg, borderRadius:6, padding:"6px 10px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, flex:1 }}><div style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600, marginBottom:1 }}>第{i+1}次·起租</div><div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, color:T.text }}>{toROC(rv.renewStart)||"—"}</div></div><div style={{ background:T.bg, borderRadius:6, padding:"6px 10px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, flex:1 }}><div style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600, marginBottom:1 }}>第{i+1}次·到期</div><div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, color:T.text }}>{toROC(rv.renewEnd)||"—"}</div></div></div>)}</div>}
                  {/* ── 加租車位展示 ── */}
                  {(room.parkingSpots||[]).length>0&&(()=>{
                    const carSpots  = room.parkingSpots.filter(s=>s.type==="car");
                    const motoSpots = room.parkingSpots.filter(s=>s.type==="moto");
                    const SpotRow = ({spot})=>{
                      const lr = spot.linkedRoomId?(data.rooms||[]).find(r=>r.id===spot.linkedRoomId):null;
                      const dl = spot.contractEnd?daysUntil(spot.contractEnd):null;
                      return (
                        <div style={{ background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:7, padding:"8px 10px", marginBottom:6 }}>
                          <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:4 }}>
                            <span style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:T.text }}>{spot.spotNo||"（未填編號）"}</span>
                            {spot.rent&&<span style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.accent, fontWeight:600 }}>{fmt(spot.rent)}/月</span>}
                          </div>
                          <div style={{ display:"flex", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:6 }}>
                            {lr&&<span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textSub }}>📍 {lr.communityName}{lr.address?` (${lr.address})`:""}</span>}
                            {spot.leaseStart&&<span style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted }}>{toROC(spot.leaseStart)} 起</span>}
                            {spot.contractEnd&&<span style={{ fontSize:11, color:dl!==null&&dl<=30&&dl>=0?T.red:T.textMuted }}>到 {toROC(spot.contractEnd)}{dl!==null?` (${dl}天)`:""}</span>}
                          </div>
                          {(spot.renewals||[]).length>0&&<div style={{ marginTop:4, fontSize:11, color:T.accent }}>🔄 已續約 {spot.renewals.length} 次</div>}
                        </div>
                      );
                    };
                    return (
                      <div style={{ marginBottom:10, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:9, overflow:"hidden" }}>
                        <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.text, padding:"8px 12px", background:T.bgMuted, borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>🅿 加租車位（{room.parkingSpots.length} 個）</div>
                        <div style={{ padding:"10px 12px" }}>
                          {carSpots.length>0&&<><div style={{ fontSize:11, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, marginBottom:6 }}>🚗 汽車車位</div>{carSpots.map(s=><SpotRow key={s.id} spot={s}/>)}</>}
                          {motoSpots.length>0&&<><div style={{ fontSize:11, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, marginTop:carSpots.length>0?8:0, marginBottom:6 }}>🛵 機車車位</div>{motoSpots.map(s=><SpotRow key={s.id} spot={s}/>)}</>}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    );
                  })()}

                  {((room.contractPhotos||[]).length>0||(room.contractPhoto&&!(room.contractPhotos||[]).length)||room.ownerBankPhoto) && <div style={{ marginBottom:10 }}>
                    {(()=>{
                      const photos = room.contractPhotos||(room.contractPhoto?[{id:room.id+"_legacy",dataUrl:room.contractPhoto}]:[]);
                      return photos.length>0&&(
                        <div style={{ marginBottom:8 }}>
                          <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, marginBottom:6 }}>📄 租約電子檔</div>
                          <div style={{ display:"flex", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:6 }}>
                            {photos.map((p,i)=>(
                              <div key={p.id||i} style={{ position:"relative" }}>
                                <img src={p.dataUrl} style={{ width:64, height:64, borderRadius:7, objectFit:"cover", cursor:"pointer", border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }} onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(p.dataUrl)}/>
                                <a href={p.dataUrl} download={`租約電子檔_${i+1}.jpg`} title="下載" style={{ position:"absolute", bottom:3, right:3, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.52)", color:"#fff", borderRadius:4, padding:"2px 5px", fontSize:10, textDecoration:"none", lineHeight:1 }}>⬇</a>
                              </div>
                            ))}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      );
                    })()}
                    {room.ownerBankPhoto&&<div style={{ display:"flex", gap:4 }}>
                      <button onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(room.ownerBankPhoto)} style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:7, padding:"7px", fontSize:13, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>🏦 匯款帳號</button>
                      <a href={room.ownerBankPhoto} download="屋主匯款帳號.jpg" title="下載" style={{ background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:7, padding:"7px 10px", fontSize:13, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", textDecoration:"none" }}>⬇️</a>
                    </div>}
                  </div>}

                  {/* ── 出租點交室內照片（所有人可讀取下載） ── */}
                  {(room.inspectionPhotos||[]).length>0&&(
                    <div style={{ marginBottom:10 }}>
                      <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, marginBottom:8 }}>📷 點交室內照片</div>
                      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:6 }}>
                        {(room.inspectionPhotos||[]).map((p,i)=>(
                          <div key={p.id||i} style={{ position:"relative" }}>
                            <img src={p.dataUrl} style={{ width:64, height:64, borderRadius:7, objectFit:"cover", cursor:"pointer", border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }} onClick={()=>setViewPhoto(p.dataUrl)}/>
                            <a href={p.dataUrl} download={`點交照片_${i+1}.jpg`} title="下載" style={{ position:"absolute", bottom:3, right:3, background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.52)", color:"#fff", borderRadius:4, padding:"2px 5px", fontSize:10, textDecoration:"none", lineHeight:1 }}>⬇</a>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}

                  {/* ── 電費記錄（分租套房） ── */}
                  {room.roomType==="shared"&&(()=>{
                    const readings=(room.meterReadings||[]).slice().sort((a,b)=>a.date.localeCompare(b.date));
                    const rent=Number(room.rent||0);
                    const isMeterOpen=showMeterForm===room.id;
                    const prevReading=readings.length>0?readings[readings.length-1]:null;
                    const draftCur=Number(meterDraft.reading);
                    const draftRate=Number(meterDraft.rate);
                    const previewOk=prevReading&&draftCur>prevReading.reading&&draftRate>0;
                    const previewDiff=previewOk?draftCur-prevReading.reading:0;
                    const previewFee=previewOk?Math.round(previewDiff*draftRate):0;
                    const previewTotal=previewOk?previewFee+rent:0;
                    return (
                      <div style={{ marginBottom:12 }}>
                        <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:8 }}>
                          <span style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub }}>⚡ 電費記錄</span>
                          {(isSA||isAdmin)&&(
                            <button onClick={()=>{ setShowMeterForm(isMeterOpen?null:room.id); setMeterDraft({ date:todayStr(), reading:"", rate:"" }); }}
                              style={{ ...S.btn(T.amber,true), fontSize:11, padding:"3px 10px" }}>
                              {isMeterOpen?"取消":"＋ 新增電表記錄"}
                            </button>
                          )}
                        </div>

                        {isMeterOpen&&(
                          <div style={{ background:"#fffbeb", border:"1.5px solid #fcd34d", borderRadius:9, padding:"12px 13px", marginBottom:10 }}>
                            <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:"#92400e", marginBottom:10 }}>⚡ 新增電表記錄</div>
                            <label style={S.label}>抄表日期</label>
                            <ROCDateInput value={meterDraft.date} onChange={e=>setMeterDraft(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>
                            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8 }}>
                              <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                                <label style={S.label}>本期電表度數（累計）</label>
                                <input type="number" style={S.input} value={meterDraft.reading} onChange={e=>setMeterDraft(f=>({...f,reading:e.target.value}))} placeholder="例：1905"/>
                              </div>
                              <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                                <label style={S.label}>電費單價（元/度）</label>
                                <input type="number" step="0.01" style={{ ...S.input, marginBottom:0 }} value={meterDraft.rate} onChange={e=>setMeterDraft(f=>({...f,rate:e.target.value}))} placeholder="例：3.34"/>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                            {/* 預覽計算 */}
                            {previewOk&&(
                              <div style={{ background:"#fff", border:"1px solid #fcd34d", borderRadius:7, padding:"8px 12px", margin:"8px 0", fontSize:12 }}>
                                <div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:"#92400e", marginBottom:4 }}>📊 本期預覽</div>
                                <div style={{ color:T.textSub }}>用電：{draftCur} − {prevReading.reading} = <strong>{previewDiff} 度</strong></div>
                                <div style={{ color:T.textSub }}>電費：{previewDiff} × {draftRate} = <strong>NT$ {previewFee.toLocaleString()}</strong></div>
                                <div style={{ color:"#d97706", fontWeight:800, marginTop:4, fontSize:13 }}>合計匯款：NT$ {previewTotal.toLocaleString()}</div>
                              </div>
                            )}
                            {prevReading===null&&(
                              <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:"#d97706", marginTop:4, marginBottom:8 }}>📌 首筆記錄為起始度數，不計算電費。</div>
                            )}
                            <button onClick={()=>{
                              if (!meterDraft.reading) return;
                              const r={ id:uid(), date:meterDraft.date||todayStr(), reading:Number(meterDraft.reading), ratePerKwh:Number(meterDraft.rate)||0, createdAt:nowISO() };
                              onUpdate(d=>({ ...d, rooms:d.rooms.map(x=>x.id===room.id?{...x,meterReadings:[...(x.meterReadings||[]),r].sort((a,b)=>a.date.localeCompare(b.date))}:x) }));
                              setShowMeterForm(null);
                            }} style={{ ...S.btn(T.amber), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center" }}>
                              💾 儲存電表記錄
                            </button>
                          </div>
                        )}

                        {readings.length>0?(
                          <div style={{ overflowX:"auto", marginBottom:8, borderRadius:8, border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
                            <table style={{ width:"100%", borderCollapse:"collapse", fontSize:12 }}>
                              <thead>
                                <tr style={{ background:T.bgMuted }}>
                                  {["抄表日期","抄表度數","電費單價","本期電費","租金","合計匯款"].map(h=>(
                                    <th key={h} style={{ padding:"6px 8px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, fontWeight:700, color:T.textSub, textAlign:"center", whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>{h}</th>
                                  ))}
                                  {(isSA||isAdmin)&&<th style={{ padding:"6px 8px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}></th>}
                                </tr>
                              </thead>
                              <tbody>
                                {readings.map((r,i)=>{
                                  const prev=i>0?readings[i-1]:null;
                                  const diff=prev?r.reading-prev.reading:0;
                                  const elecFee=prev?Math.round(diff*r.ratePerKwh):null;
                                  const total=elecFee!==null?elecFee+rent:null;
                                  const isLast=i===readings.length-1;
                                  const c=isLast?"#c2410c":T.text;
                                  const bg=isLast?"#fffbeb":i%2===0?T.bg:T.bgSub;
                                  return (
                                    <tr key={r.id} style={{ background:bg, fontWeight:isLast?700:400 }}>
                                      <td style={{ padding:"5px 8px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, textAlign:"center", color:c }}>{toROC(r.date)}</td>
                                      <td style={{ padding:"5px 8px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, textAlign:"right", color:c }}>{r.reading.toLocaleString()}</td>
                                      <td style={{ padding:"5px 8px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, textAlign:"right", color:c }}>{elecFee!==null?r.ratePerKwh.toFixed(2):"—"}</td>
                                      <td style={{ padding:"5px 8px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, textAlign:"right", color:c }}>{elecFee!==null?elecFee.toLocaleString():"—"}</td>
                                      <td style={{ padding:"5px 8px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, textAlign:"right", color:c }}>{rent.toLocaleString()}</td>
                                      <td style={{ padding:"5px 8px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, textAlign:"right", color:c, fontWeight:isLast?800:600 }}>{total!==null?total.toLocaleString():i===0?"（起始）":"—"}</td>
