```html
        {[{l:"目前出租",v:`${rented.length} 間`,sub:`入住率 ${occ}%`,c:T.green},{l:"空房",v:`${(rooms||[]).filter(r=>r.status==="vacant").length} 間`,sub:`共 ${(rooms||[]).length} 間`,c:T.amber},{l:`${yr-1911}年已收款`,v:fmt(yColl),sub:"全年合計",c:T.blue},{l:`${yr-1911}年未收款`,v:fmt(yUncoll),sub:"全年合計",c:T.red}].map((s,i)=>(
          <div key={i} style={S.card}><div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:4 }}>{s.l}</div><div style={{ fontSize:18, fontWeight:800, color:s.c }}>{s.v}</div><div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2 }}>{s.sub}</div></div>
        ))}
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, marginBottom:12, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
        {[["monthly","月份統計"],["rooms","房源明細"]].map(([k,l])=><button key={k} onClick={()=>setMode(k)} style={{ background:mode===k?T.accent:T.bgMuted, color:mode===k?"#fff":T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${mode===k?T.accent:T.border}`, borderRadius:7, padding:"6px 16px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>{l}</button>)}
      </div>
      {mode==="monthly"&&<div style={{ ...S.card, padding:0, overflow:"hidden" }}>
        <div style={{ padding:"14px 14px 6px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:10 }}>月收租走勢（民國 {yr-1911} 年）</div>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:4, alignItems:"flex-end", height:64 }}>
            {monthly.map((m,i)=>{ const h=maxT>0?Math.max(4,Math.round((m.total/maxT)*60)):4; const hp=maxT>0?Math.round((m.coll/maxT)*60):0; const cur=m.m===new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7); return <div key={i} style={{ flex:1, display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"center", gap:2 }}><div style={{ width:"100%", height:h, borderRadius:"4px 4px 0 0", position:"relative", background:T.bgMuted, overflow:"hidden" }}><div style={{ position:"absolute", bottom:0, width:"100%", height:hp, background:cur?T.blue:T.green+"bb", borderRadius:"4px 4px 0 0" }}/></div><div style={{ fontSize:10, color:cur?T.blue:T.textMuted, fontWeight:cur?700:400 }}>{i+1}月</div></div>; })}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style={{ overflowX:"auto" }}>
          <table style={{ width:"100%", borderCollapse:"collapse", fontSize:13 }}>
            <thead><tr style={{ background:T.bgSub }}>{["月份","出租間數","已收租金","未收租金","合計"].map(h=><th key={h} style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:h==="月份"?"left":"right", color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, fontSize:11, borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>{h}</th>)}</tr></thead>
            <tbody>{monthly.map((m,i)=>{ const cur=m.m===new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7); return <tr key={i} style={{ background:cur?T.accentBg:"transparent", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", color:cur?T.accent:T.text, fontWeight:cur?700:500 }}>{i+1} 月{cur&&<span style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.accent, marginLeft:4 }}>●本月</span>}</td><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.text, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.roomCount} 間</td><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:"right", color:m.coll>0?T.green:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.coll>0?fmt(m.coll):"—"}</td><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:"right", color:m.uncoll>0?T.red:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.uncoll>0?fmt(m.uncoll):"—"}</td><td style={{ padding:"9px 10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.text, fontWeight:700 }}>{m.total>0?fmt(m.total):"—"}</td></tr>; })}</tbody>
            <tfoot><tr style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderTop:`2px solid ${T.borderMd}` }}><td style={{ padding:"10px", fontWeight:800, color:T.text }}>全年合計</td><td style={{ padding:"10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.textSub }}>—</td><td style={{ padding:"10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.green, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(yColl)}</td><td style={{ padding:"10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.red, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(yUncoll)}</td><td style={{ padding:"10px", textAlign:"right", color:T.accent, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(yColl+yUncoll)}</td></tr></tfoot>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>}
      {mode==="rooms"&&<div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:8 }}>{(rooms||[]).map(r=>{ const yb=(bills||[]).filter(b=>b.roomId===r.id&&b.month?.startsWith(yrStr)); const rc=yb.filter(b=>b.status==="paid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0); const ru=yb.filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0),0); return <div key={r.id} style={S.card}><div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"flex-start", marginBottom:8 }}><div><div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{r.communityName}</div>{r.address&&<div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, marginTop:1 }}>📍 {r.address}</div>}</div><span style={S.tag(r.status==="rented"?T.green:T.amber)}>{r.status==="rented"?"已出租":"空房"}</span></div><div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr 1fr", gap:6 }}>{[["月租金",fmt(r.rent),T.text],[`${yr-1911}年已收`,fmt(rc),T.green],[`${yr-1911}年未收`,fmt(ru),T.red]].map(([l,v,c])=><div key={l} style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderRadius:7, padding:"7px 8px", border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}><div style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.textMuted, fontWeight:700 }}>{l}</div><div style={{ fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:c, marginTop:2 }}>{v}</div></div>)}</div></div>; })}</div>}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  USER MANAGEMENT
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function UserManagement({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const [showAdd, setShowAdd] = useState(false);
  const [confirmDel, setConfirmDel] = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ name:"", email:"", password:"", role:"viewer" });
  const save = async () => {
    if(!form.name||!form.email) return;
    const rawPw = form.password || form.email;
    const hashedPw = await sha256(rawPw);
    const nu={id:uid(),...form,password:hashedPw,avatar:form.name[0],online:false,lastSeen:null};
    onUpdate(d=>({...d,users:[...d.users,nu],activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`新增使用者 ${form.name}`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}));
    setShowAdd(false); setForm({name:"",email:"",password:"",role:"viewer"});
  };
  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:16 }}>
        <h2 style={S.title}>人員管理</h2>
        <button onClick={()=>setShowAdd(true)} style={S.btn()}><Icon n="plus" s={13}/> 新增人員</button>
      </div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10 }}>
        {(data.users||[]).map(u=>(
          <div key={u.id} style={{ ...S.card, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:12 }}>
            <AvatarBadge user={u} size={40}/>
            <div style={{ flex:1 }}><div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6 }}><span style={{ fontWeight:600, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>{u.name}</span>{u.id===currentUser.id&&<span style={S.tag(T.blue)}>我</span>}</div><div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, marginTop:2 }}>{u.email}</div></div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"flex-end", gap:6 }}>
              <span style={S.tag(safeRole(u.role).color)}>{safeRole(u.role).label}</span>
              {u.id!==currentUser.id&&<>
                <select value={u.role} onChange={e=>onUpdate(d=>({...d,users:d.users.map(x=>x.id===u.id?{...x,role:e.target.value}:x),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`變更 ${u.name} 權限為 ${safeRole(e.target.value).label}`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}))} style={{ background:T.bg, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:6, padding:"3px 8px", fontSize:13, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>{Object.entries(ROLES).filter(([k])=>k!=="system"&&k!=="staff").map(([k,v])=><option key={k} value={k}>{v.label}</option>)}</select>
                <button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(u)} style={{ background:T.redBg, color:T.red, border:`1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius:6, padding:"4px 10px", fontSize:13, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:4, fontFamily:"inherit" }}><Icon n="trash" s={12}/> 刪除</button>
              </>}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
      {confirmDel&&<Modal title="確認刪除使用者" onClose={()=>setConfirmDel(null)} width={360}><div style={{ textAlign:"center", padding:"8px 0 16px" }}><div style={{ width:52, height:52, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.redBg, border:`2px solid ${T.red}44`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", margin:"0 auto 14px", color:T.red }}><Icon n="trash" s={22}/></div><div style={{ color:T.text, fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:8 }}>刪除「{confirmDel.name}」？</div><div style={{ color:T.textSub, fontSize:14, lineHeight:1.6, marginBottom:20 }}>此操作無法復原。</div><div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}><button onClick={()=>setConfirmDel(null)} style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button><button onClick={()=>{onUpdate(d=>({...d,users:d.users.filter(x=>x.id!==confirmDel.id),activityLog:[...d.activityLog,{id:uid(),userId:currentUser.id,action:`刪除使用者 ${confirmDel.name}`,timestamp:nowISO()}]}));setConfirmDel(null);}} style={{ flex:1, background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>確認刪除</button></div></div></Modal>}
      {showAdd&&<Modal title="新增人員" onClose={()=>setShowAdd(false)}>{[["name","姓名"],["email","Email"],["password","密碼"]].map(([k,l])=><div key={k}><label style={S.label}>{l}</label><input style={S.input} type={k==="password"?"password":"text"} value={form[k]} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,[k]:e.target.value}))}/></div>)}<label style={S.label}>權限角色</label><select style={S.input} value={form.role} onChange={e=>setForm(f=>({...f,role:e.target.value}))}>{Object.entries(ROLES).filter(([k])=>k!=="system"&&k!=="staff").map(([k,v])=><option key={k} value={k}>{v.label}</option>)}</select><button onClick={save} style={{ ...S.btn(), width:"100%", justifyContent:"center", padding:11 }}>確認新增</button></Modal>}
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  ACTIVITY LOG
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function ActivityLog({ data, currentUser, onUpdate }) {
  const { activityLog, users, bills, rooms, repairs } = data;
  const isSA    = isSARole(currentUser?.role);
  const isAdmin = currentUser?.role === "admin";
  const canExportLog = isSA || isAdmin;

  const thisYear = new Date().getFullYear();
  const [confirmClear,     setConfirmClear]     = useState(false);
  const [confirmExportLog, setConfirmExportLog] = useState(false);
  const [showPL,           setShowPL]           = useState(false);
  const [plYear,           setPlYear]           = useState(thisYear);
  const [pendingImport,    setPendingImport]    = useState(null); // { data, meta }
  const importFileRef                           = useRef(null);

  // ── 年度損益計算 ──────────────────────────────────────
  const plBillYears = [...new Set((bills||[]).map(b=>b.month?.slice(0,4)).filter(Boolean).map(Number))];
  const plYears = [...new Set([...plBillYears, thisYear-1, thisYear])].sort((a,b)=>b-a);

  const buildPLData = (yr) => {
    return Array.from({ length: 12 }, (_, i) => {
      const mo = `${yr}-${String(i+1).padStart(2,"0")}`;
      const mb = (bills||[]).filter(b => b.month === mo);
      const collected   = mb.filter(b=>b.status==="paid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0), 0);
      const uncollected = mb.filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").reduce((s,b)=>s+(b.amount||0), 0);
      const expected    = collected + uncollected;
      const rate        = expected > 0 ? Math.round((collected/expected)*100) : null;
      const roomIds     = [...new Set(mb.map(b=>b.roomId))];
      const repairCnt   = (repairs||[]).filter(r => {
        const d = r.date||"";
        return d.startsWith(mo) && roomIds.includes(r.roomId);
      }).length;
      return { mo, roomCount: roomIds.length, expected, collected, uncollected, rate, repairCnt };
    });
  };

  const plMonthly = buildPLData(plYear);
  const plTotalExpected    = plMonthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.expected, 0);
  const plTotalCollected   = plMonthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.collected, 0);
  const plTotalUncollected = plMonthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.uncollected, 0);
  const plAvgRate          = plTotalExpected > 0 ? Math.round((plTotalCollected/plTotalExpected)*100) : null;

  // ── 匯出損益表 CSV ────────────────────────────────────
  const exportPLCSV = () => {
    const rocYr = plYear - 1911;
    const header = ["月份","出租間數","應收租金(NT$)","已收租金(NT$)","未收租金(NT$)","收租率(%)","報修筆數"];
    const rows = plMonthly.map((m, i) => [
      csvEsc(`${rocYr}年${i+1}月`), csvEsc(m.roomCount||0), csvEsc(m.expected), csvEsc(m.collected), csvEsc(m.uncollected),
      m.rate!=null?csvEsc(m.rate+"%"):csvEsc("—"), csvEsc(m.repairCnt),
    ]);
    const totalRow = [
      csvEsc("全年合計"), csvEsc("—"), csvEsc(plTotalExpected), csvEsc(plTotalCollected), csvEsc(plTotalUncollected),
      plAvgRate!=null?csvEsc(plAvgRate+"%"):csvEsc("—"), csvEsc(plMonthly.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.repairCnt,0)),
    ];
    const lines = [
      csvEsc(`家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司　民國 ${rocYr} 年度損益表`),
      csvEsc(`製表日期：${toROC(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10))}　製表人：${currentUser?.name||""}`),
      "",
      header.map(csvEsc).join(","),
      ...rows.map(r=>r.join(",")),
      totalRow.join(","),
    ];
    downloadCSV(`家樂美_${rocYr}年度損益表.csv`, "\uFEFF"+lines.join("\n"));
    onUpdate(d => ({
      ...d,
      activityLog: [...d.activityLog, { id:uid(), userId:currentUser?.id, action:`匯出民國 ${rocYr} 年度損益表 CSV`, timestamp:nowISO() }],
    }));
  };

  const exportLogCSV = () => {
    const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    const header = ["時間","操作人員","角色","操作內容"].map(csvEsc).join(",");
    const rows = [...(activityLog||[])]
      .sort((a,b)=>new Date(a.timestamp)-new Date(b.timestamp))
      .map(log => {
        const u = (users||[]).find(u=>u.id===log.userId);
        return [csvEsc(toROC(log.timestamp,true)), csvEsc(u?.name||"系統"), csvEsc(u?safeRole(u.role).label:"—"), csvEsc(log.action)].join(",");
      });
    downloadCSV(`家樂美_操作記錄_${today}.csv`, "\uFEFF"+[header,...rows].join("\n"));
    onUpdate(d=>({...d, activityLog:[{ id:uid(), userId:currentUser?.id, action:`匯出操作記錄 CSV（共 ${(activityLog||[]).length} 筆），並清空記錄`, timestamp:new Date().toISOString() }]}));
    setConfirmExportLog(false);
  };

  // ── 匯入系統備份（JSON）────────────────────────────────
  const handleImportFile = (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    e.target.value = "";
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (ev) => {
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(ev.target.result);
        if (!parsed._rentkeeper || !Array.isArray(parsed.users) || !Array.isArray(parsed.rooms)) {
          showToast("檔案格式不正確，非 RentKeeper 備份檔", "error");
          return;
        }
        setPendingImport({
          data: parsed,
          meta: {
            backupTime: parsed._backupTime || "未知",
            rooms: (parsed.rooms||[]).length,
            tenants: (parsed.tenants||[]).length,
            users: (parsed.users||[]).length,
            bills: (parsed.bills||[]).length,
            repairs: (parsed.repairs||[]).length,
            fileName: file.name,
          },
        });
      } catch (err) {
        showToast("無法解析備份檔："+err.message, "error");
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file, "utf-8");
  };

  const confirmImportBackup = () => {
    if (!pendingImport) return;
    const { _backupTime, _rentkeeper, ...clean } = pendingImport.data;
    onUpdate(() => ({
      ...clean,
      activityLog: [
        ...(clean.activityLog || []),
        { id: uid(), userId: currentUser?.id || "system",
          action: `匯入系統備份還原資料（${pendingImport.meta.fileName}，備份時間：${pendingImport.meta.backupTime.slice(0,19).replace("T"," ")}）`,
          timestamp: nowISO() },
      ],
    }));
    setPendingImport(null);
    showToast("已還原備份資料！", "success");
  };

  // ── 匯出系統備份（JSON）────────────────────────────────
  const exportBackup = () => {
    const ts   = new Date().toISOString();
    const snap = { ...data, _backupTime: ts, _rentkeeper: true };
    const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(snap, null, 2)], { type: "application/json" });
    const url  = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a    = document.createElement("a");
    a.href     = url;
    a.download = `RentKeeper_備份_${ts.slice(0, 10)}.json`;
    document.body.appendChild(a); a.click();
    document.body.removeChild(a); URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    onUpdate(d => ({
      ...d,
      activityLog: [...d.activityLog, {
        id: uid(), userId: currentUser?.id || "system",
        action: "手動匯出系統備份檔案",
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      }],
    }));
  };

  const logCount = (activityLog || []).length;

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:16 }}>
        <h2 style={{ ...S.title, marginBottom:0 }}>操作記錄</h2>
        <span style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub }}>共 <strong style={{ color:T.text }}>{logCount}</strong> 筆</span>
      </div>

      {/* ── 操作按鈕區 ── */}
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:10, marginBottom:20 }}>

        {/* 年度損益表 + 一鍵匯出記錄（管理員 + 後台維修） */}
        {canExportLog && (
          <button onClick={()=>setShowPL(true)}
            style={{ width:"100%", background:"#7c3aed", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:12, padding:"13px 16px", fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:8, fontFamily:"inherit", boxShadow:"0 4px 12px #7c3aed44" }}>
            📊 匯出年度損益表
          </button>
        )}
        {canExportLog && (
          <button onClick={()=>setConfirmExportLog(true)}
            style={{ width:"100%", background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:12, padding:"13px 16px", fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:8, fontFamily:"inherit", boxShadow:`0 4px 12px ${T.green}44` }}>
            📋 一鍵匯出操作記錄（CSV）
          </button>
        )}

        {/* 備份 / 還原 / 清空（僅後台維修） */}
        {isSA && (
          <>
            <div style={{ background:T.accentBg, border:`1.5px solid ${T.accent}44`, borderRadius:10, padding:"10px 12px", marginBottom:2, fontSize:12, color:T.text, lineHeight:1.6 }}>
              <div style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, marginBottom:4 }}>💾 資料備份建議</div>
              建議每次新增大量房源後，點「⬇ 匯出系統備份」下載 JSON 檔；若遇到資料消失（清快取、換裝置、空間不足），可點「⬆ 匯入備份」一鍵還原。
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}>
              <button onClick={exportBackup}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.accent, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:10, padding:"11px 8px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:6, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                ⬇ 匯出系統備份
              </button>
              <input ref={importFileRef} type="file" accept=".json,application/json" style={{ display:"none" }} onChange={handleImportFile}/>
              <button onClick={()=>importFileRef.current?.click()}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:10, padding:"11px 8px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:6, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                ⬆ 匯入備份
              </button>
              <button onClick={()=>setConfirmClear(true)}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.bg, color:T.red, border:`1px solid ${T.red}44`, borderRadius:10, padding:"11px 8px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:6, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                🗑 清空記錄
              </button>
            </div>
          </>
        )}

        {/* 權限說明 */}
        {!canExportLog && (
          <div style={{ ...S.card, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, padding:"12px 16px" }}>
            <Icon n="lock" s={16}/>
            <span style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub }}>您的身份無法匯出或清空記錄</span>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* ── 年度損益表 Modal ── */}
      {showPL && (
        <Modal title="年度損益表" onClose={()=>setShowPL(false)} width={600}>
          <div style={{ paddingBottom:8 }}>
            {/* 年份選擇器 */}
            <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:14 }}>
              <div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700 }}>家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2 }}>製表日期：{toROC(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10))}</div>
              </div>
              <select value={plYear} onChange={e=>setPlYear(Number(e.target.value))}
                style={{ background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.borderMd}`, borderRadius:8, color:T.text, padding:"6px 10px", fontSize:13, outline:"none", cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                {plYears.map(y=><option key={y} value={y}>民國 {y-1911} 年</option>)}
              </select>
            </div>

            {/* 統計卡片 */}
            <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:8, marginBottom:14 }}>
              {[
                { l:"全年應收租金",   v:fmt(plTotalExpected),    c:"#7c3aed", sub:"已收＋未收合計" },
                { l:"全年已收租金",   v:fmt(plTotalCollected),   c:T.green,   sub:`佔應收 ${plAvgRate!=null?plAvgRate+"%" : "—"}` },
                { l:"全年未收租金",   v:fmt(plTotalUncollected), c:T.red,     sub:"尚未繳清款項" },
                { l:"全年收租率",     v:plAvgRate!=null?`${plAvgRate}%`:"—", c:plAvgRate>=90?T.green:plAvgRate>=70?T.amber:T.red, sub:"按已收/應收計算" },
              ].map((s,i)=>(
                <div key={i} style={{ background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:10, padding:"11px 12px" }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700 }}>{s.l}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:17, fontWeight:800, color:s.c, margin:"4px 0 2px" }}>{s.v}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted }}>{s.sub}</div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            {/* 月份明細表 */}
            <div style={{ overflowX:"auto", borderRadius:8, border:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
              <table style={{ width:"100%", borderCollapse:"collapse", fontSize:12 }}>
                <thead>
                  <tr style={{ background:T.bgSub }}>
                    {["月份","間數","應收","已收","未收","收租率"].map(h=>(
                      <th key={h} style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:h==="月份"?"left":"right", color:T.textSub, fontWeight:700, fontSize:11, borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>{h}</th>
                    ))}
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody>
                  {plMonthly.map((m,i)=>{
                    const isCur = m.mo === new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);
                    const hasData = m.expected > 0;
                    return (
                      <tr key={i} style={{ background:isCur?T.accentBg:"transparent", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}` }}>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", color:isCur?T.accent:T.text, fontWeight:isCur?700:500, whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>
                          {i+1} 月{isCur&&<span style={{ fontSize:10, color:T.accent, marginLeft:4 }}>●</span>}
                        </td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:hasData?T.text:T.textMuted }}>{hasData?`${m.roomCount} 間`:"—"}</td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:hasData?T.text:T.textMuted, fontWeight:500 }}>{hasData?fmt(m.expected):"—"}</td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:m.collected>0?T.green:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.collected>0?fmt(m.collected):"—"}</td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:m.uncollected>0?T.red:T.textMuted, fontWeight:600 }}>{m.uncollected>0?fmt(m.uncollected):"—"}</td>
                        <td style={{ padding:"8px 8px", textAlign:"right" }}>
                          {m.rate!=null
                            ? <span style={{ color:m.rate>=90?T.green:m.rate>=70?T.amber:T.red, fontWeight:700 }}>{m.rate}%</span>
                            : <span style={{ color:T.textMuted }}>—</span>
                          }
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    );
                  })}
                </tbody>
                <tfoot>
                  <tr style={{ background:T.bgSub, borderTop:`2px solid ${T.borderMd}` }}>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", fontWeight:800, color:T.text }}>全年合計</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:T.textMuted }}>—</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:T.text, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(plTotalExpected)}</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:T.green, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(plTotalCollected)}</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:T.red, fontWeight:800 }}>{fmt(plTotalUncollected)}</td>
                    <td style={{ padding:"9px 8px", textAlign:"right", color:plAvgRate>=90?T.green:plAvgRate>=70?T.amber:T.red, fontWeight:800 }}>
                      {plAvgRate!=null?`${plAvgRate}%`:"—"}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                </tfoot>
              </table>
            </div>

            {/* 備註 */}
            <div style={{ marginTop:10, padding:"8px 12px", background:T.bgMuted, borderRadius:8, fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, lineHeight:1.6 }}>
              ⚠️ 備註：本損益表以帳單紀錄計算，應收 = 已收 ＋ 未收，收租率 = 已收 ÷ 應收。匯出為 CSV 可直接用 Excel 開啟。
            </div>

            {/* 匯出按鈕 */}
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10, marginTop:14 }}>
              <button onClick={()=>setShowPL(false)}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                關閉
              </button>
              <button onClick={exportPLCSV}
                style={{ flex:2, background:"#7c3aed", color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:6 }}>
                ⬇ 下載 CSV（可用 Excel 開啟）
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      )}

      {/* ── 確認匯出記錄對話框 ── */}
      {confirmExportLog && (
        <Modal title="確認匯出並清空記錄" onClose={()=>setConfirmExportLog(false)} width={360}>
          <div style={{ padding:"4px 0 16px" }}>
            <div style={{ background:T.accentBg, border:`1px solid ${T.accent}33`, borderRadius:10, padding:"14px", marginBottom:14 }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, color:T.accent, marginBottom:6 }}>📋 匯出操作記錄</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub, lineHeight:1.7 }}>
                將匯出 <strong style={{ color:T.text }}>{logCount} 筆</strong> 記錄為 CSV 檔案，<br/>
                可直接用 Excel 開啟。<br/>
                <span style={{ color:T.amber, fontWeight:600 }}>匯出完成後記錄將自動清空。</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}>
              <button onClick={()=>setConfirmExportLog(false)}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                取消
              </button>
              <button onClick={exportLogCSV}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                確認匯出並清空
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      )}

      {/* ── 確認清空對話框 ── */}
      {confirmClear && (
        <Modal title="確認清空記錄" onClose={()=>setConfirmClear(false)} width={360}>
          <div style={{ padding:"4px 0 16px" }}>
            <div style={{ background:T.redBg, border:`1px solid ${T.red}33`, borderRadius:8, padding:"12px 14px", marginBottom:14 }}>
              <div style={{ color:T.red, fontWeight:700, fontSize:13, marginBottom:4 }}>⚠️ 清空後無法復原</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub }}>目前共 <strong>{logCount}</strong> 筆記錄，清空後僅保留本次操作記錄。</div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}>
              <button onClick={()=>setConfirmClear(false)}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                取消
              </button>
              <button onClick={()=>{ onUpdate(d=>({...d,activityLog:[{id:uid(),userId:currentUser?.id,action:`清空操作記錄（共 ${logCount} 筆）`,timestamp:new Date().toISOString()}]})); setConfirmClear(false); }}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                確認清空
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      )}

      {/* ── 確認匯入備份對話框 ── */}
      {pendingImport && (
        <Modal title="確認匯入備份" onClose={()=>setPendingImport(null)} width={420}>
          <div style={{ padding:"4px 0 16px" }}>
            <div style={{ background:"#fff7ed", border:"1px solid #fb923c55", borderRadius:8, padding:"12px 14px", marginBottom:14 }}>
              <div style={{ color:"#c2410c", fontWeight:700, fontSize:13, marginBottom:6 }}>⚠️ 將覆蓋目前所有資料</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, lineHeight:1.7 }}>
                備份時間：<strong>{pendingImport.meta.backupTime.slice(0,19).replace("T"," ")}</strong><br/>
                檔名：{pendingImport.meta.fileName}
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ background:T.bgSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px 14px", marginBottom:14, fontSize:13, color:T.text, lineHeight:1.8 }}>
              房源：<strong>{pendingImport.meta.rooms}</strong> 筆　|　租客：<strong>{pendingImport.meta.tenants}</strong><br/>
              帳單：<strong>{pendingImport.meta.bills}</strong>　|　修繕：<strong>{pendingImport.meta.repairs}</strong>　|　使用者：<strong>{pendingImport.meta.users}</strong>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}>
              <button onClick={()=>setPendingImport(null)}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                取消
              </button>
              <button onClick={confirmImportBackup}
                style={{ flex:1, background:T.green, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"11px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                確認還原
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      )}

      {/* ── 記錄列表 ── */}
      <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:8 }}>
        {logCount === 0 && (
          <div style={{ textAlign:"center", color:T.textSub, padding:"32px 0", fontSize:14 }}>目前沒有操作記錄</div>
        )}
        {[...(activityLog || [])].reverse().map(log => {
          const u  = (users || []).find(u => u.id === log.userId);
          const lr = u ? safeRole(u.role) : null;
          return (
            <div key={log.id} style={{ ...S.card, display:"flex", gap:10, alignItems:"flex-start" }}>
              {u
                ? <AvatarBadge user={u} size={30}/>
                : <div style={{ width:30, height:30, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.bgMuted, flexShrink:0, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:13 }}>⚙</div>
              }
              <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.text, lineHeight:1.5 }}>
                  <span style={{ color:lr?lr.color:T.textSub, fontWeight:600 }}>{u?.name || "系統"}</span>
                  {" "}{log.action}
                </div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textMuted, marginTop:2 }}>{toROC(log.timestamp, true)}</div>
              </div>
              {u && <span style={S.tag(lr ? lr.color : T.textMuted)}>{lr ? lr.badge : "◆"}</span>}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  MAIN APP
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function RentKeeperApp() {
  const [data, setData] = useState(null);
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null);
  const [tab, setTab]   = useState("dashboard");
  const [toast, setToast] = useState(null);
  const [syncing, setSyncing] = useState(false);
  const [notifications, setNotifications] = useState([]);
  const [showNotif, setShowNotif] = useState(false);
  const [showReset, setShowReset] = useState(false);
  const [viewAs, setViewAs]           = useState(null); // null | "admin" | "viewer"
  const [showViewAsPicker, setShowViewAsPicker] = useState(false);
  const mounted      = useRef(true);
  const lastActivity = useRef(Date.now());

  useEffect(() => {
    mounted.current = true;
    return () => { mounted.current = false; };
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    (async () => {
      let d = await loadData();
      if (d) {
        d = await migratePasswords(d);
        const existingIds = new Set((d.users||[]).map(u => u.id));
        const missingUsers = DEFAULT_DATA.users.filter(u => !existingIds.has(u.id));
        if (missingUsers.length) d = { ...d, users: [...d.users, ...missingUsers] };
        if (!d._nameSwapV1) {
          d = { ...d, users: (d.users||[]).map(u => {
            if (u.id === "u4" && u.name === "憲哥")   return { ...u, name:"管理員", avatar:"管" };
            if (u.id === "u6" && u.name === "管理員") return { ...u, name:"憲哥", avatar:"憲" };
            return u;
          }), _nameSwapV1: true };
        }
        await saveData(d);
        // 啟動時自動複製一份到次要備份鍵（救援用）
        if ((d.rooms||[]).length > 0) { try { await saveBaseline(d); } catch {} }
      } else {
        // 主資料不存在時，嘗試從次要備份還原
        const fallback = await loadBaseline();
        if (fallback && (fallback.rooms||[]).length > 0) {
          d = fallback;
          await saveData(d);
        } else {
          d = DEFAULT_DATA;
          await saveData(d);
        }
      }
      setData(d);
    })();
  }, []);

  const showToast = useCallback((msg, type="ok") => {
    if (!mounted.current) return;
    setToast({ msg, type });
    setTimeout(() => { if (mounted.current) setToast(null); }, 2500);
  }, []);

  const updateData = useCallback((fn) => {
    setData(prev => {
      const next = fn(prev);
      if (!next) return prev; // 防守 fn 回傳 null/undefined
      (async () => { await saveData(next); if (mounted.current) { setSyncing(false); showToast("已儲存"); } })();
      return next;
    });
    setSyncing(true);
  }, [showToast]);

  const handleLogin = (u) => {
    setUser(u);
    setData(d => {
      if (!d) return d;
      // viewer 是 synthetic user，不一定存在於 users 陣列，僅更新存在的帳號
      const updUsers = d.users.some(x => x.id === u.id)
        ? d.users.map(x => x.id===u.id?{...x,online:true}:x)
        : d.users;
      const upd = { ...d, users: updUsers, activityLog: [...d.activityLog, {id:uid(),userId:u.id,action:"登入系統",timestamp:nowISO()}] };
      saveData(upd);
      return upd;
    });
    showToast(`歡迎，${u.name}！`);
  };

  const handleLogout = () => {
    setData(d => {
      if (!d) return d;
      const upd = { ...d, users: d.users.map(x => x.id===user.id?{...x,online:false}:x) };
      saveData(upd);
      return upd;
    });
    setUser(null); setTab("dashboard"); setNotifications([]); setSyncing(false); setViewAs(null); setShowViewAsPicker(false);
  };

  const handleReset = async () => {
    const bl = await loadBaseline();
    const target = bl || DEFAULT_DATA;
    await saveData(target);
    setData(target); setUser(null); setTab("dashboard"); setShowReset(false);
  };

  const handleSaveBaseline = async () => {
    const snap = { ...data, users: data.users.map(u=>({...u,online:false})) };
    await saveBaseline(snap); await saveData(snap);
    showToast("✅ 已儲存為預設版本！");
  };

  // ── 閒置自動登出（60 分鐘）────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!user) return;
    const SESSION_TIMEOUT = 60 * 60 * 1000;
    const touch = () => { lastActivity.current = Date.now(); };
    window.addEventListener("mousemove", touch);
    window.addEventListener("keydown",   touch);
    window.addEventListener("click",     touch);
    window.addEventListener("touchstart",touch);
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
      if (mounted.current && Date.now() - lastActivity.current > SESSION_TIMEOUT) {
        handleLogout();
        setTimeout(() => showToast("閒置超過 60 分鐘，已自動登出", "warn"), 100);
      }
    }, 60000);
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener("mousemove", touch);
      window.removeEventListener("keydown",   touch);
      window.removeEventListener("click",     touch);
      window.removeEventListener("touchstart",touch);
      clearInterval(timer);
    };
  }, [user]); // eslint-disable-line

  // ── 押金退還 → 到期自動退租（每次資料更新都檢查一次）────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!data) return;
    const now = Date.now();
    const toEvict = (data.rooms||[]).filter(r =>
      r.depositRefundStatus === "refunded" &&
      r.depositEvictionAt &&
      new Date(r.depositEvictionAt).getTime() <= now &&
      !r.depositEvictionDone
    );
    if (!toEvict.length) return;
    const evictIds = new Set(toEvict.map(r => r.id));
    const removeIds = new Set();
    toEvict.forEach(r => {
      (data.tenants||[])
        .filter(t => t.roomId === r.id || t.linkedRoom === r.id)
        .forEach(t => {
          const hasOther = (data.rooms||[]).some(rm =>
            rm.id !== r.id && !evictIds.has(rm.id) &&
            (rm.tenantId === t.id || t.roomId === rm.id || t.linkedRoom === rm.id)
          );
          if (!hasOther) removeIds.add(t.id);
        });
    });
    const updRooms = (data.rooms||[]).map(r =>
      evictIds.has(r.id)
        ? { ...r, depositEvictionDone:true, status:"vacant", tenantId:null, tenantContactName:"", tenantContactPhone:"", cohabitants:[] }
        : r
    );
    const updTenants = (data.tenants||[]).filter(t => !removeIds.has(t.id));
    const logs = toEvict.map(r => ({ id:uid(), userId:"system", action:`【自動退租】「${r.communityName}」押金退還完畢，租客已連動退出系統`, timestamp:nowISO() }));
    const next = { ...data, rooms:updRooms, tenants:updTenants, activityLog:[...(data.activityLog||[]), ...logs] };
    setData(next);
    (async()=>{ await saveData(next); })();
  }, [(data?.rooms||[]).map(r=>r.id+r.depositEvictionDone+r.depositEvictionAt).join()]); // eslint-disable-line

  if (!data) return <div style={{ minHeight:"100vh", background:T.bgSub, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", color:T.textSub, fontSize:14, fontFamily:"'Noto Sans TC',sans-serif" }}>載入中...</div>;
  if (!user)  return <LoginScreen users={data.users} tenants={data.tenants} onLogin={handleLogin}/>;

  const role         = safeRole(user.role);
  const effectiveUser = viewAs ? { ...user, role: viewAs } : user;
  const effectiveRole = safeRole(effectiveUser.role);
  const isImpersonating = viewAs !== null;
  const switchOptions = isSARole(user.role)
    ? [{ role:"admin",   label:"管理員視角",       color:T.blue },
       { role:"viewer",  label:"租客視角（唯讀）", color:T.textMuted }]
    : user.role === "admin"
    ? [{ role:"viewer",  label:"租客視角（唯讀）", color:T.textMuted }]
    : [];
  const unpaidCnt = (data.bills||[]).filter(b=>b.status==="unpaid").length;
  const repairCnt = (data.repairs||[]).filter(r=>r.status==="pending").length;

  const ALL_TABS = [
    {id:"dashboard",label:"總覽",icon:"chart"},
    {id:"rooms",    label:"房源",icon:"building"},
    {id:"tenants",  label:"房客",icon:"users"},
    {id:"bills",    label:"帳務",icon:"dollar",badge:unpaidCnt},
    {id:"repairs",  label:"報修",icon:"tool",badge:repairCnt},
    {id:"report",   label:"報表",icon:"file"},
    {id:"users",    label:"人員",icon:"shield"},
    {id:"log",      label:"記錄",icon:"activity"},
  ];
  const tabs = ALL_TABS.filter(t=>effectiveRole.pages.includes(t.id));
  const active = effectiveRole.pages.includes(tab)?tab:(tabs[0]?.id||"dashboard");

  return (
    <div style={{ minHeight:"100vh", background:T.bgSub, fontFamily:"'Noto Sans TC','PingFang TC',sans-serif", color:T.text, fontSize:15 }}>
      <style>{`@keyframes pulse{0%,100%{opacity:1}50%{opacity:.4}} @keyframes flash-alert-border{0%,100%{box-shadow:0 0 0 0 rgba(239,68,68,0)}50%{box-shadow:0 0 0 4px rgba(239,68,68,0.55)}} @keyframes warn-blink{0%,100%{background:#ea580c;box-shadow:0 0 0 rgba(234,88,12,0)}50%{background:#c2410c;box-shadow:0 0 12px rgba(234,88,12,0.7)}} *{box-sizing:border-box} select option{background:#fff;color:#111827} @media print{body>*:not(#print-contract){display:none!important} #print-contract{display:block!important;position:fixed;inset:0;background:#fff;padding:24px;z-index:99999}}`}</style>

      {/* Header（上方橫幅：公司名稱 + 通知鈴鐺 + 登出） */}
      <div style={{ background:T.bg, borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, padding:"10px 16px", display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", position:"sticky", top:0, zIndex:200 }}>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:10 }}>
          <JRMLogo s={32}/>
          <span style={{ fontWeight:800, fontSize:13, color:T.text }}>家樂美房產管理顧問有限公司</span>
          {syncing&&<div style={{ width:6, height:6, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.amber, animation:"pulse 1s infinite" }}/>}
        </div>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8 }}>
          <button onClick={()=>{setShowNotif(v=>!v);setNotifications(n=>n.map(x=>({...x,read:true})));}} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", color:T.textSub, padding:4, position:"relative" }}>
            <Icon n="bell" s={20}/>
            {notifications.some(n=>!n.read)&&<div style={{ position:"absolute", top:2, right:2, width:8, height:8, background:T.red, borderRadius:"50%", border:`2px solid ${T.bg}`, animation:"pulse 1.5s infinite" }}/>}
          </button>
          <button onClick={handleLogout} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", color:T.textSub, padding:4 }}><Icon n="logout" s={18}/></button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Notification Panel */}
      {showNotif&&<div style={{ position:"fixed", top:52, right:0, width:"min(320px,100vw)", maxHeight:"60vh", background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:"0 0 0 14px", zIndex:300, overflow:"hidden", display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", boxShadow:"0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)" }}>
        <div style={{ padding:"12px 14px 10px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center" }}>
          <span style={{ fontWeight:700, color:T.text, fontSize:14 }}>🔔 對話通知</span>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8 }}>{notifications.length>0&&<button onClick={()=>setNotifications([])} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", color:T.textSub, fontSize:13, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>清除全部</button>}<button onClick={()=>setShowNotif(false)} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", color:T.textSub, cursor:"pointer" }}><Icon n="x" s={16}/></button></div>
        </div>
        <div style={{ overflowY:"auto", flex:1 }}>
          {notifications.length===0?<div style={{ padding:28, textAlign:"center", color:T.textMuted, fontSize:13 }}>目前沒有新通知</div>
            :notifications.map(n=>{const mr=safeRole(n.senderRole); return <div key={n.id} onClick={()=>{setShowNotif(false);setTab("rooms");}} style={{ padding:"10px 14px", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, cursor:"pointer", background:n.read?"transparent":T.accentBg }}>
              <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, marginBottom:3 }}>
                <div style={{ width:24, height:24, borderRadius:"50%", background:mr.color+"22", border:`1px solid ${mr.color}44`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:mr.color, flexShrink:0 }}>{n.senderName?.[0]||"?"}</div>
                <div style={{ flex:1 }}><div style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.text }}><span style={{ color:mr.color, fontWeight:600 }}>{n.senderName}</span><span style={{ color:T.textSub }}> 在 </span><span style={{ color:T.text, fontWeight:600 }}>{n.roomName}</span></div><div style={{ fontSize:12, color:T.textSub, overflow:"hidden", textOverflow:"ellipsis", whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>{n.text}</div></div>
                {!n.read&&<div style={{ width:6, height:6, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.accent, flexShrink:0 }}/>}
              </div>
              <div style={{ fontSize:11, color:T.textMuted, paddingLeft:32 }}>{toROC(n.timestamp,true)}</div>
            </div>;})}
        </div>
      </div>}

      {/* Reset Modal */}
      {showReset&&<Modal title="重置系統資料" onClose={()=>setShowReset(false)} width={360}><div style={{ textAlign:"center", padding:"8px 0 16px" }}><div style={{ width:52, height:52, borderRadius:"50%", background:T.redBg, border:`2px solid ${T.red}44`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", margin:"0 auto 14px", color:T.red }}><Icon n="refresh" s={22}/></div><div style={{ color:T.text, fontSize:15, fontWeight:700, marginBottom:8 }}>確定要重置所有資料？</div><div style={{ color:T.textSub, fontSize:14, lineHeight:1.7, marginBottom:20 }}>這將恢復成系統預設狀態。<br/><span style={{ color:T.red, fontWeight:600 }}>此操作無法復原，請謹慎使用。</span></div><div style={{ display:"flex", gap:10 }}><button onClick={()=>setShowReset(false)} style={{ flex:1, background:T.bgMuted, color:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>取消</button><button onClick={handleReset} style={{ flex:1, background:T.red, color:"#fff", border:"none", borderRadius:8, padding:"10px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:600, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>確認重置</button></div></div></Modal>}

      {/* 身份視角切換提示橫幅 */}
      {isImpersonating && (
        <div style={{ background:T.amberBg, borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.amber}44`, padding:"7px 16px", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", gap:8 }}>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:7 }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize:14 }}>👁</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.amber, fontWeight:700 }}>正在以「{safeRole(viewAs).label}」視角瀏覽（預覽模式）</span>
          </div>
          <button onClick={()=>{ setViewAs(null); setTab("dashboard"); }}
            style={{ background:"none", border:`1px solid ${T.amber}66`, borderRadius:7, color:T.amber, fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, padding:"3px 10px", cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit", whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>
            ↩ 返回{safeRole(user.role).label}
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
      {/* Viewer Banner */}
      {!effectiveRole.canEdit&&<div style={{ background:T.bgMuted, borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, padding:"6px 16px", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8 }}><Icon n="lock" s={14}/><span style={{ fontSize:13, color:T.textSub }}>您目前為租客模式，僅能查看資料，無法編輯</span></div>}

      {/* Content */}
      <div style={{ padding:"16px 16px 200px", maxWidth:640, margin:"0 auto" }}>
        {active==="dashboard"&&<Dashboard data={data} currentUser={effectiveUser} onUpdate={updateData}/>}
        {active==="rooms"    &&<Rooms     data={data} currentUser={effectiveUser} onUpdate={updateData}/>}
        {active==="tenants"  &&<Tenants   data={data} currentUser={effectiveUser} onUpdate={updateData}/>}
        {active==="bills"    &&<Bills     data={data} currentUser={effectiveUser} onUpdate={updateData}/>}
        {active==="repairs"  &&<Repairs   data={data} currentUser={effectiveUser} onUpdate={updateData}/>}
        {active==="report"   &&<Report    bills={data.bills} rooms={data.rooms} tenants={data.tenants}/>}
        {active==="users"    &&<UserManagement data={data} currentUser={user} onUpdate={updateData}/>}
        {active==="log"      &&<ActivityLog    data={data} currentUser={user} onUpdate={updateData}/>}
      </div>

      {/* Action Bar */}
      {(role.canManageUsers||((effectiveRole.canViewFinance)&&active==="report"))&&<div style={{ position:"fixed", bottom:122, left:0, right:0, zIndex:199, padding:"0 16px 6px", display:"flex", gap:10, maxWidth:640, margin:"0 auto" }}>
        {active==="report"?null:role.canManageUsers?<button onClick={handleSaveBaseline} style={{ flex:1, background:T.bg, color:T.accent, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:10, padding:"10px 8px", fontSize:14, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", gap:5, fontFamily:"inherit" }}><Icon n="check" s={15}/> 修改並儲存</button>:null}
      </div>}

      {/* Bottom User Banner（下方橫幅：登入者身分 + 切換視角 + 重新整理 + 在線使用者） */}
      <div style={{ position:"fixed", bottom:60, left:0, right:0, background:T.bg, borderTop:`1px solid ${T.border}`, padding:"7px 14px", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", gap:8, zIndex:200 }}>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, minWidth:0, flex:1 }}>
          <AvatarBadge user={{...user,online:true}} size={28}/>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", lineHeight:1.2, minWidth:0 }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:T.text, whiteSpace:"nowrap", overflow:"hidden", textOverflow:"ellipsis" }}>{user.name}</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize:10, fontWeight:600, color:role.color }}>{role.label}</span>
          </div>
          {(data.users||[]).filter(u=>u.online&&u.id!==user.id).length>0&&<div style={{ display:"flex", marginLeft:4 }}>{(data.users||[]).filter(u=>u.online&&u.id!==user.id).slice(0,5).map(u=><AvatarBadge key={u.id} user={u} size={22}/>)}</div>}
        </div>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6, flexShrink:0 }}>
          {(switchOptions.length > 0 || isImpersonating) && (
            <div style={{ position:"relative" }}>
              <button onClick={()=>setShowViewAsPicker(v=>!v)}
                style={{ background:isImpersonating?T.amberBg:T.bgMuted, color:isImpersonating?T.amber:T.textSub, border:`1px solid ${isImpersonating?T.amber+"55":T.border}`, borderRadius:7, padding:"5px 10px", fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:"inherit", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:4 }}>
                <Icon n="users" s={13}/>
                {isImpersonating ? safeRole(viewAs).label : "切換視角"}
              </button>
              {showViewAsPicker && (
                <div style={{ position:"absolute", bottom:"calc(100% + 6px)", right:0, background:T.bg, border:`1px solid ${T.border}`, borderRadius:12, boxShadow:"0 -8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.13)", zIndex:500, minWidth:168, overflow:"hidden" }}>
                  {isImpersonating && (
                    <button onClick={()=>{ setViewAs(null); setShowViewAsPicker(false); setTab("dashboard"); }}
                      style={{ width:"100%", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, padding:"11px 14px", background:"none", border:"none", borderBottom:`1px solid ${T.border}`, cursor:"pointer", fontSize:13, fontWeight:700, color:safeRole(user.role).color, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                      ↩ 返回{safeRole(user.role).label}
                    </button>
                  )}
                  {switchOptions.filter(o=>o.role!==viewAs).map(o=>(
                    <button key={o.role} onClick={()=>{ setViewAs(o.role); setShowViewAsPicker(false); setTab(o.role==="viewer"?"rooms":"dashboard"); }}
                      style={{ width:"100%", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8, padding:"11px 14px", background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", fontSize:13, color:o.color, fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
                      👁 {o.label}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}
          {role.canManageUsers&&<button onClick={()=>setShowReset(true)} title="重置系統資料" style={{ background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", color:T.textSub, padding:4 }}><Icon n="refresh" s={17}/></button>}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Bottom Nav */}
      <div style={{ position:"fixed", bottom:0, left:0, right:0, background:T.bg, borderTop:`1px solid ${T.border}`, display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-around", padding:"8px 0 16px", zIndex:200 }}>
        {tabs.map(t=>(
          <button key={t.id} onClick={()=>setTab(t.id)} style={{ background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"center", gap:3, color:active===t.id?T.accent:T.textMuted, padding:"4px 6px", position:"relative", transition:"color 0.15s", fontFamily:"inherit" }}>
            <Icon n={t.icon} s={20}/>
            <span style={{ fontSize:11, fontWeight:active===t.id?700:500 }}>{t.label}</span>
            {t.badge>0&&<div style={{ position:"absolute", top:0, right:0, minWidth:16, height:16, background:T.red, color:"#fff", borderRadius:99, fontSize:10, fontWeight:700, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", padding:"0 4px" }}>{t.badge}</div>}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {toast&&<Toast msg={toast.msg} type={toast.type}/>}
    </div>
  );
}


ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById("root")).render(React.createElement(RentKeeperApp));

</script>
</body>
</html>
```
